[ASSUMPTION] The headline: **Aurora now records provider/rendering/delivery *occurrences* as append-only, ref-only `DomainEventRecord`s through an additive catalog expansion + pure factories — so the output-out edge is fully traceable — while `event-recording` stays dependency-neutral and the records stay inert: they reference artifacts by id only, persist nothing, call nothing, emit from nothing automatically, and never become evidence, quality judgments, retries, delivery commands, or domain mutations. Events record what happened; they do not make anything happen.**

---

## Update — Implementation 025 (Explicit Application Orchestration Boundary)

[FACT] **Implementation 025** added Aurora's **first application composition layer**: a new top-level module `src/modules/application-orchestration` whose one surface, **`orchestrateRenderDeliver(command, deps)`**, composes the **existing** public services of `rendering` / `delivery` / `event-recording` in a **fixed, explicit order** over **injected** collaborators. It is an **application-composition module, not a domain capability module**: it owns **no domain model, no repository, no persistence, no bounded context**. It coordinates boundaries; it does not dissolve them. It is **additive**: the only existing-file change is the documented AC20 `ALLOWED_MODULES` allowlist update for the new module — **no production behavior changed, no dependency changed, no documented blocker**.

[FACT] **Now true:**
- A new module `src/modules/application-orchestration/` exists with a single public function **`orchestrateRenderDeliver(command, deps): Promise<OrchestrationOutcome>`**, a **closed `OrchestrationOutcome`** (8 kinds: `delivered`/`delivery-failed`/`rendered`/`review-rejected`/`display-ineligible`/`provider-not-rendered`/`recording-failed`/`partial-success`), a **ref-only `OrchestrationTrace`** (safe ids + closed enums + safe codes only), a **closed `OrchestrationStage`** catalog (10 stages), and explicit **`ExplicitOrchestrationCommand`** / **`ExplicitOrchestrationDependencies`** types.
- **Every collaborator is injected** — provider client, non-secret config, secret ref, renderer/provider-adapter kinds, the rendered-message-record repository, and the *optional* provider-attempt repository, delivery sink, delivery-record repository, and event repository. Optional dependencies select optional steps (partial composition); no global service locator.
- **Each step is an explicit call**, in order: `requestRealProviderRendering(...)` → (if selected) `auditProviderAttempt(...)` + explicit `providerAttemptRepository.save(...)` → `RenderedMessageRecord.fromRenderedMessage(...)` + explicit `renderedMessageRecordRepository.save(...)` → (if selected) `renderReview(...)` + `record.appendReview(...)` + explicit save → `displayEligibilityOf(record)` (derived, never asserted) → (if selected **and** eligible) `deliveryRequest(...)` + `requestDelivery(...)` (self-persists) → (if selected) the Impl 024 occurrence-event factories + `eventRepository.append(...)`. **No event or repository write triggers the next step — this function's control flow does.**
- **The real-surface persistence asymmetry is respected** (verified against the code): `auditProviderAttempt(...)` and `RenderedMessageRecord.fromRenderedMessage(...)` **return** records that the orchestrator **persists explicitly**; a review is **appended to the rendered-message record** (`appendReview` returns a new record) and the orchestrator **saves explicitly** (there is no separate review repository); `requestDelivery(...)` **self-persists** through the injected delivery repository; the event repository uses **`append`**. Each persistence/action step is recorded as a safe ref/stage in the trace.
- **Failures are safe stops or a safe partial outcome, never an automatic retry.** A required-persistence failure (audit/record/review) is a safe `recording-failed` stop **before** delivery; a non-`rendered` provider outcome stops at `provider-not-rendered` with **no record/review/delivery**; review rejection / display-ineligibility stop **before** delivery (`review-rejected`/`display-ineligible`); a delivery failure returns `delivery-failed` and **does not retry**; an occurrence-event-append failure returns **`partial-success`** — **non-invalidating**, the completed domain steps stand and their refs remain in the trace.
- **The trace/result carry safe refs only.** No raw draft/prompt/payload/provider-response/secret/env value/message body is representable; a serialized-result/event scan proves no `bearer`/`authorization`/`apikey`/`secret`/`process.env`/message-body marker leaks; `displayEligibility` is a closed enum, `reasonCode` is always a closed code.
- **Dependency direction is clean.** `application-orchestration` imports **only the public indexes** of `rendering`/`delivery`/`event-recording` (+ `shared-kernel`); it depends on the `ProviderClientBoundary` **abstraction** through the rendering boundary; it imports **no** live HTTP transport, credential-resolver internals, process-env adapter, or concrete-provider internals, and **no upstream domain module** (`observation`/`reasoning`/`understanding`/`athlete`). **`rendering`/`delivery`/`event-recording` import no `application-orchestration`; no module depends on it for core behavior.**
- **AC20 was updated additively, not weakened.** The end-to-end guard's `ALLOWED_MODULES` set gained `application-orchestration` (Impl 016 `delivery` precedent) with a documenting comment that it is approved application composition, not a domain capability or a new bounded context; the guard still **rejects every other unapproved top-level module**.
- **Still absent (intentional):** an **event bus / publish-subscribe / handler**, a **queue / scheduler / retry / workflow engine**, **auto-emission** from any operation, **automatic delivery**, a **domain mutation** (it touches no `Athlete`/`Understanding`/`DecisionSupport`/`Observation`/`Hypothesis`), **telemetry / model evaluation**, a **production DB / schema / migration**, a **UI / API**, and any **live call / SDK / dependency** change (live calls remain disabled by default through the injected client).

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **application orchestration ≠ domain module** · **≠ bounded context** · **≠ workflow engine** · **≠ event bus** · **≠ scheduler** · **≠ retry engine** · **≠ persistence owner** · **≠ provider logic** · **≠ delivery logic** · **≠ event recording itself**.
- **explicit composition ≠ hidden side effect** · **injected collaborator ≠ global service locator** · **event-recording step ≠ event-triggered step** · **repository save ≠ implicit next step** · **display eligibility ≠ automatic delivery**.
- **provider success ≠ evidence** · **validation pass ≠ recommendation quality** · **delivery success ≠ athlete understanding** · **delivery success ≠ athlete decision** · **ref-only trace ≠ raw content storage** · **AC20 allowlist update ≠ guard weakening**.

[ASSUMPTION] The headline: **Aurora now has an explicit application orchestration boundary — `orchestrateRenderDeliver(command, deps)` composes the existing rendering, provider-attempt audit, rendered-message record/review/display, delivery, and event-recording services through injected collaborators in explicit ordered steps, returning a closed outcome + a ref-only trace — while owning no domain model/repository/persistence, introducing no event bus/scheduler/retry/workflow engine, never delivering automatically, never letting an event or save trigger the next step, never treating provider/delivery success as evidence or an athlete decision, and never mutating the domain. Composition is explicit; it is not a hidden side effect.**

---

## Update — Implementation 026 (Opt-In Live-Provider Smoke-Test Boundary)

[FACT] **Implementation 026** added Aurora's first **"real outside world" wiring check**: a **pure, fully-injected smoke-test boundary helper** inside `rendering/application` — `liveProviderSmoke(command, deps)` — that can exercise **one** live provider call through the **existing** rendering/provider seam (`requestRealProviderRendering(...) → the unchanged mandatory validateDraft`) **only** behind explicit, ordered, fail-closed gates, returning a **closed, redacted result**. It is **not an operator script and adds no npm script**; the default suite and CI make **no live call and need no credential**. It is **additive**: the only existing-file change is the `rendering/application/index.ts` exports — **no production behavior changed, no dependency changed, no new top-level module, no documented blocker**. **A smoke test proves wiring, not wisdom.**

[FACT] **Now true:**
- A new helper `src/modules/rendering/application/live-provider-smoke.ts` exposes **`liveProviderSmoke(command, deps): Promise<LiveProviderSmokeResult>`**, a **closed `LiveProviderSmokeStatus`** catalog (`not-enabled`/`ci-disabled`/`credential-missing`/`credential-invalid`/`live-policy-disabled`/`provider-failed`/`validation-failed`/`passed`/`unexpected-failure`) + `LIVE_PROVIDER_SMOKE_STATUSES`, and the **closed `LiveProviderSmokeCommand` / `LiveProviderSmokeDependencies` / `LiveProviderSmokeResult`** types. It is **application composition inside `rendering`**, not a new module.
- **Everything is injected** — the opt-in indicator, the CI indicator, the `ProviderCredentialResolver`, the `LiveCallPolicy`, the `ProviderClientBoundary` client, the non-secret `ProviderClientConfig`, and an optional ms clock. The helper **reads no `process.env`** (opt-in/CI are injected booleans; the credential arrives via the injected resolver).
- **Explicit fail-closed gates run in order — opt-in → CI → credential → live policy — and EACH stops before any provider call:** absent opt-in → `not-enabled`; CI indicator → `ci-disabled`; resolver `missing`/`invalid` → `credential-missing`/`credential-invalid`; disabled policy → `live-policy-disabled`. **The credential is resolved only after the opt-in and CI gates pass**; the provider call happens **only after** the credential is available **and** the policy is enabled.
- **At most one provider call — no loops, no re-issue.** The single call goes through the unchanged `requestRealProviderRendering` (so `validateDraft` stays the **only** path to a `RenderedMessage`): a rendered outcome → `passed` (`validationPassed: true`); a `provider-output-failed-validation` → `validation-failed`; any other `ProviderFailure` → `provider-failed` (carrying the closed `providerFailureCode`; timeout/malformed/unavailable are folded here, per the honest granularity of `ProviderRenderOutcome`); an unexpected throw → `unexpected-failure`.
- **The result is closed and redacted** (`rawRetained: false`): it carries safe codes only — **no rendered-message body, no raw draft/prompt/payload/response, no secret/credential token, no `process.env` value, no chain-of-thought, no metadata bag, no delivery target/body**.
- **Boundary-clean:** the helper imports **no** live HTTP transport, **no** process-environment adapter, **no** concrete-provider internals, **no** `delivery`/`event-recording`/`application-orchestration`, and **no** upstream-domain module; it carries **no** network/vendor/secret/retry token; **no module outside `rendering` imports it**. It composes the live client through the **injected** `ProviderClientBoundary` (the two existing credential gates — the `ProviderSecretRef.status` fast-path in the service and the resolver inside `LiveProviderClient` — remain backstops behind the helper's explicit early gate).
- **Side-effect-free:** the helper **persists nothing, delivers nothing, records no event, creates no rendered-message record / review / display eligibility / evidence / athlete decision, and mutates no domain state.** **Smoke success is wiring success, not evidence; smoke failure is not domain failure.**
- **Guards hold, nothing weakened:** the repo-wide **`process.env` one-file guard** stays green (the helper is not a new token site); the existing **live-provider guard** catches `live-provider-smoke.ts` (filename matches) and stays green (no network/vendor/env/retry token); **AC20 is untouched** (no new top-level module).
- **Still absent (intentional):** an **operator script / real env-flag reading** (deferred — Tech Spec 026A §14), an **npm script**, a **CI-live lane**, a **production secret manager / live-call rollout / real endpoint**, **finer provider-failure granularity** (timeout/malformed surfaced distinctly), an **application-orchestration end-to-end live smoke**, and any **event bus / queue / scheduler / retry / workflow / telemetry / model-evaluation / DB / SDK / dependency** change.

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **smoke boundary helper ≠ operator script** · **≠ npm script** · **≠ default live test** · **≠ CI live test** · **≠ production rollout** · **≠ model evaluation** · **≠ telemetry**.
- **smoke helper ≠ application-orchestration delivery path** · **≠ delivery** · **≠ event recording** · **≠ domain reasoning** · **smoke helper owns no repository / adds no persistence**.
- **smoke success ≠ product readiness** · **≠ evidence** · **≠ recommendation quality** · **≠ athlete decision** · **smoke failure ≠ domain failure**.
- **provider reachable ≠ provider output trusted** · **validation pass ≠ wisdom** · **injected opt-in/CI indicators ≠ env read** · **credential available ≠ automatic live call** · **live policy enabled for the helper ≠ global production live enablement** · **redacted smoke result ≠ raw provider transcript**.

[ASSUMPTION] The headline: **Aurora can now verify, manually and opt-in, that the live-provider path is wired correctly — one bounded call through the existing seam behind the unchanged validator — while the default suite stays deterministic, CI stays credential-free, the helper reads no environment and imports no transport/adapter/delivery/event/orchestration internal, the result stays redacted, and nothing is persisted, delivered, recorded, or mutated. A smoke test proves wiring, not wisdom; the operator entrypoint that reads real env flags remains future.**

## Update — Implementation 027 (Manual Operator Live-Smoke Entry Point)

[FACT] **Implementation 027** added the **operator entrypoint** that Impl 026 deferred: a **manual, executable `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs`** that reads the **real** opt-in / CI / endpoint flags and wires the **real** live-provider collaborators into the *existing* `liveProviderSmoke` helper — plus a **pure, typechecked `src` support helper** that holds the decidable/redaction logic. `[FACT]` 027A's empirical correction held: **Node 22.22 native type-stripping makes a `.mjs` import the real `.ts` `src` modules with no build and no dependency** (verified), so the executable entrypoint shipped now rather than being deferred to a build-output slice. It is **additive**: the only existing-file changes are the `rendering/application/index.ts` exports and the **reconciled (strengthened, not weakened) Impl 026 `scripts/` guard**; **no production behavior changed, no dependency changed, no `package.json`/lockfile change, no documented blocker**. **A smoke test proves wiring, not wisdom.**

[FACT] **Now true:**
- A new **manual operator surface OUTSIDE `src`** — `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs` (plain ESM) — runs via **`node scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs`**. It is **not an npm script**, **not part of `npm run check`**, **not in the default test glob** (`src/**/*.test.ts`), and **outside both guard scan roots** (the process-env one-file guard scans `src`; the live-provider guard scans `src/modules/rendering`).
- A new **pure, typechecked `src` support helper** — `src/modules/rendering/application/operator-live-smoke-entrypoint.ts` — exposes `parseOperatorSmokeEnv` (injected env record → `{ optIn, ci }`), `syntheticSmokeRenderingRequest()`, `operatorSmokeOutput(result)` (redacted projection), `operatorSmokeExitCode(status)`, and the flag-name constants (`OPERATOR_SMOKE_OPT_IN_KEY = "AURORA_LIVE_PROVIDER_SMOKE"`, value `"1"`; `OPERATOR_SMOKE_CI_KEY`; `OPERATOR_SMOKE_ENDPOINT_KEY`). It **reads no `process.env`** (the env is an injected record), calls no provider, imports no live transport / process-env adapter / concrete-provider internals / `delivery` / `event-recording` / `application-orchestration`, and has **no side effects**.
- **The script reads narrowly-scoped operator flags outside `src`** (opt-in / CI / endpoint) — legitimate there, since no in-`src` token is added and **the production `process.env` one-file seal is untouched** (the credential is read **only** through the approved `ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter` → `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver` chain). It does **not** dump the environment.
- **The script wires the existing public rendering surfaces** (`LiveCallPolicy.enabled` + `LiveProviderClient` + `liveProviderHttpTransport` + the credential chain + the unchanged serializer/parser/error-mapper inside the client) and **calls `liveProviderSmoke` once** — it **duplicates no smoke semantics** and **bypasses neither `liveProviderSmoke` nor `requestRealProviderRendering` nor `validateDraft`**. The helper still owns the **opt-in → CI → credential → live-policy** gates (each before any provider call), the **one bounded call**, and the **redaction**.
- **The script prints one redacted JSON object** (`status` + `rawRetained: false` + `wiringOnly` + `sideEffects: "none"` + safe optional fields) — **no rendered-message body, no raw draft/prompt/payload/response, no secret/credential token, no `process.env` value, no metadata bag** — and **exits 0** for `passed`/`not-enabled`/`ci-disabled`, **1** for operational failures. Verified end-to-end: `not-enabled`/`ci-disabled` (exit 0, no live call) and `credential-missing` (exit 1, no transport).
- **No side effects:** the entrypoint **persists nothing, delivers nothing, records no event, calls no `application-orchestration` delivery path, creates no evidence / athlete decision, and mutates no domain state.**
- **Guard reconciliation (strengthened, not weakened):** the Impl 026 "no `scripts/` yet" guard (operator entrypoint deferred) was reconciled to the post-027 invariant — **`scripts/` may exist only for the approved `operator-live-smoke.mjs`** (no other unapproved script; `package.json` wires no npm script to it; no operator script dir inside `src`; the smoke HELPER stays pure and in `src`). The script's internal boundary (no delivery/event/orchestration imports, redacted output, no retry/loop) is asserted by the new Impl 027 negative-capability test.
- **Still absent (intentional):** a **production secret manager / secret rotation**, a **CI-live lane**, a **production live-call rollout / real endpoint**, an **`application-orchestration` end-to-end live smoke**, and any **npm script / package-lock change / SDK / dependency / event bus / queue / scheduler / retry / workflow / telemetry / model-evaluation / DB / schema**.

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **operator entrypoint ≠ smoke helper** · **≠ smoke semantics** · **≠ npm script** · **≠ default test** · **≠ CI live lane** · **≠ production rollout** · **≠ production secret manager** · **≠ telemetry / model evaluation**.
- **operator entrypoint ≠ delivery** · **≠ event recording** · **≠ application orchestration** · **operator entrypoint success ≠ product readiness** · **smoke success ≠ evidence / athlete decision** · **smoke failure ≠ domain failure**.

The operator can now run the wire; the wire still proves wiring, not wisdom.**

## Update — Implementation 028 (Provider-Neutral Managed-Secret Credential-Source Boundary)

[FACT] **Implementation 028** added Aurora's first **provider-neutral managed-secret credential-source boundary** inside `rendering/application` — a pure TypeScript async interface (`ManagedSecretStoreClient`) behind which any managed secret store (cloud or otherwise) can supply a credential, and a `ManagedSecretCredentialSource` class that **pre-fetches** the secret and produces the `EnvironmentCredentialSource` map consumed by the **existing, unchanged synchronous `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver`**. No cloud SDK, no `process.env` read, no dependency change, no new module, no live-call enablement. It is **additive**: the only existing-file change is the `rendering/application/index.ts` exports; the downstream synchronous chain is unchanged. **`ManagedSecretCredentialSource` ≠ cloud adapter ≠ production rollout ≠ live-call enablement ≠ provider trust ≠ domain evidence. secret manager = credential source.**

[FACT] **Now true:**
- A new interface **`ManagedSecretStoreClient`** (`retrieve(secretName): Promise<ManagedSecretResolution>`) is the **pure TypeScript async boundary** for any managed-secret store — always resolves (never rejects; implementations must catch all exceptions internally); no cloud SDK, no vendor dependency, no network token; **injected in all usage**.
- A new type **`ManagedSecretResolution`** is a **4-state discriminated union**: `{ status: "available"; value: string }` / `{ status: "missing" }` / `{ status: "invalid" }` / `{ status: "unavailable" }` — closed; the `available` value is placed in the source map and never exposed raw to callers outside this boundary.
- A new class **`ManagedSecretCredentialSource`** wraps the interface: **`async toEnvironmentCredentialSource(): Promise<EnvironmentCredentialSource>`** pre-fetches the secret and produces the `EnvironmentCredentialSource` map (`{ [secretName]: value }` on `available`; `{}` on `missing`/`invalid`/`unavailable`). An empty source causes the existing resolver to classify the credential as `missing` — **no provider call occurs**.
- **Pre-fetch pattern**: `await managedSecretSource.toEnvironmentCredentialSource()` is called **before** constructing `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver`. The downstream **synchronous chain is entirely unchanged**; resolver/live-client/gate/validator/audit/orchestration code is untouched.
- A **deterministic `FakeManagedSecretStoreClient`** covers all 4 `ManagedSecretClientScenario` values (`available`/`missing`/`invalid`/`unavailable`); `available` returns the sentinel `"opaque:test-managed-secret"` (not a real credential — same pattern as `StaticProviderCredentialResolver`'s `"opaque:test-credential"`). **No real secret, no real network, no SDK; constructed explicitly, never a global singleton.**
- **+39 tests** across two new test files: functional tests (source-map shape across 4 scenarios, resolver integration, live-call gate — availability ≠ enablement, redaction proof, smoke integration, always-resolves contract) and negative-capability tests (no `process.env` in new file; process-env seal intact — still exactly one approved adapter file; no vendor/SDK/network/retry token; no forbidden import; no module outside `rendering` imports the new symbols; no forbidden directory created; no SDK/dependency change; operator script unchanged and not referencing `ManagedSecretCredentialSource`).
- **710/710 tests pass; `tsc --noEmit` clean.** The process-env one-file seal remains intact; the live-provider and `provider-credential` guards stay green; AC20 is untouched; `package.json`/lockfile unchanged; operator script unchanged.
- **Still absent (intentional):** a **cloud adapter** (AWS Secrets Manager / GCP Secret Manager / Azure Key Vault / HashiCorp Vault client) implementing `ManagedSecretStoreClient`; a **production secret rotation** strategy; a **CI-live lane** or **production live-call rollout**; any **event-bus / scheduler / retry / workflow / telemetry / DB / dependency change**.

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **managed-secret seam ≠ cloud adapter** · **≠ production secret store** · **≠ production rollout** · **≠ live-call enablement** · **≠ provider trust** · **≠ domain evidence** · **≠ `LiveCallPolicy` approval**.
- **pre-fetch pattern ≠ async resolver** · **pre-fetched source ≠ real-time secret** · **`toEnvironmentCredentialSource()` ≠ rotation-aware retrieval** · **`EnvironmentCredentialSource` map ≠ live store call**.
- **`FakeManagedSecretStoreClient` ≠ real secret manager** · **sentinel `"opaque:test-managed-secret"` ≠ production credential** · **`available` scenario ≠ real secret in tests**.
- **`ManagedSecretCredentialSource` ≠ `ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter`** · **managed-secret source ≠ process-env read** · **injected async store client ≠ `process.env` access** · **process-env seal intact**.
- **credential availability ≠ live-call enablement** · **`missing`/`invalid`/`unavailable` → empty source → resolver classifies as `missing` → no provider call** · **safe ref ≠ secret value**.
- **`ManagedSecretStoreClient` ≠ SDK boundary** · **≠ cloud-provider import** · **≠ network token** · **≠ retry engine** · **≠ scheduler**.

[ASSUMPTION] The headline: **Aurora now has a provider-neutral async managed-secret credential-source seam — `ManagedSecretStoreClient` / `ManagedSecretCredentialSource` — that pre-fetches a secret into the existing `EnvironmentCredentialSource` map consumed by the unchanged synchronous `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver`, keeping the downstream chain synchronous and untouched while making any cloud or managed store pluggable behind a pure TypeScript interface. No cloud SDK, no `process.env` read, no dependency, no live-call enablement — the seam exists; cloud adapters and production wiring are a later slice.**

---

## Update — Implementation 029 (Cloud-Specific Secret Adapter Contract)

[FACT] **Implementation 029** added Aurora's first **cloud-secret adapter contract** inside `rendering/application`, living **BEHIND the Impl 028 provider-neutral managed-secret seam** — a **`CloudSecretStoreAdapter` that `implements ManagedSecretStoreClient`** and drives an **injected `CloudSecretValueClient`** (a cloud-like transport boundary, distinct from `ManagedSecretStoreClient`; it MAY throw — the adapter catches). It maps a richer cloud-like outcome union (`CloudSecretLookupResult`) into the existing 4-state `ManagedSecretResolution` and **fails closed**. No real cloud SDK, no provider selection (no AWS/GCP/Azure), no `process.env` read, no dependency change, no new module, no live-call enablement. It is **additive**: the only existing-file change is the `rendering/application/index.ts` exports; the downstream synchronous chain — and the Impl 028 seam itself — is unchanged. **`CloudSecretStoreAdapter` ≠ AWS/GCP/Azure adapter ≠ selected provider ≠ SDK integration ≠ production rollout ≠ live-call enablement. cloud-like adapter contract = a `ManagedSecretStoreClient` implementation, nothing more.**

[FACT] **Now true:**
- A new class **`CloudSecretStoreAdapter`** **`implements ManagedSecretStoreClient`** — its `retrieve(secretName): Promise<ManagedSecretResolution>` **always resolves, never rejects** (it catches every exception from the injected client internally), so it slots behind the Impl 028 seam with the downstream synchronous chain entirely unchanged.
- A new interface **`CloudSecretValueClient`** is the **injected cloud-like transport boundary** — **distinct from `ManagedSecretStoreClient`** (it returns the richer `CloudSecretLookupResult` and **MAY throw**; the adapter, not the client, is responsible for catching and failing closed). No cloud SDK, no vendor dependency, no network token; injected in all usage.
- A new type **`CloudSecretLookupResult`** is the **richer cloud-like outcome union** (found-with-value / blank-or-control found value / malformed / not_found / empty-ref / denied / unauthenticated / unavailable / timeout / throttled); **`CloudSecretAdapterFailureCode`** is a **closed, redacted classification** of safe failure codes (no raw cloud response, no secret value).
- A **deterministic `FakeCloudSecretValueClient`** drives the adapter across every scenario **including "throws"**; on a value-bearing success it returns the sentinel **`"opaque:test-cloud-secret"`** (not a real credential — same pattern as `FakeManagedSecretStoreClient`'s `"opaque:test-managed-secret"`). **No real secret, no real SDK, no network; constructed explicitly, never a global singleton.**
- **The mapping into the existing 4-state `ManagedSecretResolution` is exactly:** `found` (valid value) → **available** · `blank`/control found value → **invalid** · `malformed` → **invalid** · `not_found` / empty ref → **missing** · `denied` / `unauthenticated` / `unavailable` / `timeout` / `throttled` / **thrown exception** → **unavailable**. **`retrieve()` always resolves, never rejects** — every cloud-like failure folds to a non-`available` state → an empty source → the resolver classifies the credential as `missing` → **no provider call**.
- **It redacts raw secret values AND raw cloud responses** — proven by negative tests with the markers `sk-test-cloud-secret-do-not-leak`, `raw-cloud-response-do-not-leak`, and `cloud-access-token-do-not-leak`: none appear in the resolution, the failure code, the source map, or anywhere observable.
- **+38 tests** across new functional and negative-capability test files: functional tests (the full outcome→4-state mapping incl. the throw path, always-resolves contract, sentinel-only success, resolver integration — availability ≠ enablement) and negative-capability tests (no real secret value or raw cloud response leaks; no `process.env` in the new file; process-env one-file seal intact; no vendor/SDK/network token; no provider selection; no forbidden import; no module outside `rendering` imports the new symbols; no SDK/dependency change; operator script unchanged).
- **710/710 tests pass; `tsc --noEmit` clean.** The process-env one-file seal remains intact; the live-provider and `provider-credential` guards stay green; AC20 is untouched; `package.json`/lockfile unchanged; operator script unchanged.
- **It does NOT:** select a concrete cloud provider (no AWS / GCP / Azure); add an SDK / dependency / lockfile change; make a real cloud or network call; read `process.env`; add a production `process.env` token; change `ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter` / `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver` / `ManagedSecretCredentialSource` semantics; change the operator smoke or wire the cloud adapter into the operator smoke by default; introduce source precedence; enable live calls; bypass `LiveCallPolicy` / operator opt-in / the CI guard / `validateDraft`; create delivery / events / orchestration / evidence / athlete decisions / domain mutation; or add telemetry / model evaluation / DB / schema / retry / scheduler / queue / event bus. The `package.json`/lockfile is unchanged, the operator script is unchanged, and the process-env one-file seal is intact.
- **Still absent (intentional):** a **concrete cloud provider selection** (a real AWS Secrets Manager / GCP Secret Manager / Azure Key Vault SDK adapter); **production secret wiring**; **source precedence**; **rotation / cache / TTL**; a **CI-live lane** or **production live-call rollout**; any **event-bus / scheduler / retry / workflow / telemetry / DB / dependency change**.

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **`CloudSecretValueClient` ≠ `ManagedSecretStoreClient`**
- **`CloudSecretStoreAdapter` ≠ AWS/GCP/Azure adapter**
- **cloud-like adapter contract ≠ selected provider ≠ SDK integration ≠ production rollout ≠ live-call enablement**
- **credential available ≠ `LiveCallPolicy` approval ≠ operator opt-in ≠ CI live lane ≠ provider trust ≠ evidence ≠ athlete decision**
- **safe cloud failure code ≠ raw cloud response**
- **secret ref ≠ secret value**
- **redacted output ≠ secret payload**

[ASSUMPTION] The headline: **Aurora now has a cloud-secret adapter *contract* — `CloudSecretStoreAdapter implements ManagedSecretStoreClient`, driving an injected `CloudSecretValueClient` (the cloud-like transport boundary that MAY throw) — that maps a richer cloud-like outcome union (`CloudSecretLookupResult`, classified by the closed `CloudSecretAdapterFailureCode`) into the existing 4-state `ManagedSecretResolution`, fails closed, always resolves (never rejects), and redacts raw secret values AND raw cloud responses. It lives BEHIND the Impl 028 managed-secret seam without changing it. No concrete cloud provider, no real SDK, no `process.env` read, no production wiring, no source precedence, no rotation/cache/TTL, no CI-live lane, no live-call enablement — the cloud adapter *contract* exists; a real provider-specific SDK adapter and production wiring are a later slice.**

## Update — Implementation 032R-A (Operator-Mediated Offline Reflection Runtime)

[FACT] **Implementation 032R-A** is complete; validation is now **737/737** (+27 tests). It adds **Aurora's FIRST product-runtime code slice** — a single **PURE application-level function `offlineReflectionRuntime(command, deps)`** inside the `application-orchestration` application layer. The runtime is **operator-mediated offline/manual reflection**: an operator submits manual input on the athlete's behalf, the runtime projects a **safe athlete-facing reflection**, **withholds delivery**, and returns a **decision-capture prompt/ref** — it creates **no `AthleteDecision`**. It is **NOT executable infrastructure**: not an executable script, not a package command, not a CLI, not an API/server/UI/worker, not a deployment target, not a production rollout, and **not an operator smoke** (operator-mediated runtime ≠ operator smoke). **Aurora advises; the athlete decides.**

[FACT] **Now true:**
- A pure function **`offlineReflectionRuntime(command, deps)`** lives in `application-orchestration/application/` — a **product-runtime application service**, NOT an executable runtime shell. It is invoked in-process with injected collaborators; it installs **no** technology (no DB/auth/package/deployment/CI/runtime-shell), opens no network, reads no `process.env`, and adds no dependency.
- It **wires the injected manual-intake collaborator (`deps.runManualIntake`)** to record the operator-submitted manual input, then composes the **render-only `orchestrateRenderDeliver`** to express the result. **`validateDraft` remains mandatory** through the existing path — the runtime invents no new render/validation path.
- It projects a **safe athlete-facing reflection** and **withholds delivery** (`deliveryWithheld: true`); it returns a **decision-capture prompt/ref** and **creates NO `AthleteDecision`**. Operator mediation is treated as **mediation, not an athlete decision**; the **athlete remains the sole decision owner**.
- **Inference is marked as inference, not fact;** provider output is **not returned raw**; **no hidden reasoning is returned**; **no live provider by default**; **no real secret required**; it **records no events implicitly**.
- The result is a **closed status union**: `reflection-ready` / `input-rejected` / `not-rendered` / `recording-failed` / `unexpected-failure`.

[FACT] **The TRUE BLOCKER and its resolution** (documented so it is not re-collapsed):
- **Blocker:** the **Impl 025 negative-capability guard** forbids `application-orchestration` production files from importing **upstream domain modules** (including `observation`). The original plan to import `ingestManualInput` **directly** into the production file would have **broken the guard**.
- **Resolution:** the manual-intake step is **INJECTED** (`deps.runManualIntake`), the **command is GENERIC over the submission type**, the **production file imports NO `observation` module**, and the **TESTS wire the real `ingestManualInput`**. **No guard was weakened.** The runtime composes manual intake through the injected seam exactly as Impl 025 composes rendering/delivery through injected collaborators.

[FACT] **Second note (display-eligibility vs. delivery):** a successful render **with no review** may stop at orchestration **"display-ineligible"** — because display eligibility gates **DELIVERY**, which is **withheld** here. Therefore **`reflection-ready` is keyed off the RENDERED record itself**, **not** delivery or display-eligibility. A withheld delivery is **not a delivery failure** (delivery withheld ≠ delivery failure), and a rendered record is **not** an athlete decision (rendered record ≠ athlete decision).

[FACT] **What this slice does NOT do (still FUTURE):** the missing **`ObservationSet → reasoning → understanding → decision-support → RenderableDomainOutput` composition remains future work.** The **renderable / `RenderingRequest` is supplied IN THE COMMAND** — the slice **does not invent the pipeline** (renderable injected ≠ inferred pipeline result; manual intake ≠ full reasoning pipeline). No API/UI/worker, no deployment, no production rollout, and no real reasoning pipeline exist.

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **operator-mediated runtime ≠ operator smoke** · **operator mediation ≠ athlete decision** · **offline runtime ≠ deployment target ≠ production rollout** · **runtime function ≠ CLI/package command** · **application service composition ≠ executable runtime shell**.
- **reflection-ready ≠ delivered** · **delivery withheld ≠ delivery failure** · **delivery success ≠ athlete decision** · **decision-capture prompt ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **rendered record ≠ athlete decision**.
- **validated draft ≠ recommendation quality** · **provider output ≠ truth** · **manual intake ≠ full reasoning pipeline** · **renderable injected ≠ inferred pipeline result** · **reflection ≠ prescription**.
- **Aurora advises, the athlete decides** · **Aurora never presents inference as fact.**

[ASSUMPTION] The headline: **Aurora now has its FIRST product-runtime code slice — a pure application-level `offlineReflectionRuntime(command, deps)` in `application-orchestration` that wires the injected manual-intake collaborator (`deps.runManualIntake`) + the render-only `orchestrateRenderDeliver` (with `validateDraft` still mandatory) to project a safe athlete-facing reflection, withhold delivery (`deliveryWithheld: true`), and return a decision-capture prompt while creating no `AthleteDecision`. It is operator-mediated offline/manual reflection ONLY — not a script/package command/CLI/API/server/UI/worker/deployment/production rollout/operator smoke; the Impl 025 negative-capability guard held because manual intake is injected and the production file imports no `observation` module; `reflection-ready` is keyed off the rendered record, not delivery/display-eligibility; the `ObservationSet → … → RenderableDomainOutput` reasoning composition remains future (the renderable is supplied in the command). +27 tests; 737/737 pass.**

---

## Update — Implementation 035-A / 035-B (External Renderable Admission Check, Tier 2 wired)

[FACT] **Implementation 035-A** and **035-B** are complete; validation is now **779/779** (+32 tests for Impl 035-A, +10 tests for Impl 035-B). Together they add — and then **WIRE** — a **PURE Tier 2 external-renderable admission check** in the `application-orchestration` application layer, so the external renderable contract is now **ENFORCED before rendering**, not merely contractual. **035-A** added the pure check; **035-B** wired it into `offlineReflectionRuntime` so a renderable that is not structurally admissible **fails closed BEFORE any provider rendering**. **Aurora advises; the athlete decides** — and now Aurora refuses to render a renderable that does not pass the structural admission gate.

[FACT] **Now true (Impl 035-A — the PURE check):**
- A pure, synchronous, structural function **`admitExternalRenderable(request: RenderingRequest): ExternalRenderableAdmission`** lives in `application-orchestration/application/external-renderable-admission.ts`. It is a **Tier 2** admission check: it verifies **STRUCTURAL safety only** and returns a closed `ExternalRenderableAdmission` outcome (admitted / inadmissible with a safe closed `ExternalRenderableRejectionReason`).
- It composes **no** technology: it reads no `process.env`, opens no network, calls no provider/`validateDraft`/renderer/delivery sink, persists nothing, mutates nothing, and adds no dependency. It is a pure value-in / value-out structural predicate.
- **What it verifies (structural only):** **provenance** (a `sourceCaseRef` is present); a **supported kind**; **claim fields** (a support renderable must carry **≥ 1 `allowedClaim`**); **`agencyRequired`**; **`uncertaintyVisibleRequired`**; **traceability where required**; and the **voice ceiling for support** — it **rejects `Recommendation` / `Silence` / an absent voice** for a support renderable.
- **Documented limitation:** an **empty `forbiddenClaims` is admissible** — Tier 2 cannot prove a claim set is exhaustive; it only checks structural presence/shape, not semantic completeness.

[FACT] **Now true (Impl 035-B — the check WIRED):**
- `offlineReflectionRuntime` now invokes `admitExternalRenderable` **AFTER manual intake** (`deps.runManualIntake`) and **BEFORE render-only orchestration** (`orchestrateRenderDeliver`). The external renderable contract is therefore **ENFORCED before rendering** rather than relying on the caller's contractual guarantee alone.
- A new **ADDITIVE closed runtime status `renderable-inadmissible`** is added to the runtime's closed status union (alongside `reflection-ready`/`input-rejected`/`not-rendered`/`recording-failed`/`unexpected-failure`). The inadmissible outcome carries an optional **`admissionReason?: ExternalRenderableRejectionReason`** (a safe closed code — never a raw payload), **`deliveryWithheld: true`**, **`trace.stoppedAt: "stopped"`**, and **no reflection**.
- A **rejected renderable fails closed BEFORE provider rendering**: orchestration **never starts**, so the runtime **does NOT call `validateDraft`**, **does NOT call delivery**, and **does NOT create an `AthleteDecision`**; **`deliveryWithheld` stays `true`**.
- An **ADMITTED renderable still goes through the downstream mandatory `validateDraft`** on the existing render-only path — admission is a *precondition*, never a *replacement*, for validation.

[FACT] **The three-tier contract is now enforced (not merely contractual):**
- **Tier 1 — caller contractual guarantees** (the caller promises the renderable is well-formed and truthful; a guarantee, not a machine proof).
- **Tier 2 — `admitExternalRenderable` (WIRED, structural)** — the runtime now *enforces* the structural contract before rendering; it can disprove structural safety but cannot prove Tier 1.
- **Tier 3 — the downstream mandatory `validateDraft`** — still the only path to a `RenderedMessage`; unchanged and still mandatory for admitted renderables.

[FACT] **What `admitted` is NOT (do not collapse):** **admitted ≠ true ≠ evidence-backed fact ≠ recommendation quality ≠ wisdom.** A Tier 2 structural pass cannot prove a Tier 1 caller guarantee — **Tier 2 cannot prove Tier 1.**

[FACT] **What remains UNCHANGED / still absent (intentional):**
- **AC20 remains UNCHANGED** (no new top-level module; the admission check lives inside the already-approved `application-orchestration`). **Spec 034 Option C remains superseded; Tech Spec 034A remains on hold/superseded.**
- **No production whole-core composer exists; no reflection-composition module exists; whole-core composition remains a TEST HARNESS.** `offlineReflectionRuntime` keeps its **injected-renderable seam** (the renderable is still supplied in the command) — now **GUARDED by admission**.
- **No package/dependency/runtime/API/UI/CLI/worker/deployment/CI change.**

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **external renderable ≠ truth** · **caller guarantee ≠ machine proof** · **admitted ≠ evidence-backed fact** · **admitted ≠ recommendation quality**.
- **admission check ≠ `validateDraft`** · **`validateDraft` ≠ recommendation quality** · **`RenderingRequest` ≠ provider call**.
- **`renderable-inadmissible` ≠ delivery failure** · **delivery withheld ≠ delivery failure** · **validated reflection ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **operator mediation ≠ athlete decision** · **AC20 seam ≠ whole-core composer**.

[ASSUMPTION] The headline: **Aurora now ENFORCES its external renderable contract before rendering. Impl 035-A added a pure, synchronous, structural Tier 2 admission check — `admitExternalRenderable(request: RenderingRequest): ExternalRenderableAdmission` in `application-orchestration/application` — that verifies provenance (`sourceCaseRef`), supported kind, claim fields (support needs ≥ 1 `allowedClaim`), `agencyRequired`, `uncertaintyVisibleRequired`, traceability where required, and the support voice ceiling (rejecting Recommendation/Silence/absent), with the documented limitation that an empty `forbiddenClaims` is admissible. Impl 035-B WIRED it into `offlineReflectionRuntime` — running after manual intake and before render-only orchestration — adding the additive closed status `renderable-inadmissible` (optional safe `admissionReason`, `deliveryWithheld: true`, `trace.stoppedAt: "stopped"`, no reflection); a rejected renderable fails closed before provider rendering and never calls `validateDraft`/delivery or creates an `AthleteDecision`, while an admitted renderable still goes through the mandatory `validateDraft`. The three-tier contract is now enforced (Tier 1 caller guarantee / Tier 2 wired structural admission / Tier 3 downstream `validateDraft`), but admitted ≠ true ≠ evidence-backed fact ≠ recommendation quality ≠ wisdom — Tier 2 cannot prove Tier 1. AC20 is unchanged; Spec 034 Option C remains superseded; Tech Spec 034A remains on hold/superseded; no production whole-core composer and no reflection-composition module exist; whole-core composition remains a TEST HARNESS; the injected-renderable seam stays, now guarded by admission. No package/dependency/runtime/API/UI/CLI/worker/deployment/CI change. +32 tests for Impl 035-A, +10 for Impl 035-B; 779/779 pass.**

## Update — Implementation 036-A (First Operator-Mediated Reflection Session, test-only)

[FACT] **Implementation 036-A** is complete; validation is now **784/784** (+5 tests). It adds **Aurora's FIRST operator-mediated reflection session** as a **TEST-ONLY whole-core responsible-reflection harness** — a **single new file under `src/modules/__tests__/`** (`first-operator-mediated-reflection-session.test.ts`). It adds **NO production code, NO runtime shell, NO CLI/script/package command, and NO API/UI/worker/deployment/CI/SDK files.** Composing the whole core in `__tests__/` is **AC20-permitted**; **no production whole-core composer and no reflection-composition module are created.** **Aurora advises; the athlete decides** — and this session proves the loop end-to-end without ever delivering or deciding.

[FACT] **What this proves (the real athlete-input-to-reflection loop, end-to-end):**
- A test-only harness wires the **real responsible-reflection chain** in order: **athlete manual input → whole-core responsible-reflection harness (test-only)** → a **real `TerminalOutput`** → **`renderableFromTerminalOutput`** → a **`RenderingRequest`** → **`offlineReflectionRuntime`** → **`admitExternalRenderable` (Tier 2 admission)** → **render-only orchestration** → the **downstream mandatory `validateDraft`** → **reflection-ready** → **delivery withheld** → **no `AthleteDecision`**.
- The renderable is now produced from a **real `TerminalOutput`** (via `renderableFromTerminalOutput`) inside the test harness, then carried through the existing injected-renderable seam — the harness still does **not** introduce a production pipeline composer; it composes the real chain in `__tests__/` only.

[FACT] **Cases proven (5 tests):**
- **safe input → `reflection-ready`** (the full chain completes through the mandatory `validateDraft`, delivery withheld, no `AthleteDecision`).
- **inadmissible renderable → `renderable-inadmissible`** (Tier 2 admission fails closed before render-only orchestration).
- **admitted-but-invalid draft → `not-rendered`** (fail-closed at the downstream `validateDraft`; admission is a precondition, never a replacement, for validation).
- **invalid manual input → `input-rejected`** (the manual-intake step rejects the unrepresentable before anything downstream runs).
- **cross-path invariant:** on **every** path the session **never delivers** and **never creates an `AthleteDecision`**.

[FACT] **What never happens on any path (the withholding invariants):**
- **Delivery is withheld on every path; no delivery sink is invoked.** **No `AthleteDecision` is created.** A **decision-capture prompt/ref ≠ `AthleteDecision`**; **operator mediation ≠ athlete decision**; **reflection-ready ≠ delivered**; **a validated reflection ≠ `AthleteDecision`**. The **athlete remains the future decision owner.**
- **No live provider / no real secret; no `process.env` read.** The harness uses the existing deterministic/injected collaborators only.

[FACT] **What remains UNCHANGED / still absent (intentional):**
- **AC20 is preserved (all AC20 guards green).** Whole-core composition **remains a TEST HARNESS**; **no production whole-core composer** and **no reflection-composition module** exist. The `offlineReflectionRuntime` injected-renderable seam stays — now exercised end-to-end through a real `TerminalOutput` **in the test harness**, still guarded by the Tier 2 admission check.
- **No production code, runtime shell, CLI/script/package command, API/UI/worker, deployment, CI, or SDK file** was added. **Spec 034 Option C remains superseded; Tech Spec 034A remains on hold/superseded.**

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **test-only harness ≠ production composer** · **whole-core composition in `__tests__/` ≠ a reflection-composition module** · **operator-mediated session (test proof) ≠ deployment target ≠ production rollout** · **proof of the loop ≠ a runtime shell / CLI / package command**.
- **reflection-ready ≠ delivered** · **delivery withheld ≠ delivery failure** · **decision-capture prompt/ref ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **operator mediation ≠ athlete decision** · **validated reflection ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **admitted ≠ true ≠ recommendation quality** (Tier 2 cannot prove Tier 1).
- **Aurora advises, the athlete decides** · **Aurora never presents inference as fact.**

[ASSUMPTION] The headline: **Aurora now has its FIRST operator-mediated reflection session, proven end-to-end as a TEST-ONLY whole-core responsible-reflection harness (one new `src/modules/__tests__/` file, +5 tests, 784/784 pass). ## Update — Implementation 037-A (Post-Reflection Athlete Decision Capture, test-only)

[FACT] **Implementation 037-A** is complete; validation is now **795/795** (+11 tests). It adds the **post-reflection athlete decision capture proof** as a **TEST-ONLY harness** — a **single new file under `src/modules/__tests__/`** (`post-reflection-athlete-decision-capture.test.ts`). Per Spec 037 / Tech Spec 037A Decision 1 (Option A + C) it is **documented usage of the EXISTING decision machinery (Impl 009)** and adds **NO production code, NO runtime integration, NO production decision-capture wrapper, NO runtime shell, NO CLI/script/package command, and NO API/UI/worker/deployment/CI/SDK files.** **AC20 is preserved**; **`offlineReflectionRuntime` remains unchanged**; the **session reflection loop remains separate from decision capture.** **Aurora advises; the athlete decides.**

[FACT] **What this proves (the post-reflection capture loop, by documented usage):**
- The capture path is an **explicit, separate athlete step**: **reflection-ready session context → decision-capture invitation/ref → explicit `athlete-declared` or `athlete-reported` input → `athleteDecision(...)` → `decisionContext({ decisionSupportCaseRef: sourceCaseRef })` → `recordAthleteDecision(...)` → `SubjectiveObservation` feedback output only.**
- Captured decisions **link back to the reflection/session context** via the **existing** `decisionContext({ decisionSupportCaseRef: sourceCaseRef })` (the reflection's `sourceCaseRef` is a decision-support case ref).
- The decision **re-enters only as a `SubjectiveObservation`** (`decisionAsObservation`); **no `Signal` or `Evidence` is created directly**, and **no reasoning/understanding update is triggered directly.**

[FACT] **No-auto-creation invariants proven (the withholding separations):**
- **`reflection-ready` alone creates no `AthleteDecision`.** **`validateDraft` success creates no `AthleteDecision`.** **Admission success creates no `AthleteDecision`.**
- **Delivery withheld / future delivery success is not an `AthleteDecision`** (delivery withheld ≠ delivery failure).
- **Silence / no response is not an `AthleteDecision`.**
- **Observed behavior is not an `AthleteDecision`** without `athlete-declared`/`athlete-reported` input (it may inform future hypotheses only, re-entering as observation).
- The runtime only **invites** a future decision (`athlete-decision-invitation`); it never records one.

[FACT] **Source honesty (structural):**
- **Valid decision sources remain only `athlete-declared` and `athlete-reported`.** Non-athlete sources (system/inferred/operator/AI/delivery/reflection) are a **compile error** on the typed path and **fail closed** at runtime.
- **Operator/scribe input is valid only as `athlete-reported` content; the operator is not the decision source.** **Operator mediation ≠ athlete decision.** **`athlete-reported` ≠ system-inferred.**

[FACT] **What remains UNCHANGED / still absent (intentional):**
- **AC20 is preserved (all AC20 guards green).** **No production module, no production decision-capture wrapper, no reflection-composition module, no production whole-core composer.** `offlineReflectionRuntime` is exercised **unchanged** (only to re-assert it auto-creates no decision).
- **No new persistence/event surface**: no production repository, DB, schema, migration, auth/session/user system, or event-recording integration. The harness may use the **existing in-memory** `AthleteDecisionRecordRepository` only.
- **No production code, test change to existing files, runtime shell, CLI/script/package command, API/UI/worker, deployment, CI, or SDK file** was added. `package.json` / `package-lock.json` / `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs` unchanged.

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **reflection-ready ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **validated reflection ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **delivery success ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **delivery withheld ≠ delivery failure** · **admission success ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **`validateDraft` success ≠ `AthleteDecision`**.
- **operator mediation ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **operator scribe ≠ decision source** · **`athlete-reported` ≠ system-inferred** · **observed behavior ≠ decision** · **silence ≠ decision**.
- **following Aurora ≠ obedience-success ≠ recommendation-quality proof** · **`AthleteDecision` re-entry as `SubjectiveObservation` ≠ `Signal`/`Evidence`** · **decision capture ≠ runtime rendering ≠ delivery**.
- **Aurora advises, the athlete decides** · **Aurora never presents inference as fact.**

[ASSUMPTION] The headline: **Aurora now proves the FULL post-reflection decision loop without breaking a single boundary — documented usage of the existing source-constrained `athleteDecision(...)` + `recordAthleteDecision(...)` + `decisionContext({ decisionSupportCaseRef })`, shown by one new `src/modules/__tests__/` file (+11 tests, 795/795 pass). A decision is captured only by an explicit `athlete-declared`/`athlete-reported` step, linked back to the reflection via the session's `sourceCaseRef`, and re-enters only as a `SubjectiveObservation` — never as `Signal`/`Evidence`. Nothing on the reflection/runtime path (reflection-ready, validateDraft, admission, delivery withheld, silence, observed behavior) ever auto-creates an `AthleteDecision`. It adds NO production code, runtime integration, decision-capture wrapper, runtime shell, CLI/script/package command, or API/UI/worker/deployment/CI/SDK file; `offlineReflectionRuntime` is unchanged; AC20 is preserved; the athlete remains the decision owner. A test proves the loop, not a deployment.**

[FACT] **Implementation 038-A** is complete; validation is now **803/803** (+8 tests). It proves the **operator

**docs-only checklist** (`docs/runbooks/operator-session-runbook.md`). It adds **NO production code, NO production
wrapper, NO CLI/runtime shell, NO script/package command, and NO API/UI/worker/deployment/CI/SDK files.** **AC20
is preserved**; **`offlineReflectionRuntime` remains unchanged** (only exercised). **Aurora advises; the athlete
decides.**

[FACT] **What this proves (the operator runbook, bound end-to-end):**
- The runbook sequence runs in one place: **athlete manual input → caller-assembled `RenderingRequest`
  (PREFERRED path: real `TerminalOutput` → `renderableFromTerminalOutput`) → `offlineReflectionRuntime` →
  `admitExternalRenderable` (Tier 2, before rendering) → render-only orchestration → `validateDraft` (Tier 3
  downstream) → reflection-ready → delivery withheld → no `AthleteDecision` → later explicit
  `athlete-declared`/`athlete-reported` capture → `recordAthleteDecision(...)` → `SubjectiveObservation`
  feedback only.**

  **preferred assembly path is `TerminalOutput → renderableFromTerminalOutput`**; **admission runs before
  rendering**; **`validateDraft` remains downstream**; **delivery is withheld**; **the runtime creates no
  `AthleteDecision`**.

  via `decisionContext({ decisionSupportCaseRef: sourceCaseRef })`; **operator/scribe is not the decision
  source**; **feedback re-enters only as a `SubjectiveObservation`** and **no `Signal`/`Evidence` is created
  directly**.

[FACT] **Fail-closed runbook dispositions proven (per-outcome operator obligations):**
- **`renderable-inadmissible` stops the runbook** — no provider/render/validate/deliver/decision; the operator
  must not strip safety fields to force admission.
- **`not-rendered` stops the runbook** — provider output is not safe; no delivery; no `AthleteDecision`.
- **`input-rejected` stops the runbook** — correct the athlete manual input; no admission/rendering; no
  `AthleteDecision`.
- **Silence/no-response creates no `AthleteDecision`.** Cross-path: it never delivers and never auto-creates a
  decision.

  `src/modules/__tests__/`; **no production module, no production wrapper, no `reflection-composition` module, no
  production whole-core composer.** `offlineReflectionRuntime` is **exercised unchanged**.
- **No live provider / real secret / `process.env`; no delivery sink** (deterministic fakes only). The checklist
  is **docs-only**; the human-readable runbook lives at `docs/runbooks/operator-session-runbook.md`.
- **No production code, test change to existing files, runtime shell, CLI/script/package command, API/UI/worker,
  deployment, CI, or SDK file** was added. `package.json` / `package-lock.json` / `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs`
  unchanged.

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **runbook ≠ CLI ≠ runtime shell ≠ deployment** · **caller assembly ≠ proof of truth** · **`TerminalOutput`
  preferred path ≠ production whole-core composer** · **AC20 seam ≠ whole-core composer**.
- **admission success ≠ evidence-backed fact** · **`validateDraft` success ≠ recommendation quality** ·
  **reflection-ready ≠ delivered** · **reflection-ready ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **delivery withheld ≠ delivery
  failure**.
- **operator mediation ≠ athlete decision** · **operator scribe ≠ decision source** · **silence ≠ decision** ·
  **decision feedback ≠ `Signal`/`Evidence`** · **decision capture ≠ runtime rendering ≠ delivery ≠
  recommendation-quality proof**.
- **Aurora advises, the athlete decides** · **Aurora never presents inference as fact.**

  test-only** envelope `OperatorInvocationResult`. The helper accepts a **caller-assembled**
  `OfflineReflectionRuntimeCommand` + **injected deterministic deps**, calls the existing
  `offlineReflectionRuntime(...)` (after `admitExternalRenderable`), and **narrows** the (already-safe) outcome to
  a **reference-only** envelope.

  preserved — no rename), `deliveryWithheld` (preserved), `rawRetained: false` (preserved), `reflectionRef?` (a
  **ref/summary only**, never `reflection.text`), the `decisionCapture` **invitation/ref only**, `admissionReason?`,

  `AthleteDecision` (asserted by field checks **and** a JSON banned-substring scan).

  production changes, documented in the proof.)

  (a throwing client proves stopped paths never render). The invocation surface is **not** a CLI/script/package
  command/API/UI/deployment, and **not** a production helper/wrapper — the helper is **local to the test**.
- **AC20 is preserved (all AC20 guards green).** No production module, no `src/modules/session`, no
  `reflection-composition` module, no production whole-core composer. `offlineReflectionRuntime` is invoked
  **unchanged**. `package.json` / `package-lock.json` / `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs` unchanged.

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **invocation surface ≠ CLI ≠ script ≠ package command ≠ deployment ≠ API/UI ≠ live-provider enablement ≠
  delivery mechanism ≠ whole-core composer ≠ AthleteDecision creator** · **safe envelope ≠ raw runtime dump** ·
  **AC20 seam ≠ whole-core composer**.
- **reflection-ready ≠ delivered** · **reflection-ready ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **deliveryWithheld ≠ delivery
  failure** · **admission success ≠ truth** · **`validateDraft` success ≠ recommendation quality** ·
  **decision-capture invitation ≠ `AthleteDecision`**.
- **Aurora advises, the athlete decides** · **Aurora never presents inference as fact.**

## Update — Implementation 040-A (Session Envelope Mapper + Type, production pure projection)

[FACT] **Implementation 040-A** is complete; validation is now **832/832** (+22 tests). It is the **first
production-code realization of the session envelope / redaction contract** (Spec 040 / Tech Spec 040A). It adds
`src/modules/application-orchestration/application/operator-session-envelope.ts` — the `OperatorSessionEnvelope`
type + `toOperatorSessionEnvelope(outcome: OfflineReflectionRuntimeOutcome): OperatorSessionEnvelope` — exported
additively from `application-orchestration/application/index.ts`, plus `operator-session-envelope.test.ts` (+9)
and `operator-session-envelope-negative-capability.test.ts` (+13). It is a **pure, synchronous, whitelist-only
mapper** — **NOT** an invocation helper, wrapper, CLI, runtime shell, delivery, live-provider enablement,
persistence, or `AthleteDecision` capture. **AC20 is preserved**; **`offlineReflectionRuntime` remains
unchanged**. **Aurora advises; the athlete decides.**

[FACT] **What this adds (a safety addition, not a product surface):**
- A **pure, synchronous** projection that **constructs the envelope field-by-field** (a whitelist) and **never
  spreads the raw outcome** (`{ ...outcome }`) — so no unsafe field can leak by accident. It makes Spec 040's
  redaction contract **enforceable in code**.
- It maps the **exact** statuses (no rename): `reflection-ready`, `renderable-inadmissible`, `not-rendered`,
  `input-rejected`, `recording-failed`, `unexpected-failure`.
- It **preserves** `deliveryWithheld` and sets/preserves `rawRetained: false`; on `reflection-ready` it exposes a
  `reflectionRef` + safe `reflectionFlags` **only** (never `reflection.text`); it exposes the `decisionCapture`
  **invitation/ref only**; it summarizes `trace` as **refs/codes only**; `admissionReason?`/`safeReason?` are safe
  closed codes.

[FACT] **What it always excludes (the redaction whitelist):**
- Raw provider output; hidden reasoning; secret material; delivery artifact / delivery ids; `eventRecordIds`;
  `AthleteDecision`; raw exception/stack; and any raw runtime internal not explicitly whitelisted.

[FACT] **What it never does:**
- Calls **no** runtime (`offlineReflectionRuntime`), provider/live client, delivery sink, repository, event
  recorder, or secret resolver; creates **no** `AthleteDecision`; records **no** events; reads **no**
  `process.env`. The mapper imports only **types** from the runtime file (never its function) + the admission-reason
  type — **no upstream core** (Impl 025 guard holds).

[FACT] **What remains UNCHANGED / still absent (intentional):**
- **AC20 preserved (all guards green).** No invocation helper/wrapper, no `src/modules/session`, no
  `reflection-composition` module, no production whole-core composer, no CLI/script/package command, no
  API/UI/worker/deployment/CI/SDK file. `offlineReflectionRuntime` unchanged; `package.json` /
  `package-lock.json` / `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs` unchanged.

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **envelope mapper ≠ invocation helper ≠ CLI ≠ script ≠ package command ≠ deployment ≠ API/UI ≠ live-provider
  enablement ≠ delivery mechanism ≠ whole-core composer ≠ AthleteDecision creator** · **safe envelope ≠ raw
  runtime dump** · **AC20 seam ≠ whole-core composer**.
- **reflectionRef ≠ reflection text** · **decisionCapture invitation/ref ≠ `AthleteDecision`** ·
  **reflection-ready ≠ delivered ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **deliveryWithheld ≠ delivery failure** · **admission
  success ≠ truth** · **`validateDraft` success ≠ recommendation quality**.
- **Aurora advises, the athlete decides** · **Aurora never presents inference as fact.**

[ASSUMPTION] The headline: **Aurora's session envelope / redaction contract is now realized in production code as
a pure, synchronous, whitelist-only mapper (`OperatorSessionEnvelope` + `toOperatorSessionEnvelope`, +22 tests,
832/832 pass) in `application-orchestration` — the first production code in several missions, and a SAFETY
addition, not a product surface. It narrows the already-safe `OfflineReflectionRuntimeOutcome` field-by-field
(never spreading it) across all six dispositions, preserving exact status / `deliveryWithheld` / `rawRetained:
false`, exposing only `reflectionRef`+flags (never the text), the decision-capture invitation/ref, and a ref-only
trace summary, while always excluding raw provider output / hidden reasoning / secrets / delivery ids /
eventRecordIds / AthleteDecision / raw stack. It invokes nothing, persists nothing, decides nothing, and imports
no upstream core; `offlineReflectionRuntime` is unchanged and AC20 is preserved. A mapper makes the contract
enforceable; it is not a helper, a caller, or a surface.**

---

## Update — Implementation 041-A (Production Operator Invocation Helper, safe envelope only)

[FACT] **Implementation 041-A** is complete; validation is now **852/852** (+20 tests). It adds the **production
operator invocation helper** (Spec 041 / Tech Spec 041A) — the single safe handle that makes
`toOperatorSessionEnvelope` **mandatory** at the invocation seam. It adds
`src/modules/application-orchestration/application/operator-session-invocation.ts` exporting
`invokeOperatorSession<TSubmission>(command: OfflineReflectionRuntimeCommand<TSubmission>, deps:
OfflineReflectionRuntimeDependencies<TSubmission>): Promise<OperatorSessionEnvelope>` (additively exported from
`application-orchestration/application/index.ts`), plus `operator-session-invocation.test.ts` (+7) and
`operator-session-invocation-negative-capability.test.ts` (+13). It is a **production safety seam** — **NOT** a
CLI, script/package command, API/UI, deployment, runtime shell, live-provider enablement, delivery, persistence,
`AthleteDecision` capture, or whole-core composition. **AC20 is preserved.** **Aurora advises; the athlete
decides.**

[FACT] **What this adds (a safety guarantee the mapper alone cannot enforce):**
- The helper accepts a **caller-assembled `OfflineReflectionRuntimeCommand`** + **injected
  `OfflineReflectionRuntimeDependencies`**, calls `offlineReflectionRuntime(command, deps)` **once**, immediately
  maps through `toOperatorSessionEnvelope(outcome)`, and returns **only** `OperatorSessionEnvelope`.
- Returning only the envelope makes the raw `OfflineReflectionRuntimeOutcome` **structurally unreachable** through
  the helper: it **never** returns the raw outcome, a tuple `{ outcome, envelope }`, `reflection.text`, raw
  provider output, hidden reasoning, secrets, delivery artifact / delivery ids, `eventRecordIds`, or
  `AthleteDecision`.
- **No helper-level `try/catch`:** `offlineReflectionRuntime` already wraps its body and returns a safe
  `unexpected-failure` outcome on any error (never throws / never leaks), so the helper preserves that behavior and
  is a pure pass-through to the mandatory mapper.

[FACT] **What it never does:**
- Creates no deps; reads no process environment; resolves no real secrets; selects no provider; calls no live
  provider directly; calls no delivery sink directly; persists no session/events; creates no `AthleteDecision`;
  does not assemble the whole-core chain. It imports **only** `offlineReflectionRuntime` + `toOperatorSessionEnvelope`
  (and their types) — **no upstream core** (Impl 025 guard holds).

[FACT] **What remains UNCHANGED / still absent (intentional):**
- **AC20 preserved (all guards green).** No new `src/modules/session`, no `reflection-composition` module, no
  production whole-core composer, no CLI/script/package command, no API/UI/worker/deployment/CI/SDK file.
  `offlineReflectionRuntime` and `toOperatorSessionEnvelope` are **unchanged**; `package.json` /
  `package-lock.json` / `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs` unchanged.

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **invocation helper ≠ CLI ≠ script ≠ package command ≠ deployment ≠ API/UI ≠ live-provider enablement ≠
  delivery mechanism ≠ persistence/session record ≠ whole-core composer ≠ AthleteDecision creator ≠ truth
  validator ≠ recommendation quality proof** · **`OperatorSessionEnvelope` ≠ raw runtime outcome** · **AC20 seam
  ≠ whole-core composer**.
- **reflection-ready ≠ delivered ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **deliveryWithheld ≠ delivery failure** ·
  **decisionCapture invitation/ref ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **admission success ≠ truth** · **`validateDraft`
  success ≠ recommendation quality**.
- **Aurora advises, the athlete decides** · **Aurora never presents inference as fact.**

[ASSUMPTION] The headline: **Aurora now has a production invocation handle — `invokeOperatorSession` (+20 tests,
852/852 pass) — that runs the offline reflection runtime once and returns ONLY the safe `OperatorSessionEnvelope`,
making the raw `OfflineReflectionRuntimeOutcome` structurally unreachable. The mapper made redaction enforceable;
the helper makes it unavoidable. It is still NOT a CLI/API/deployment/runtime shell/live-provider/delivery/
persistence surface; it invokes the existing runtime once over injected deps, imports no upstream core, creates no
`AthleteDecision`, persists nothing, and has no own try/catch (the runtime already normalizes `unexpected-failure`).
`offlineReflectionRuntime` and the mapper are unchanged; AC20 is preserved. A future CLI/API must sit behind this
helper and receive only the envelope.**

---

## Update — Specification 042 (Real Caller / Operator Use Protocol Boundary, docs-only governance gate)

[FACT] **Specification 042** is complete; validation remains **852/852** (docs-only). It adds a **governance /
decision-gate boundary** (`docs/specs/042-real-caller-operator-use-protocol-boundary.md`) — **no production code,
no tests, no runtime/API/UI/CLI/worker/deployment/CI/SDK files, no persistence/event integration, no
provider/live/delivery integration, no DB/auth/session work.** It modifies **no** code: `invokeOperatorSession`,
`OperatorSessionEnvelope`, `offlineReflectionRuntime`, `toOperatorSessionEnvelope`, the package files, and
`scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs` are all **unchanged**. **AC20 remains unchanged.** **Aurora advises; the athlete
decides.**

[FACT] **What this fixes (an explicit evidence gate, not a build):**
- It **converts the repeated "no real caller yet" deferral into an explicit evidence gate.** Aurora will not build
  a CLI/script/package command, API/UI, persistence/event integration, provider/deployment lane, live-provider,
  delivery, DB/auth/session, or an AC20 amendment **until that lane's own concrete, recurring, demonstrated
  evidence threshold is met.**
- **Each lane is unlocked only by its own evidence; evidence for one lane does not unlock another.** The existence
  of the runbook / helper / envelope is **insufficient evidence by itself.**

[FACT] **What operator use is today (manual / offline):**
- Operator use **remains manual and offline**, **sits behind `invokeOperatorSession`**, and the operator **receives
  only `OperatorSessionEnvelope`**. **Delivery remains withheld; no default live provider; no automatic
  `AthleteDecision`.** Later decision capture remains **separate** and **athlete-declared/reported** (Impl 037-A).

[FACT] **Distinctions this update makes explicit** (do not collapse):
- **real caller ≠ hypothetical future UI ≠ developer convenience ≠ package-script desire ≠ deployment target ≠
  provider choice ≠ persistence need ≠ athlete decision ≠ operator curiosity** · **caller evidence for one lane ≠
  evidence for another lane** · **`invokeOperatorSession` seam ≠ product surface**.
- **operator use protocol ≠ CLI ≠ API/UI ≠ deployment ≠ delivery ≠ persistence ≠ athlete decision** ·
  **`OperatorSessionEnvelope` ≠ raw runtime outcome** · **reflection-ready ≠ delivered ≠ `AthleteDecision`** ·
  **deliveryWithheld ≠ delivery failure** · **decisionCapture invitation/ref ≠ `AthleteDecision`** · **AC20 seam ≠
  whole-core composer**.
- **Aurora advises, the athlete decides** · **Aurora never presents inference as fact.**

[ASSUMPTION] The headline: **Aurora's safe invocation chain is complete, and Spec 042 now governs whether it may
grow a surface — by evidence, not inertia. Aurora will not build CLI/API/persistence/provider/deployment/live/
delivery/DB-auth or amend AC20 until each lane's explicit evidence threshold is met; until then operator use stays
manual/offline behind `invokeOperatorSession`, returning only the envelope, delivery withheld, no automatic
decision, with later capture kept separate. A docs-only gate; no code, no surface; AC20 preserved.**

## 1. Executive Summary

[FACT]
- **The reasoning core is implemented end-to-end.** All five ladder stages exist in code (`observation → reasoning → understanding → decision-support`) and Implementation 006 composes them into one demonstrated chain.
- **The first full output is `Reflection`, not `Recommendation`.** The end-to-end integration test proves a complete chain that lands on a modest voice.
- **The system demonstrates restraint *by construction*.** Even with complete traceability and clean gates, a single chain tops out at Reflection because the understanding ceiling caps the voice — restraint is structural, not a runtime preference.
- **The current suite proves the core can compose without overreaching.** 145 tests pass, including module-boundary tests, negative-capability ("defining") tests, and the end-to-end Reflection proof.
- **Persistence exists now, but only as ports + in-memory adapters (Impl 010):** validated `toState()`/`reconstitute()` + repository ports for the six persisted boundaries, all in-memory. **Production persistence remains absent** — no **production DB/ORM/schema/migrations**, no **event bus**, no **cache**, no **`src/infrastructure`**, no **projection repository**.
- **Event/outcome records exist now, as a dependency-neutral append-only log (Impl 011):** the `event-recording` module records *what happened* — one ref-only `DomainEventRecord` (occurrence/outcome) over a closed catalog, with a `TraceabilityEnvelope` and an append-only in-memory log/repository — **complementing the aggregate repositories, not replacing them**. It remains **non-command, non-bus**: no event bus, publish/subscribe, handlers, async delivery, serialization tech, or **event sourcing**.
- **Reprojection exists now, as a neutral check-only harness (Impl 012):** a recompute-and-compare *safety mechanism* (test-support under `__tests__/reprojection-harness/`, **not a production module**) that re-derives `UnderstandingAssessment` through the owning module, recalculates freshness, detects candidates from event records, and **reports** drift/findings — **mutating nothing, executing no event, rebuilding nothing from the log, and turning no projection into truth**. No scheduler, event sourcing, or projection repository exists.
- **A real "data in" boundary exists now (Impl 013):** an `observation`-owned **Manual Input Adapter** records manually supplied input faithfully as an `ObservationSet` (via `recordObservationSet`, persisted through `ObservationSetRepository`), preserving provenance/source/quality and verbatim words, representing missing data explicitly, and rejecting the unrepresentable — **without interpreting, detecting a `Signal`, reasoning, mutating athlete records, or triggering downstream effects**. No UI/API/LLM/external integration exists; `observation` imports no `event-recording`.
- **A real "output out" boundary exists now (Impl 014):** a downstream **`rendering` module** turns a domain-approved `TerminalOutput` into human-facing text via a **deterministic fake renderer + a mandatory validator** — preserving voice/uncertainty/limitations/freshness/traceability/agency and **refusing** any draft that escalates voice, strengthens a claim, hides uncertainty, or invents a fact (safe non-render on failure). Generated text is **presentation, not authority**: rendering selects no voice, creates no `TerminalOutput`, mutates no aggregate, and writes no event. **No real LLM provider/prompt/UI/API/external call** exists.
- **The output-out cycle is now auditable (Impl 015):** **inside `rendering`**, an append-only **`RenderedMessageRecord`** + an append-only **`RenderReview`** (display-safety only) + a **derived `DisplayEligibility`**, behind a **repository port + in-memory adapter**. Persistence/review improve **auditability and display safety only** — a record is **never** domain truth, approval **never** strengthens the domain, rejection **invalidates nothing**, failed attempts are **never** display-eligible, and nothing triggers an event or delivery. **No rendered-output events, no production DB, no delivery/UI/API/provider.**
- **A delivery/exposure boundary exists now (Impl 016):** a downstream **`delivery` module** exposes a *display-eligible* `RenderedMessageRecord` to a **deterministic test-only sink** and records the attempt as an auditable **`DeliveryRecord`** (repository port + in-memory adapter). Delivery **verifies** eligibility via `rendering`'s `displayEligibilityOf(record)` (it never re-derives it), calls the sink **only** when eligible *and* the target is the supported `test-sink`, and **blocks** every ineligible/unsupported request. **Delivery is exposure and auditability only** — **success is not evidence, failure is not domain invalidation**; it mutates no rendered record/aggregate, emits no event, and triggers no reasoning/reprojection/retry. **No real provider/channel, UI/API, scheduler/retry, event bus, delivery events, or production DB.**
- **A provider adapter seam exists now (Impl 017):** **inside `rendering`**, a deterministic **fake provider** may **draft** human-facing text — an **untrusted `ProviderDraft`** that becomes a `RenderedMessage` **only** by passing the **unchanged mandatory `validateDraft`** (the validator, not the provider, is the authority). The provider replaces **only** the draft-text step; an unsafe request is refused **before** the call; every failure/unsafe draft **degrades to safe non-rendering**.
