The provider **selects no voice, creates no `TerminalOutput`/`Recommendation`/`RenderedMessage`/record, and persists/reviews/marks-display-eligible/delivers/emits/mutates nothing**. **No real SDK/API/network/prompt-templates and no `provider`/`llm` module exist.**
- **A provider-attempt audit exists now (Impl 018):** **inside `rendering`**, an append-only **`ProviderAttemptRecord`** (repository port + in-memory adapter) records *what the seam did* by **observing** a `ProviderRenderOutcome` — a **safe summary** (status + reasons reusing the real `ProviderFailure`/`RenderingFailure` catalogs) with **no raw draft retention** (`rawDraftRetained` literal `false`). The audit **does not call** the provider/`requestProviderRendering`/`validateDraft`; it **creates no `RenderedMessage`/record/review/display-eligibility/delivery**, **appends no event**, **triggers no retry/reprojection/reasoning**, and **mutates nothing**; a **validation failure is not domain invalidation**. It is **auditability, not authority** — not model evaluation, not telemetry. It **auto-emits no event** (Impl 024 later added a ref-only `ProviderAttemptRecorded` event type that may *reference* the audit record by id — see the Impl 024 bullet above — but the audit neither imports `event-recording` nor emits one); **no real SDK exists.**
- **A real-provider-ready boundary exists now (Impl 019):** **inside `rendering`**, an **additive async** path makes a real provider **pluggable** while **changing only the draft source** — the **synchronous Impl 017 seam is untouched**. An async **`ProviderClientBoundary`** (proven with a deterministic **`FakeProviderClient`**) takes operational **`ProviderSecretRef`s** (never raw secrets; no `process.env`), structured **`ProviderInstruction`** material (derived, not a prompt template), and maps a closed **`ProviderOperationalFailure`** **down** to the existing `ProviderFailure` (**not expanded**). `requestRealProviderRendering` **reuses** the unchanged `providerRenderingRequestFrom` guard + the mandatory **`validateDraft`** and returns the existing `ProviderRenderOutcome`; every failure **degrades to safe non-rendering** with **no automatic retry**, **no automatic persistence**, and **no review/display/delivery/event/domain-mutation**. **Real-provider-*ready*, not real-provider-*integrated*:** no real SDK/API/network/secret/prompt exists.
- **A concrete-provider adapter shell exists now (Impl 020):** **inside `rendering/application`**, the **first selected-provider adapter** behind the async `ProviderClientBoundary` — a **`ConcreteProviderClient`** (disabled by default → safe failure, no work; no live call path) plus a pure **serializer / parser / error-mapper**. The provider target (**OpenAI**) is selected at the **doc/decision level (020A) only**; code stays **vendor-neutral** (`concrete-provider-*`), so **no guard was weakened and no vendor token leaks into a guarded file**. The serializer projects only safe constraints (no arbitrary prompt / chain-of-thought field); the parser returns an **untrusted draft + operational metadata** (no raw payload, no `RenderedMessage`); the error mapper maps provider-shaped errors **down** to the existing `ProviderOperationalFailure` → `ProviderFailure` (**not expanded**). A draft becomes a message **only** via the unchanged `validateDraft`; the audit stays raw-free by explicit composition. **No SDK/package change, no network, no `process.env`, no raw secret, no prompt template, no retry/scheduler, and no record/review/display/delivery/event/domain side effect.** **Selected-provider *shell*, not live integration.**
- **An opt-in live-provider boundary exists now (Impl 021):** **inside `rendering/application`**, the **first live-call edge** behind the async `ProviderClientBoundary` — a **`LiveProviderClient`** driven by an injected **`LiveCallPolicy`** (disabled by default; explicit opt-in; no env inference), an injected **`ProviderCredentialResolver`** (deterministic `StaticProviderCredentialResolver` for tests; **no env resolver, no `process.env`**), and a single **`LiveProviderHttpTransport`** — the **only** file permitted a network token (native `fetch` behind an injected endpoint; **no SDK, no dependency/lockfile change**). It **fails closed before any transport call** when the policy is disabled or the credential is missing/invalid; **reuses** the unchanged serializer/parser/error-mapper; **never calls `validateDraft`** (validation stays with `requestRealProviderRendering`); provider output stays **untrusted**. Failures map onto the existing `ProviderOperationalFailure → ProviderFailure` (**not expanded**); the audit stays raw-free by explicit composition. **Default tests / CI make no live call and need no credentials**; the network-guard exception is **surgical** (one approved file; vendor/SDK/env stay forbidden everywhere); the sync seam, `FakeProviderAdapter`, `FakeProviderClient`, and `ConcreteProviderClient` are untouched; **no record/review/display/delivery/event/domain side effect, no retry/scheduler**. **Live-call-*capable*, not a production rollout.**
- **An injected environment credential resolver exists now (Impl 022):** **inside `rendering/application`**, an **`EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver`** behind the **unchanged** injected `ProviderCredentialResolver` port (a **sibling** of `StaticProviderCredentialResolver`). It reads **one explicitly configured key** from an **injected `EnvironmentCredentialSource`** (`Readonly<Record<string, string | undefined>>`) — no scan, no fallback, no domain-derived name — and classifies absent → `missing`; blank/control/too-short → `invalid`; else → `available` with the existing opaque transient `ProviderCredentialToken`. The **raw secret stays transient** (never in failures/outcome/audit/state/metadata/tests); **credential availability is not live-call enablement** (a disabled `LiveCallPolicy` still blocks the transport; a missing/invalid credential blocks it too); the resolver **calls no transport/provider/`validateDraft`**, persists/audits/mutates nothing. The catalogs are not expanded. **An injected *operational* resolver, not a production secret manager.**
- **A one-file process-environment source adapter exists now (Impl 023):** **inside `rendering/application`**, a **`ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter`** binds the **real process environment** to the resolver's injected source — it **feeds, does not replace,** `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver`. It reads **exactly one configured key** (neutral `AURORA_PROVIDER_CREDENTIAL`) via an **injected `ProcessEnvironmentAccessor`** (called once), returning a source with only that key when present, else empty; it **classifies nothing** (the resolver still does). The **direct `process.env` token now appears in exactly one production file** (`process-environment-credential-source-adapter.ts`, via `defaultProcessEnvironmentAccessor`), enforced by a **new repo-wide guard** — **no existing guard was weakened**. Tests inject a **fake accessor** and need **no real environment value**; the default factory's real read is never exercised by the default suite. **Availability is still not live-call enablement** (disabled policy / missing credential each block the transport); the raw secret never enters errors/outcome/audit/state/metadata; the adapter calls no resolver(unless composed)/live-client/transport/provider/`validateDraft`, persists/audits/logs nothing, and adds **no dependency**. **A one-file *operational* source adapter, not a production secret manager.**
- **The output-out edge is now occurrence-traceable (Impl 024):** the `event-recording` module gained an **additive provider/rendering/delivery occurrence event surface** — `ProducingModule` += `rendering`/`delivery`, `EventArtifactKind` += `ProviderAttemptRecord`/`RenderedMessageRecord`/`RenderReview`/`DeliveryRequest`/`DeliveryRecord` (`DisplayEligibility` stays a ref *role*, not a kind), and eight occurrence/outcome `DomainEventType`s — plus **eight pure factories** that build records through the existing `DomainEventRecord.record(...)`. The factories are **ref-only, raw-free, and inert**: they reference artifacts by id only, **persist nothing**, **call no provider/transport/validator/renderer/delivery sink**, **create no downstream artifact**, **mutate no domain**, and **emit from nothing automatically** (recording is explicit application composition). `event-recording` stays **dependency-neutral** (imports only `shared-kernel`; rendering/delivery/provider import no `event-recording`). A provider/delivery success event is **never** evidence, recommendation quality, an athlete decision, a retry, or a delivery command. **No event bus / queue / scheduler / telemetry / DB exists; the two earlier "catalog not extended" guards were reconciled, not weakened.** Events record what happened; they do not make anything happen.
- **An explicit application orchestration boundary exists now (Impl 025):** a new **application-composition module** `application-orchestration` whose one surface, **`orchestrateRenderDeliver(command, deps)`**, composes the **existing** public services of `rendering`/`delivery`/`event-recording` in a **fixed, explicit order** over **injected** collaborators — returning a **closed `OrchestrationOutcome`** (8 kinds) + a **ref-only `OrchestrationTrace`**. It is **not a domain capability module**: it owns **no domain model, no repository, no persistence of its own**, and introduces **no bounded context**. Every step is an explicit call (provider rendering → provider-attempt audit + explicit save → rendered-message record + explicit save → review + explicit save → derived display eligibility → delivery (self-persisting) → Impl 024 occurrence events via `append`); **no event or repository write triggers the next step**, **delivery is never automatic** (display eligibility is necessary, not sufficient), and **failures are safe stops or a non-invalidating `partial-success`, never an automatic retry**. The trace/result carry **safe refs only** (no raw draft/prompt/payload/secret/env value/message body). It imports **only public module surfaces** (+ `shared-kernel`) and the `ProviderClientBoundary` abstraction — never live transport, the credential resolver internals, the process-env adapter, or concrete-provider internals; **rendering/delivery/event-recording do not import it**. **AC20 was updated additively** (approved module, not a weakening). **No event bus / scheduler / retry / workflow engine / telemetry / DB, no automatic delivery, no hidden side effect, no domain mutation, and no dependency/package change.** Composition is explicit; it is not a hidden side effect.
- **An opt-in live-provider smoke-test boundary exists now (Impl 026):** a **pure, fully-injected helper** inside `rendering/application` — **`liveProviderSmoke(command, deps)`** — that exercises **one** live provider call through the **existing** seam (`requestRealProviderRendering(...) → the unchanged validateDraft`) **only** behind explicit, ordered, fail-closed gates (**opt-in → CI → credential → live policy**, each stopping **before** any provider call), returning a **closed, redacted `LiveProviderSmokeResult`** (`rawRetained: false`; 9 closed statuses; no rendered body / raw draft / payload / response / secret / env value). It is **not an operator script and adds no npm script**; it **reads no `process.env`** (opt-in/CI injected; credential via the injected resolver); it makes **at most one call (no loops, no re-issue)**; and it **imports no** live HTTP transport / process-env adapter / concrete-provider internals / `delivery` / `event-recording` / `application-orchestration`, and is imported by no module outside `rendering`. It **persists nothing, delivers nothing, records no event, creates no evidence / athlete decision, and mutates no domain**. **The default suite and CI make no live call and need no credential**; the repo-wide `process.env` one-file guard and the live-provider guard stay green; AC20 is untouched (no new module). **Smoke success is wiring success, not evidence; smoke failure is not domain failure.** The **operator entrypoint that reads real env flags remains future** (Tech Spec 026A §14). A smoke test proves wiring, not wisdom.
- **A manual operator live-smoke entrypoint exists now (Impl 027):** a **manual, executable `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs`** (plain ESM, **outside `src`/`tsconfig.include`/the default test glob/both guard scan roots**) that reads the **real** opt-in/CI/endpoint flags, resolves the credential **only** through the approved `ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter → EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver` chain, wires the existing public live-provider surfaces, and **calls `liveProviderSmoke` once** — preserving `requestRealProviderRendering` + the mandatory `validateDraft`, **duplicating no smoke semantics**. It prints **one redacted JSON object** (`rawRetained: false`, `wiringOnly`, `sideEffects: "none"`; no rendered body / raw draft / payload / response / secret / env value) and exits **0** for `passed`/`not-enabled`/`ci-disabled`, **1** for operational failures (verified end-to-end). It is **run manually** (`node scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs`) — **not an npm script, not in `npm run check`, not in the default suite, no CI-live lane** — and **persists/delivers/records/orchestrates/mutates nothing**. A **pure, typechecked `src` helper** (`operator-live-smoke-entrypoint.ts`) holds the decidable/redaction logic and **reads no `process.env`** (injected record). The **production `src` `process.env` seal stays intact** (the credential is read only by the one approved adapter; the script's flag reads are outside `src`); **Node 22 native type-stripping** lets the `.mjs` import the real `.ts` `src` with **no build and no dependency** (027A-verified); the Impl 026 `scripts/` guard was **reconciled (strengthened, not weakened)** to allow only this approved entrypoint. **No package/lockfile change, no SDK, no dependency.** The operator can now run the wire; the wire still proves wiring, not wisdom.
- **A provider-neutral managed-secret credential-source seam exists now (Impl 028):** a pure TypeScript async interface **`ManagedSecretStoreClient`** (`retrieve(secretName): Promise<ManagedSecretResolution>`) behind which any managed secret store can supply a credential, and a **`ManagedSecretCredentialSource`** class with **`async toEnvironmentCredentialSource()`** that pre-fetches the secret and produces the `EnvironmentCredentialSource` map consumed by the **unchanged synchronous `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver`** (pre-fetch pattern: `await` the source before constructing the resolver). The 4-state `ManagedSecretResolution` (`available`/`missing`/`invalid`/`unavailable`) maps non-`available` paths to an empty source → the resolver classifies as `missing` → **no provider call**. A **deterministic `FakeManagedSecretStoreClient`** covers all 4 scenarios (sentinel `"opaque:test-managed-secret"`; no real secret). **No cloud SDK, no `process.env` read, no dependency change, no new module, no live-call enablement; +39 tests; process-env seal intact; operator script unchanged.** `secret manager = credential source; managed-secret seam ≠ live-call enablement ≠ cloud adapter ≠ production rollout.`
- **A cloud-secret adapter contract exists now (Impl 029):** **inside `rendering/application`**, **behind the Impl 028 managed-secret seam**, a **`CloudSecretStoreAdapter` that `implements ManagedSecretStoreClient`** drives an **injected `CloudSecretValueClient`** — a cloud-like transport boundary **distinct from `ManagedSecretStoreClient`** that **MAY throw** (the adapter catches and fails closed). It maps a richer cloud-like outcome union (**`CloudSecretLookupResult`**, classified by the closed redacted **`CloudSecretAdapterFailureCode`**) into the existing 4-state `ManagedSecretResolution`: `found` (valid) → `available`; `blank`/control found value → `invalid`; `malformed` → `invalid`; `not_found`/empty ref → `missing`; `denied`/`unauthenticated`/`unavailable`/`timeout`/`throttled`/thrown exception → `unavailable`. `retrieve()` **always resolves, never rejects**; a **deterministic `FakeCloudSecretValueClient`** covers every scenario incl. "throws" (sentinel `"opaque:test-cloud-secret"`; no real secret/SDK/network); it **redacts raw secret values AND raw cloud responses** (proven by markers `sk-test-cloud-secret-do-not-leak`, `raw-cloud-response-do-not-leak`, `cloud-access-token-do-not-leak`). **No concrete provider selected (no AWS/GCP/Azure), no SDK/dependency, no real cloud/network call, no `process.env` read, no source precedence, no live-call enablement; +38 tests; 710/710 pass; process-env seal intact; operator script unchanged.** `cloud-like adapter contract ≠ selected provider ≠ SDK integration ≠ production rollout ≠ live-call enablement; safe cloud failure code ≠ raw cloud response; secret ref ≠ secret value.`
- **What does not exist yet:** no UI, API, **production DB/persistence**, **real LLM provider/SDK** (a deterministic rendering boundary — Impl 014 — a fake **provider adapter seam** behind the unchanged validator — Impl 017 — **provider-attempt audit** — Impl 018 — a **real-provider-*ready* async client boundary** — Impl 019 — a **selected-provider adapter shell** (neutral code, disabled by default, deterministic serializer/parser/error-mapper) — Impl 020 — and an **opt-in live-provider boundary** (fail-closed, native `fetch` isolated in one approved file, injected credential resolver) — Impl 021 — an **injected environment credential resolver** (one configured key from an injected source map) — Impl 022 — and a **one-file process-environment source adapter** (the real `process.env` bound through one approved file, sealed by a repo-wide guard) — Impl 023 — and an **opt-in live-provider smoke-test boundary helper** (pure/injected, one bounded call through the existing seam behind the unchanged validator, redacted result) — Impl 026 — and a **manual operator live-smoke entrypoint** (`scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs` — manual, executable, redacted JSON, outside the default suite/CI/npm scripts; reads real flags outside `src`; credential via the approved adapter chain) — Impl 027 — exist, **and a provider-neutral managed-secret credential-source seam** (`ManagedSecretCredentialSource`/`ManagedSecretStoreClient`, pre-fetch pattern) — Impl 028 — exists, **and a cloud-secret adapter *contract* behind that seam** (`CloudSecretStoreAdapter implements ManagedSecretStoreClient`, driving an injected `CloudSecretValueClient` that maps a richer cloud-like outcome union to the 4-state resolution, fails closed, redacts raw secret values and raw cloud responses) — Impl 029 — exists, but **no concrete cloud provider selected, no real cloud SDK adapter (no AWS/GCP/Azure), no production secret wiring, no source precedence, no rotation/cache/TTL, no npm script, no SDK/dependency, no production secret manager, no CI-live lane, no default/CI live call or credential, and no production rollout**), **real delivery channel/provider** (a delivery boundary with a deterministic test sink exists — Impl 016 — but no email/SMS/push/web channel), event bus, notification layer, scheduler/retry layer, **auto-emission / event-bus delivery / self-persistence for the new ref-only provider/rendering/delivery occurrence event surface** (the inert surface itself exists — Impl 024), provider telemetry / model evaluation, or Garmin/FIT adapter. An **explicit application orchestration boundary** now exists (Impl 025 — `orchestrateRenderDeliver` composes the existing services over injected collaborators), and **Aurora's first PRODUCT-RUNTIME code slice** now exists too (Impl 032R-A — a pure application-level `offlineReflectionRuntime(command, deps)` in `application-orchestration` that wires the injected manual-intake collaborator + render-only `orchestrateRenderDeliver`, projects a safe athlete-facing reflection, withholds delivery, and returns a decision-capture prompt while creating no `AthleteDecision`), and the **first operator-mediated reflection SESSION now exists as a TEST-LEVEL PROOF** (Impl 036-A — a TEST-ONLY whole-core responsible-reflection harness under `src/modules/__tests__/` that composes the real chain end-to-end: athlete manual input → real `TerminalOutput` → `renderableFromTerminalOutput` → `RenderingRequest` → `offlineReflectionRuntime` → `admitExternalRenderable` (Tier 2) → render-only orchestration → downstream `validateDraft` → reflection-ready → delivery withheld → no `AthleteDecision`), but it is **offline / operator-mediated only** — **no production session service/wrapper/CLI, no API/UI/worker, no deployment, no production rollout, no real reasoning pipeline** (the `ObservationSet → reasoning → understanding → decision-support → RenderableDomainOutput` composition is still future; the renderable is supplied in the command — now produced from a real `TerminalOutput` inside the test harness only; whole-core composition remains a TEST HARNESS, with no production whole-core composer and no reflection-composition module), and a **production orchestration *entrypoint*** (a UI/API/use-case surface that *calls* it, or a scheduler/event-driven trigger) does **not** exist. The `athlete` module now holds **Purpose (Impl 007) + AthleteDecision (Impl 009)** — but **full Athlete** (state/capacity/constraints/path-memory), a **full `DecisionOutcome` object**, a **pattern engine**, and any **compliance/outcome-based validation** are still absent. These are **intentional absences** (see §6), not gaps left by mistake.

[ASSUMPTION] The one-sentence claim this review defends: **Aurora can run the full reasoning core end-to-end and still refuse to overreach.**

---

## 2. Implemented Core Flow

[FACT] The implemented flow, stage by stage. "Refuses to" names what is *unrepresentable or rejected* at that stage, not merely untested.

```
ObservationSet → Observation → ContextualizedObservation → Signal/SignalRejection
   → EvidenceCase → Hypothesis lifecycle → UnderstandingProfile update
   → UnderstandingAssessment → DecisionSupportCase → Terminal Output (DecisionSupport: Reflection)
```

| Step | Owning module | Implemented object(s) | Protected invariant | Handoff downstream | Refuses to |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| **ObservationSet / Observation** | `observation` | `ObservationSet`, `MeasuredObservation`, `SubjectiveObservation`, `MissingDataObservation`, `Provenance`, `Source`, `ObservationQuality` | Provenance/quality born at capture and immutable; corrections supersede, never overwrite; incompleteness explicit | raw, provenance-bearing observations | hold any interpretation/meaning field |
| **ContextualizedObservation** | `observation/signal` | `ContextualFrame`, `ContextualizedObservation`, `TraceToObservation` | Frame is context, not conclusion; the original is never mutated; trace to the set/observation is born here | a contextualized observation | assign meaning or direction |
| **Signal / SignalRejection** | `observation/signal` | `Signal`, `SignalRejection`, `SignalDetectionPolicy` (`expectedRangeDeviationPolicy`) | Relevance-without-meaning; every outcome is a Signal *or* an auditable rejection (nothing silently dropped); quality/provenance travel forward | a `Signal` (or recorded rejection) | become evidence; resolve a source conflict |
| **EvidenceCase** | `reasoning` | `EvidenceCase`, `TraceToSignal`, `EvidenceDirection` | An `EvidenceCase` is created **only** by `Hypothesis.attachEvidence`; a `SignalRejection` can never become evidence | evidence attached to a claim | exist standalone; outside a hypothesis |
| **Hypothesis lifecycle** | `reasoning` | `Hypothesis` (aggregate root), `Falsifier`, `ClaimConfidence`, lifecycle states/transitions | Always falsifiable; calibrated, defeasible confidence; no silent transitions; never "certain" | a settled lifecycle **outcome** | become a fact; be certain |
| **UnderstandingProfile update** | `understanding` | `UnderstandingProfile` (aggregate), `UnderstandingDimension`, `ReasoningOutcome` adapter, `SurvivedChallenge`, `Surprise`, `Staleness`, `Fragility` | Per-dimension, never global; promotion only by survived challenge across ≥2 distinct conditions; population/repetition never promote; history never deleted | a per-dimension level + trail | read raw signals; store claim confidence; go global |
| **UnderstandingAssessment** | `understanding` | `UnderstandingAssessment`, `SafeVoiceCeiling`, `deriveSafeVoiceCeiling` | Read-only projection; staleness/fragility can only **lower** the ceiling; the ceiling is **not** a `VoiceMode` | a `SafeVoiceCeiling` (max assertiveness) | select a voice; recommend |
| **DecisionSupportCase** | `decision-support` | `DecisionOpportunity`, `DecisionSupportCase` (aggregate), 5 gates, `TraceabilityVerification`, `VoiceSelectionPolicy`, `VoiceMode`, terminal outputs, `SupportQuality` | No output before gates run; voice gated not derived; Recommendation needs complete trace + confident ceiling; agency preserved; `AthleteDecision` referenced, never owned | a terminal output | own the decision; author claims; command |
| **Terminal Output** | `decision-support` | `DecisionSupport` (with `VoiceMode`), `Inquiry`, `Withholding` | `DecisionSupport` requires `preservesAgency: true` (literal); `Inquiry` is not a `VoiceMode`; `Withholding` carries an auditable reason | (the athlete-facing edge) | emit a command; hide uncertainty |

---

## 3. Module Inventory

### `observation` *(intake + Manual Input Adapter — Impl 013)*
[FACT] Implements `ObservationSet` (aggregate), `MeasuredObservation` / `SubjectiveObservation` / `MissingDataObservation`, `Provenance` / `Source` / `ObservationQuality`, `ContextualFrame` + `contextualize`, `Signal` / `SignalRejection`, and `expectedRangeDeviationPolicy` (the `SignalDetectionPolicy`). Coordinators: `recordObservationSet`, `detectSignals`. **Plus the Manual Input Adapter (Impl 013):** `ManualInputSubmission`, `ManualInputEntry`, `ManualInputIngestionOutcome` + closed rejection/limitation/quality catalogs, and `ingestManualInput({ submission, observationSetRepository })`.
- **Clarify:** `observation` still does **not reason** — it imports only `shared-kernel`; `Hypothesis`/`Evidence`/`Impact`/`Understanding`/`DecisionSupport` are not reachable here. **A `Signal` is not `Evidence`** — it asserts only *possible relevance to a future reasoning question*, with no slot for cause/impact/state.
- **Manual Input Adapter (Impl 013):** the first real **"data in"** boundary — it records manual input **faithfully as an `ObservationSet`** (via `recordObservationSet`, persisted through `ObservationSetRepository`), preserving **verbatim subjective `words`**, **explicit missing data**, and **provenance/quality** (`source: "manual"`). It returns `accepted`/`partially-accepted`/`rejected` (rejection saves nothing); `measured-value` is reserved; an `athlete-decision-report` is recorded **only as a subjective observation** (no `AthleteDecisionRecord` write). It **detects no `Signal`**, **infers nothing**, and **imports no downstream module or `event-recording`** — the optional `ObservationSetRecorded` is composed only in a neutral harness from a ref-only candidate. **Manual input is source material, never meaning.**

### `reasoning`
[FACT] Implements `Hypothesis` (aggregate root) owning `EvidenceCase` (entity), `EvidenceDirection`, `ClaimConfidence`, `Falsifier`, and the lifecycle (`proposed → supported/weakened/contradicted/falsified/retired/promoted-to-working-knowledge`). Coordinators: `openHypothesis`, `attachSignalAsEvidence`, `transitionHypothesis`.
- **Clarify:** a `Hypothesis` is **not fact** and never reaches a "certain"/"proven" state; **confidence is not certainty** (it is calibrated and defeasible); **an `EvidenceCase` exists only inside a `Hypothesis`** — `createEvidenceCase` is deliberately *not* exported, and a `SignalRejection` is rejected as evidence at runtime and by type.

### `understanding`
[FACT] Implements `UnderstandingProfile` (aggregate, per-dimension), `UnderstandingDimension`, `UnderstandingLevel` (Unknown < Thin < Working < Trusted < Mature), the `ReasoningOutcome` anti-corruption adapter (`reasoningOutcomeFrom`), `SurvivedChallenge`, `Surprise`, `Staleness`, `Fragility`, `UnderstandingAssessment`, and `SafeVoiceCeiling`. **Plus projection freshness (Impl 008):** `ProjectionFreshness`/`Status`, `StalenessReason`, `ProjectionSourceRef`/`Kind`, `ProjectionTrace`, `ProjectionLimitations`, `RefreshTrigger`/`Kind`, `ProjectionRefreshDecision`/`Kind`, `ProjectionRefreshPolicy`, `clampCeilingByFreshness`, `applyFreshness`. Coordinators: `updateUnderstandingFromOutcome`, `produceUnderstandingAssessment` (now `at`-aware), `markUnderstandingStale`.
- **Clarify:** **claim confidence is not understanding** — the adapter deliberately drops `ClaimConfidence` and raw `EvidenceCase`s; **repetition does not promote** — promotion requires survived challenge across ≥2 distinct conditions; **`SafeVoiceCeiling` is not a `VoiceMode`** — it is understanding's own vocabulary for *maximum permitted assertiveness*.
- **Projection freshness (Impl 008):** `UnderstandingAssessment` is a **projection/read model** carrying explicit `freshness` (`current`/`stale`/`partial`/`invalid`/`unknown`), `derivedAt`, and `sourceRefs`. Non-current freshness can only **lower** the ceiling; `invalid`/`unknown` clamp it to `none`. The refresh policy is **pure, selective, conservative**; **refresh = recompute** (new view, old one auditable, never mutated). Freshness reaches `decision-support` **only via the clamped `safeVoiceCeiling`** — no `decision-support` change.

### `decision-support`
[FACT] Implements `DecisionOpportunity`, `DecisionSupportCase` (aggregate root), the five gates (`EvidenceGate`, `UnderstandingGate`, `PurposeGate`, `RiskGate`, `AgencyGate`), `TraceabilityVerification` (`verifyTraceability`), `VoiceSelectionPolicy` (`selectTerminalOutput`), `VoiceMode`, terminal outputs (`DecisionSupport`/`Inquiry`/`Withholding`), `RiskAssessment`, `PurposeContext`, `SupportQuality`, and `AthleteDecisionRef`. Coordinators: `openDecisionSupportCase`, `evaluateDecisionSupportCase`, `recordAthleteDecisionRef`.
- **Clarify:** **voice is gated, not derived** — `VoiceSelectionInputs` carries **no claim-confidence field**, so confidence→voice is unrepresentable; **`Recommendation` is hard to construct** — it requires `confident` ceiling + complete traceability + all gates passing; **`AthleteDecision` is referenced, not owned** — only an `AthleteDecisionRef` field exists, recorded after the fact, and `SupportQuality` reflects gate integrity, not outcome.

### `athlete` *(Purpose — Impl 007 · AthleteDecision — Impl 009)*
[FACT] Implements a thin `Athlete` aggregate root (+ `AthleteId`) owning an **append-only `PurposeHistory`** of immutable `PurposeVersion`s; `Purpose`/`DeclaredPurpose`, `PurposeStatus`, `PurposeSource`, `PurposeChangeReason`; `PurposeVersionRef`; `PurposeChanged` (a derived/returned value, **no event bus**); `PurposeReinterpretationStatus` + result value type (**type only — no engine**); a `RevealedPurposeSignal` placeholder. **Plus the AthleteDecision slice (Impl 009):** `AthleteDecisionId`, `AthleteDecision` (+ athlete-local `AthleteDecisionRef`, `DecisionReportSource`), `DecisionChoice`, `DecisionRationale`, `DecisionContext`, `DecisionOutcomeRef`, `AthleteDecisionRecord` (append-only; `amend`/supersede). Coordinators: `declarePurpose`, `changePurpose`, `recordAthleteDecision`, `amendAthleteDecision`. Imports **only `shared-kernel`**.
- **Clarify (Purpose):** **`Athlete` owns declared context, not inferred truth** — no state/capacity/readiness/fatigue/constraints/path-memory; **purpose changes the future lens, it does not repaint the past** — history is append-only, prior reasoning is never rewritten; **`athlete` reaches no downstream module** — purpose flows to `decision-support` (as `PurposeContext`) and to `understanding` (as selective staleness) only through **neutral harness/application adapters**; **declared ≠ revealed**.
- **Clarify (AthleteDecision, Impl 009):** the decision is **athlete-owned** and **append-only** (corrections amend/supersede, original retained); `DecisionSupportCase` records **only an `AthleteDecisionRef`** (referenced, never owned); a `DecisionChoice` keeps a **modification** as free text (**no binary compliance**), and `divergedFromSupport` is **neutral fact, not a score**; there is **no compliance/obedience/shame/reward field**; `DecisionOutcomeRef` is a **reference only** (no full outcome object); the decision **re-enters as a `SubjectiveObservation`** via a neutral adapter (`athlete` never imports `observation`) — **never** directly as Signal/Evidence/Understanding.

### Persistence (Impl 010) — across modules
[FACT] Each persisted boundary gained an additive `toState()` / `static reconstitute(state)` and a module-owned repository **port** + **in-memory adapter** (in `application/`): `observation/ObservationSetRepository`, `reasoning/HypothesisRepository`, `understanding/UnderstandingProfileRepository`, `decision-support/DecisionSupportCaseRepository`, `athlete/AthleteRepository`, `athlete/AthleteDecisionRecordRepository`.
- **Clarify:** **persistence is a boundary around aggregates, not a driver of the domain** — `reconstitute` **validates invariants and rejects invalid state** (never a raw field bag); the in-memory adapter **stores deep-copied state, not live references**, so loads are independent (mutation isolation); `PurposeHistory` persists **through `Athlete`**; there is **no projection repository** (freshness survival is a test helper); and **no technology is chosen** (no DB/ORM/schema/event-bus/cache/infrastructure).

### `event-recording` *(Impl 011 — append-only event/outcome records · Impl 024 — additive output-out occurrence surface)*
[FACT] Implements a **dependency-neutral** occurrence log: `DomainEventRecord` (+ `DomainEventRecordId`), `DomainEventType` (closed **34-type catalog** — 26 reasoning-core + **8 output-out, Impl 024**) + `DomainEventCategory` (`occurrence`/`outcome`), `TraceabilityEnvelope` (+ `ProjectionFreshnessStatus` label), `EventPayloadRef` (+ `EventArtifactKind`, now including the **5 output-out artifact kinds**), `ProducingModule` (now including **`rendering`/`delivery`**), `CausationRef`, `CorrelationRef`, `EventActor`, `DomainEventRecordLog`; and in `application/`, the `DomainEventRecordRepository` **port** (`append`/`findById`/`all`/`findByCorrelation`) + `InMemoryDomainEventRecordRepository`, **plus the 8 pure provider/rendering/delivery occurrence factories (Impl 024)**. Imports **only `shared-kernel`**.
- **Clarify:** the module records **what happened**, never **what should execute** — a record **is not a command** (appending mutates nothing), **is not an aggregate / projection / source truth**, and **does not replace** the Impl 010 repositories (those answer *what is the aggregate now?*). Payloads are **ref-only** (`kind`/`id`/`role?`/`ownerModule?`) — **copied aggregate state and arbitrary bags are unrepresentable**; the log is **append-only** (corrections are new records; duplicate ids rejected); the in-memory repository **stores copies, not live references** and has **no** update/delete/dispatch/publish/subscribe surface; `toState()`/`reconstitute()` **re-validate** the closed catalog (type↔module/category, required refs, `occurredAt ≤ recordedAt`) and execute nothing on rehydrate. **No domain module imports `event-recording`; the catalog stays out of `shared-kernel`; no event bus / event sourcing / serialization tech exists.**
- **Clarify (output-out surface, Impl 024):** the catalog expansion is **additive and string-literal** (provider events are produced by `rendering`, delivery events by `delivery`; **no `provider` producing module**; `DisplayEligibility` is id-less so it is a ref *role*, not a kind). The **8 factories are pure**: they build a `DomainEventRecord` through the existing `DomainEventRecord.record(...)`, **return** it, and **persist nothing / call no provider·transport·validator·renderer·delivery sink / create no downstream artifact / mutate no domain / emit from nothing automatically** — recording is **explicit application composition only**. `event-recording` referencing `ProviderAttemptRecord`/`RenderedMessageRecord`/… by **string kind is not a cross-module import** (it still imports only `shared-kernel`; rendering/delivery import no `event-recording`). A provider/delivery success event is **never** evidence, recommendation quality, an athlete decision, a retry, or a delivery command.

### `reprojection-harness` *(Impl 012 — neutral check-only recompute-and-compare seam, NOT a module)*
[FACT] Lives under `src/modules/__tests__/reprojection-harness/` as **test-support / coordination**, not a production module: `runReprojection` + `ReprojectionRun`/`Result`/`Finding`/`Mode`/`Target`/`InputSet`, a **pure** event→candidate map, and an `understanding` recompute adapter. It is the neutral cross-module coordinator (like the existing purpose/decision adapters); it imports the modules it coordinates, and **no production module imports it**.
- **Clarify:** the harness **recomputes** derived views *only through the owning module's existing functions* (`produceUnderstandingAssessment`, `applyFreshness`) — it **coordinates, never reasons**; **recalculates** freshness (never promotes it, never raises a ceiling); reads **event records as candidates/context only** (never replayed/executed, never rebuilding an aggregate — empty repos → `event-record-only`/`missing-source`); **reports drift** (never overwrites); and in `check-only` (default and only mode; `refresh-derived`/`mark-stale` reserved and throwing) **mutates no repository, appends no record, and creates no `TerminalOutput`/recommendation/`SupportQuality` rewrite/`Purpose` overwrite/`DomainEventRecord`**. **Repositories remain the source of aggregate state; event records remain occurrence history; reprojection recomputes views and reports findings — none replaces the others.**

### `rendering` *(Impl 014 — deterministic downstream rendering boundary)*
[FACT] Implements `src/modules/rendering/`: `RenderableDomainOutput` (+ module-local `RenderableFreshness`) + `renderableFromTerminalOutput`, `RenderingRequest` (+ closed `SAFE_STYLES`/`SUPPORTED_LOCALES`), `RenderedMessage`/`RenderOutcome`, a closed **12-value `RenderingFailure`** catalog, the `RenderingPolicy` cue vocabularies + predicates, a **mandatory `RenderingValidator`** (`validateDraft`), and a deterministic **fake renderer** (`fakeRender`/`render`). Imports **only `shared-kernel` + read-only `decision-support` types**.
- **Clarify:** rendering is **downstream presentation, never reasoning and never `decision-support`** — it reads a **read-only projection** of a completed `TerminalOutput` and owns **phrasing only** (`decision-support` owns voice + terminal output). The **fake renderer is deterministic** (no provider/model/randomness); **every draft must pass the mandatory validator** (the validator, not the renderer, is the guarantee). Voice may **match or soften, never escalate**; `Inquiry` stays a question; `Withholding` stays a refusal; `Recommendation` preserves conditions/uncertainty/traceability/agency; invented facts/citations, hidden uncertainty/limitations, and unsafe domain language are **rejected** (safe non-render). A `RenderedMessage` is **not** domain authority (`≠ Evidence/Observation/Understanding/AthleteDecision`); rendering **mutates no aggregate, writes no event**, and **no domain module imports `rendering`**. **No real LLM provider / prompt templates / UI / API / external call.**
- **Record/review persistence (Impl 015):** `rendering` also owns an **append-only `RenderedMessageRecord`** (auditable presentation artifact; source-domain-output ref + terminal-output kind + `VoiceMode` + validation flags preserved), an **append-only `RenderReview`** (closed 5-decision / 11-reason catalogs; display-safety only), **derived** current review status + **derived `DisplayEligibility`**, and a **`RenderedMessageRecordRepository` port + in-memory adapter** (deep-copy round-trip, mutation isolation, validated reconstitution). **Persistence is auditability, not authority**: a record is not domain truth; approval changes no domain (voice/traceability/freshness/`SupportQuality`); rejection invalidates nothing; failed attempts are auditable but never display-eligible/approvable; revision/supersession preserve the old record; **`rendering` imports no `event-recording` and emits no event** (a `RenderedMessageRecord`/`RenderReview` may now be **referenced by id** in a ref-only `event-recording` event — Impl 024 — but `rendering` neither creates nor auto-emits one), and there is **no production DB / delivery / UI / API**.
- **Provider adapter seam (Impl 017):** `rendering` also owns a **provider seam** — `ProviderRenderingRequest` (+ the `providerRenderingRequestFrom` construction guard), an untrusted `ProviderDraft`/`ProviderDraftOutcome`, a closed **`ProviderFailure`** catalog (10), a **`ProviderAdapter`** port, a deterministic **`FakeProviderAdapter`**, and a **`requestProviderRendering`** service. It replaces **only** the draft-text step the `FakeRenderer` performs: the provider produces an **untrusted draft** that becomes a `RenderedMessage` **only** by passing the **unchanged mandatory `validateDraft`** (the `rendered` branch is the existing path; a validation failure → `provider-output-failed-validation` + the underlying `RenderingFailure[]`). The request is a **constrained projection** (no raw reasoning / chain-of-thought / mutable handle / override field); an **unsafe request is refused before the call**; **every** failure **degrades to safe non-rendering**. The provider **selects/changes no `VoiceMode`**, **creates no `TerminalOutput`/`Recommendation`/`RenderedMessage`/record**, and **persists/reviews/marks-display-eligible/delivers/emits/mutates nothing**. It imports only its own `rendering` surfaces + read-only `decision-support` *types*; **no module outside `rendering` imports it**; there is **no real SDK/API/network/`process.env`/prompt-templates** and **no `provider`/`llm` top-level module**. **A provider drafts; the validator decides; the domain stays the source of truth.**
- **Provider attempt audit (Impl 018):** `rendering` also owns a **provider-attempt audit** — `ProviderAttemptStatus` (closed; `requested`/`draft-produced` reserved), `ProviderAttemptFailureReason` (= `ProviderFailure | RenderingFailure`, real catalogs reused), a safe `ProviderDraftSummary`, a `ProviderAttemptRecord` (+ State), a **`ProviderAttemptRecordRepository` port + in-memory adapter**, and an observe-only **`auditProviderAttempt`** service. It **observes** a `ProviderRenderOutcome` (it **does not call** the provider/`requestProviderRendering`/`validateDraft`) and records an append-only **safe summary** — status + reasons + refs — with **no raw draft retention** (`rawDraftRetained` literal `false`; reconstitution rejects raw draft/text/content/prompt fields, `rawDraftRetained: true`, unknown keys, and status/flag mismatches). The record is **auditability, not authority**: it is **not** a `ProviderDraft`/source-truth/`Evidence`/`Observation`/`Understanding`/`AthleteDecision`/`DecisionSupport`/`TerminalOutput`/`RenderedMessage`/`RenderedMessageRecord`; it **creates no review/display-eligibility/delivery**, **appends no event**, **triggers no retry/reprojection/reasoning**, and **mutates nothing**; a **validation failure is not domain invalidation**. It imports only its own `rendering` surfaces + read-only `decision-support` *types*; **no module outside `rendering` imports it**; **no `event-recording` import and no auto-emit** (a `ProviderAttemptRecord` may now be **referenced by id** in a ref-only `event-recording` event — Impl 024 — but the audit neither imports `event-recording` nor emits one); and it is **not model evaluation or telemetry**. **The audit remembers what the seam did; the draft never becomes authority.**
- **Real-provider-ready boundary (Impl 019):** `rendering` also owns a **real-provider-*ready*** async path — `ProviderSecretRef` (+ `ProviderCredentialStatus`), a non-secret `ProviderClientConfig`, a structured `ProviderInstruction` (+ `providerInstructionFrom`), `ProviderClientRequest`/`ProviderClientResponse` (+ operational `ProviderClientMetadata`), a closed `ProviderOperationalFailure` (+ `toProviderFailure`), an **async `ProviderClientBoundary`** port, a deterministic **`FakeProviderClient`**, a **`RealProviderAdapter`**, and an async **`requestRealProviderRendering`** service. It **changes only the draft source**: the synchronous Impl 017 seam is **untouched** (Option B); the async path **reuses** the unchanged `providerRenderingRequestFrom` guard + a credential fast-path + the mandatory **`validateDraft`** and returns the existing `ProviderRenderOutcome` (validation failure → `provider-output-failed-validation` + the underlying `RenderingFailure[]`). **Secret refs, never secrets** (status + opaque ref; no raw secret in records/responses/errors; no `process.env`); **structured instruction, not prompts** (derived; no template/arbitrary-prompt/chain-of-thought); **operational failures map down** to the existing `ProviderFailure` (**not expanded**); every failure **degrades to safe non-rendering** with **no automatic retry**. Provider output is **untrusted draft** (only `validateDraft` makes a message); **provider metadata is operational, not evidence**; the Impl 018 raw-free audit observes the outcome by **explicit composition** (**no automatic persistence**); and there is **no review/display-eligibility/delivery/event/domain-mutation**. It imports only its own `rendering` surfaces + read-only `decision-support` *types*; **no module outside `rendering` imports it**; **no real SDK/API/network/`process.env`/prompt-template** and **no `provider`/`llm`/`telemetry`/`evaluation` top-level module**. This is the codebase's **first `async` surface**, isolated here. **Real-provider-*ready*, not real-provider-*integrated*: a real provider changes the draft source, never the authority model.**
- **Concrete-provider adapter shell (Impl 020):** `rendering/application` also owns the **first selected-provider adapter** behind the Impl 019 async `ProviderClientBoundary` — a **`ConcreteProviderClient`** plus pure **`serializeProviderInstruction`** (+ `ConcreteProviderRequestPayload`), **`parseProviderResponse`** (+ `ConcreteProviderResponseShape`), and **`mapProviderError`** (+ `ConcreteProviderErrorKind`/`Shape`). The provider target (**OpenAI**) is recorded at the **doc/decision level (020A) only**; code stays **vendor-neutral** (`concrete-provider-*`, `providerKind: "concrete"`) so **no guard is weakened and no vendor token appears in a guarded provider file**. The client is **disabled by default** (no transport → safe `provider-unavailable`, no work; **no live call path**); a non-`present` credential fails safe before any transport; the only non-default behavior is a **deterministic in-process fixture transport for tests** (not a network call). The serializer projects **only** safe constraints (no arbitrary-prompt/chain-of-thought/secret field; no prompt template/`src/prompts`); the parser returns an **untrusted draft + operational metadata** (empty/malformed → safe operational failures; **no raw payload retained**; **no `RenderedMessage`**); the error mapper maps provider-shaped errors to the existing `ProviderOperationalFailure`, which `toProviderFailure` maps **down** to the existing `ProviderFailure` (**not expanded**; unknown → `provider-unavailable`). A draft becomes a message **only** via the unchanged `requestRealProviderRendering` → **`validateDraft`**; the raw-free audit observes the outcome by explicit composition. It imports only its own `rendering` surfaces + read-only `decision-support` *types*; **no module outside `rendering` imports it**; **no SDK/package dependency** (`package.json`/lockfile unchanged), **no network/`process.env`/raw secret/prompt template**, and **no retry/scheduler/record/review/display/delivery/event/domain side effect**. **A selected-provider *shell*, not live integration.**
- **Opt-in live-provider boundary (Impl 021):** `rendering/application` also owns the **first live-call edge** behind the same async `ProviderClientBoundary` — a **`LiveCallPolicy`** (injected value object; `disabled()`/`enabled({timeoutMs})`; disabled by default; no env inference; no global state), a **`ProviderCredentialResolver`** port (+ opaque `ProviderCredentialToken`) with a deterministic test/composition-only **`StaticProviderCredentialResolver`**, a **`LiveProviderHttpTransport`** (the **only** network-token file — native `fetch` + `AbortSignal.timeout` behind an **injected endpoint**; no hard-coded vendor URL; no retry/persist/validate/secret-in-errors), and a **`LiveProviderClient`** (implements the async `ProviderClientBoundary`; a **sibling** of `ConcreteProviderClient`). It **fails closed before any transport call** when the policy is disabled or the credential is missing/invalid; **reuses** the unchanged `serializeProviderInstruction`/`parseProviderResponse`/`mapProviderError`; **never calls `validateDraft`** (validation stays with `requestRealProviderRendering`); provider output is an **untrusted draft**; failures map onto the existing `ProviderOperationalFailure → ProviderFailure` (**not expanded**); the raw-free audit observes by explicit composition. **No SDK/package dependency** (`package.json`/lockfile unchanged), **no `process.env`/env resolver/raw secret/prompt template**, **no default/CI live call or credential**, and **no retry/scheduler/record/review/display/delivery/event/domain side effect**. The native-network guard exception is **surgical** (one approved file; vendor/SDK/env forbidden everywhere); the sync seam, `FakeProviderAdapter`, `FakeProviderClient`, and `ConcreteProviderClient` are untouched. It imports only its own `rendering` surfaces + read-only `decision-support` *types*; **no module outside `rendering` imports it**. **Live-call-*capable*, not a production rollout.**
- **Injected environment credential resolver (Impl 022):** `rendering/application` also owns an **`EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver`** (+ `EnvironmentCredentialSource`, `EnvironmentResolverConfig`, `CredentialValidationPolicy`) — a **sibling** of `StaticProviderCredentialResolver` on the **unchanged** injected `ProviderCredentialResolver` port. It reads **exactly one explicitly configured key** from an **injected `EnvironmentCredentialSource`** (`Readonly<Record<string, string | undefined>>`) — **no real `process.env`**, **no scan**, **no fallback list**, **no domain-derived key name**. Classification: absent → `missing`; blank/whitespace → `invalid`; control chars/line breaks → `invalid`; too-short → `invalid`; else → `available` with the existing opaque transient `ProviderCredentialToken` (a blank/whitespace key name fails closed → `invalid`). The **raw credential stays transient** — never in failures/outcome/audit/state/metadata/tests; **availability is not live-call enablement** (a disabled `LiveCallPolicy` and a missing/invalid credential each block the transport); it **calls no transport/provider/`validateDraft`**, persists/audits/mutates nothing, and **expands no catalog**. **`process.env` appears nowhere in `src/`** so **no guard exception was needed** (the file is scanned by the Impl 017 `/provider-/` + Impl 021 `/provider-credential/` guards plus a dedicated negative-capability test). It imports only its own `rendering` surfaces (+ `shared-kernel` if needed); **no module outside `rendering` imports it**; the static resolver and live transport are untouched. **An injected *operational* resolver, not a production secret manager.**
- **One-file process-environment source adapter (Impl 023):** `rendering/application` also owns a **`ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter`** (+ `ProcessEnvironmentAccessor`, the `processEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter(keyName?)` factory, `defaultProcessEnvironmentAccessor`, `APPROVED_PROVIDER_CREDENTIAL_KEY`). It **binds the real process environment** to the resolver's injected source shape — it **feeds, does not replace,** `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver`. `toEnvironmentCredentialSource()` reads **exactly one explicitly configured key** (the accessor is called **once**) and returns a source with only that key when present, else an **empty source**; it **classifies nothing** (a blank value passes through; a blank/whitespace key name fails closed to empty). The adapter **requires an injected `ProcessEnvironmentAccessor`** (no implicit default), so tests use a fake and never read the real environment; **`defaultProcessEnvironmentAccessor` is the only direct `process.env` read site in the codebase** (wired only by the production factory; unused by the default suite). The approved key is **neutral** (`AURORA_PROVIDER_CREDENTIAL`). The direct `process.env` token is **sealed to this one file** by a **new repo-wide guard** (no existing guard weakened; the network token stays confined to the Impl 021 transport file). **Availability is not live-call enablement** (disabled policy / missing credential each block the transport); the raw secret never enters errors/outcome/audit/state/metadata/tests; it calls no resolver(unless composed)/live-client/transport/provider/`validateDraft`, persists/audits/logs nothing, expands no catalog, and **adds no dependency**. It imports only its own `rendering` surfaces (+ `shared-kernel` if needed); **no module outside `rendering` imports it**; the resolver (still the classifier), the static resolver, and the live transport are untouched. **A one-file *operational* source adapter, not a production secret manager.**
- **Opt-in live-provider smoke-test boundary helper (Impl 026):** `rendering/application` also owns **`liveProviderSmoke(command, deps)`** (+ the closed `LiveProviderSmokeStatus` / `LIVE_PROVIDER_SMOKE_STATUSES`, `LiveProviderSmokeCommand`, `LiveProviderSmokeDependencies`, `LiveProviderSmokeResult`) — a **pure, fully-injected operational WIRING CHECK**, **not an operator script** (none exists; **no npm script, no `scripts/`**). It exercises **one** live provider call through the **existing** `requestRealProviderRendering(...)` seam (so the **unchanged mandatory `validateDraft`** stays the only path to a `RenderedMessage`), gated by **explicit, ordered, fail-closed checks — opt-in → CI → credential → live policy — each stopping before any provider call**; the **credential is resolved only after the opt-in and CI gates pass**, and the call runs **only** when the credential is available **and** the policy is enabled. It makes **at most one call (no loops, no re-issue)** and returns a **closed, redacted `LiveProviderSmokeResult`** (`rawRetained: false`): a rendered outcome → `passed`, `provider-output-failed-validation` → `validation-failed`, any other `ProviderFailure` → `provider-failed` (closed `providerFailureCode`; timeout/malformed/unavailable folded), an unexpected throw → `unexpected-failure`. The result carries **no rendered-message body, no raw draft/prompt/payload/response, no secret/credential token, no `process.env` value, no chain-of-thought, no metadata bag, no delivery target/body**. It **reads no `process.env`** (opt-in/CI are injected indicators; the credential arrives via the injected `ProviderCredentialResolver`), composes the live client through the **injected `ProviderClientBoundary`**, and imports **no** live HTTP transport / process-env adapter / concrete-provider internals / `delivery` / `event-recording` / `application-orchestration` / upstream-domain module; it carries **no** network/vendor/secret/retry token; **no module outside `rendering` imports it**. It **persists nothing, delivers nothing, records no event, derives no display eligibility for delivery, creates no rendered-message record / review / evidence / athlete decision, and mutates no domain**. The **default suite and CI make no live call and need no credential**; the repo-wide `process.env` one-file guard and the live-provider guard (which catches `live-provider-smoke.ts`) stay green; **AC20 is untouched** (no new module). The **operator entrypoint that reads real env flags is deferred**. **A smoke test proves wiring, not wisdom; smoke success is not evidence and smoke failure is not domain failure.**
- **Provider-neutral managed-secret credential-source boundary (Impl 028):** `rendering/application` also owns a **`ManagedSecretCredentialSource`** class (+ **`ManagedSecretStoreClient`** interface, **`ManagedSecretResolution`** 4-state type, **`ManagedSecretSourceConfig`**, **`ManagedSecretClientScenario`**, **`FakeManagedSecretStoreClient`**) — the async boundary behind which any managed secret store can supply a credential via the **pre-fetch pattern**. `async toEnvironmentCredentialSource(): Promise<EnvironmentCredentialSource>` calls `storeClient.retrieve(secretName)` once, returns `{ [secretName]: value }` on `available` or `{}` on non-`available` paths; the downstream **synchronous `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver` is entirely unchanged** (caller: `await` the source before constructing the resolver). Non-`available` → empty source → resolver classifies as `missing` → **no provider call occurs**. `FakeManagedSecretStoreClient` covers all 4 scenarios deterministically; sentinel `"opaque:test-managed-secret"` is not a real credential. **No cloud SDK, no `process.env` read, no vendor dependency, no network token, no retry primitive, no delivery/event-recording/domain import; no module outside `rendering` imports the new symbols; process-env seal intact; operator script unchanged; package.json/lockfile unchanged; no new module; AC20 untouched.** `secret manager = credential source; ≠ live-call enablement ≠ cloud adapter ≠ production rollout ≠ domain evidence.`
- **Manual operator live-smoke entrypoint (Impl 027):** `rendering/application` also owns a **pure, typechecked support helper** `operator-live-smoke-entrypoint.ts` — `parseOperatorSmokeEnv(env)` (an **injected** env record → `{ optIn, ci }`; opt-in requires the exact `AURORA_LIVE_PROVIDER_SMOKE === "1"`; CI truthy blocks), `syntheticSmokeRenderingRequest()` (bounded, synthetic, **no athlete-sensitive data**), `operatorSmokeOutput(result)` (a **redacted** `OperatorSmokeOutput` projection: `status` + `rawRetained: false` + `wiringOnly` + `sideEffects: "none"` + safe optionals), `operatorSmokeExitCode(status)` (**0** for `passed`/`not-enabled`/`ci-disabled`, **1** otherwise), and the flag-name constants. The helper **reads no `process.env`**, **calls no provider**, and **imports no** live transport / process-env adapter / concrete-provider internals / `delivery` / `event-recording` / `application-orchestration` / upstream-domain — it has **no side effects**. The **executable entrypoint** lives **OUTSIDE `src`** at **`scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs`** (plain ESM; **outside `tsconfig.include`, the default test glob, and both guard scan roots**): it reads the real opt-in/CI/endpoint flags (legitimate outside `src` — no in-`src` token added, the production `process.env` seal intact), resolves the credential **only** through the approved `ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter → EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver` chain, wires `LiveCallPolicy.enabled` + `LiveProviderClient` + `liveProviderHttpTransport` (+ the unchanged serializer/parser/error-mapper inside the client), and **calls `liveProviderSmoke` once** — **duplicating no smoke semantics** and **bypassing neither `liveProviderSmoke` nor `requestRealProviderRendering` nor `validateDraft`**. It prints **one redacted JSON object** and exits per the policy; it is **manual only** (`node scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs`), **not an npm script, not in `npm run check`, not in the default suite, with no CI-live lane**, and **persists/delivers/records/orchestrates/mutates nothing**. `[FACT]` **Node 22 native type-stripping** makes the `.mjs` import the real `.ts` `src` with **no build and no dependency** (027A-verified). The Impl 026 `scripts/` guard was **reconciled (strengthened, not weakened)** to allow **only** the approved `operator-live-smoke.mjs` (no other unapproved script; `package.json` wires none; no operator script dir inside `src`). **No `package.json`/lockfile change, no SDK, no dependency.** **The operator can run the wire; the wire still proves wiring, not wisdom.**

### `delivery` *(Impl 016 — downstream exposure boundary)*
[FACT] Implements `src/modules/delivery/`: `domain/` adds ids (`DeliveryRequestId`/`DeliveryRecordId`), the closed **`DeliveryTarget`** (only `test-sink` supported), the closed **`DeliveryOutcome`** (6; `accepted-for-delivery` reserved), the closed **`DeliveryFailureReason`** (10; `provider-unavailable` excluded, `sink-unavailable` added), `DeliveryRequest`, `DeliveryEligibilityCheck` (+ `primaryFailureReasonFor`), the `DeliverySink` interface + deterministic **`InMemoryTestSink`**, and the auditable `DeliveryRecord` (+ `DeliveryRecordState`); `application/` adds the **`DeliveryRecordRepository` port** + `InMemoryDeliveryRecordRepository` + the **`requestDelivery`** service. Imports **only `shared-kernel` + read-only `rendering`** types/functions.
- **Clarify:** delivery is **downstream exposure, never rendering and never domain** — `rendering` owns display eligibility; delivery only **attempts to expose** an already-eligible `RenderedMessageRecord` and records the attempt. It **verifies** eligibility by calling `displayEligibilityOf(record)` (**never** re-derives it) and calls the **deterministic test sink only** when the record is eligible *and* the target is the supported `test-sink`; not-reviewed/rejected/superseded/failed-render/missing-ref records and unsupported/reserved targets are **blocked** without calling the sink (raw rendering reasons retained, mapped to a closed failure reason). A `DeliveryRecord` is **not** domain authority (`≠ Evidence/Observation/Understanding/DecisionSupport/AthleteDecision`); **delivery success is not evidence**, **delivery failure is not domain invalidation**; delivery **mutates no rendered record/aggregate**, **emits no event**, and **triggers no reasoning/reprojection/retry**. The audit repo uses the Impl 010 pattern (deep-copy round-trip; mutation isolation; validated reconstitution). `delivery` imports **no `event-recording` and emits no event** (a `DeliveryRequest`/`DeliveryRecord` may now be **referenced by id** in a ref-only `event-recording` event — Impl 024 — but `delivery` neither creates nor auto-emits one), **`rendering` does not import `delivery`**, and **no upstream module imports `delivery`**. **No real provider/channel / UI / API / scheduler / retry / event bus / production DB.**

### `application-orchestration` *(Impl 025 — explicit application composition module, NOT a domain capability)*
[FACT] Implements `src/modules/application-orchestration/`: a single public function **`orchestrateRenderDeliver(command, deps): Promise<OrchestrationOutcome>`** (in `application/`), a **closed `OrchestrationOutcome`** (8 kinds: `delivered`/`delivery-failed`/`rendered`/`review-rejected`/`display-ineligible`/`provider-not-rendered`/`recording-failed`/`partial-success`) + `ORCHESTRATION_OUTCOME_KINDS`, a **ref-only `OrchestrationTrace`** + a closed **`OrchestrationStage`** catalog (10 stages) + `ORCHESTRATION_STAGES`, and the explicit input types `ExplicitOrchestrationCommand` (+ `OrchestrationTiming`/`OrchestrationIds`/`OrchestrationReviewInput`/`OrchestrationDeliveryInput`) and `ExplicitOrchestrationDependencies`. Imports **only the public indexes** of `rendering`/`delivery`/`event-recording` (+ `shared-kernel`).
- **Clarify:** this is an **application-composition module, not a domain capability module** — it owns **no domain model, no repository, no persistence of its own**, and introduces **no bounded context**. It **composes the existing public services** in a fixed, explicit order over **injected** collaborators: `requestRealProviderRendering` → (selected) `auditProviderAttempt` + explicit `providerAttemptRepository.save` → `RenderedMessageRecord.fromRenderedMessage` + explicit `renderedMessageRecordRepository.save` → (selected) `renderReview` + `record.appendReview` + explicit save → `displayEligibilityOf` (**derived, never asserted**) → (selected **and** eligible) `deliveryRequest` + `requestDelivery` (**self-persists**) → (selected) the Impl 024 occurrence-event factories + `eventRepository.append`. **Each step is an explicit call; no event or repository write triggers the next step** (the function's control flow does); **delivery is never automatic** (display eligibility is necessary, not sufficient); **failures are safe stops or a non-invalidating `partial-success`, never an automatic retry**. The **persistence asymmetry is respected** — audit/record/review **return** records the orchestrator persists explicitly (no separate review repository: a review is appended to the rendered-message record), `requestDelivery` **self-persists**, the event repo uses **`append`**. The **trace/result carry safe refs only** (string ids / closed enums / safe codes — **no raw draft/prompt/payload/provider-response/secret/env value/message body**). It depends on the `ProviderClientBoundary` **abstraction** through the rendering boundary and imports **no** live HTTP transport / credential-resolver internals / process-env adapter / concrete-provider internals / upstream domain module; **`rendering`/`delivery`/`event-recording` import no `application-orchestration`**, and no module depends on it for core behavior. `validateDraft` (inside `requestRealProviderRendering`) stays the only path to a `RenderedMessage`; **provider success is not evidence**, **delivery success is not an athlete decision**, and **nothing here mutates the domain**. **AC20's `ALLOWED_MODULES` was updated additively** (approved module, not a weakening; the guard still rejects every other unapproved top-level module). **No event bus / queue / scheduler / retry / workflow engine / telemetry / DB; no UI/API; no dependency change.** **Orchestration is explicit composition, never a hidden side effect.**

---

## 4. Structural Guarantees

[FACT] What is **impossible to construct today**, with the defense that makes it so. (These are enforced by module surface design + the negative-capability and boundary tests, not by convention.)

| # | Made impossible | Defense (module / test) |
|---|---|---|
| 1 | Raw `Observation` becoming meaning directly | `Observation` has no meaning field; meaning requires `contextualize` + `SignalDetectionPolicy`; `observation` cannot import `reasoning` (boundary test) |
| 2 | `Signal` becoming `Evidence` without a `Hypothesis` | `createEvidenceCase` not exported; `EvidenceCase` only via `Hypothesis.attachEvidence` (reasoning negative tests) |
| 3 | An `EvidenceCase` existing standalone | same as #2 — no constructor on the public surface |
| 4 | A `Hypothesis` becoming certainty | no "certain/proven" lifecycle state; confidence always calibrated/defeasible (reasoning lifecycle tests) |
| 5 | Understanding promoting from repetition alone | promotion gated on survived challenge across ≥2 distinct conditions in `update-policy` (understanding tests) |
| 6 | Claim confidence mapping to understanding | `reasoningOutcomeFrom` adapter drops `ClaimConfidence` (understanding adapter test) |
| 7 | `SafeVoiceCeiling` becoming a `VoiceMode` | distinct types in distinct modules; `maxVoiceForCeiling` maps ceiling→voice in `decision-support` (negative test) |
| 8 | Claim confidence selecting voice | `VoiceSelectionInputs` has no confidence field (decision-support negative test) |
| 9 | `Recommendation` without complete traceability + confident ceiling | final guard in `VoiceSelectionPolicy`; degrades to Framing otherwise (decision-support + e2e tests) |
| 10 | Risk escalating toward `Recommendation` | `RiskGate` yields only `caution-warning`; policy routes risk to `Warning`, never up (decision-support negative test) |
| 11 | `Inquiry` being a `VoiceMode` | `Inquiry` has no `voice` field; separate output type (decision-support negative test) |
| 12 | `DecisionSupportCase` owning `AthleteDecision` | only an `AthleteDecisionRef`; asserted `undefined` in the e2e proof (gates-and-quality + e2e tests) |
| 13 | Upstream depending on downstream | dependency-boundary tests per module + the e2e structural guard that no production file imports all four surfaces |
| 14 | `athlete` reaching a downstream module | `athlete` imports only `shared-kernel`; `athlete-boundary` test asserts no `observation`/`reasoning`/`understanding`/`decision-support` import (Impl 007) |
| 15 | Purpose history being overwritten / a purpose change rewriting the past | `PurposeHistory` append-only; `Athlete` immutable-by-operation; `PurposeChanged` carries no hypothesis mutation; never mutates `UnderstandingProfile` (Impl 007 tests) |
| 16 | Revealed behavior becoming declared purpose / inferred purpose | only an athlete-sourced declaration creates a version; runtime guard rejects non-purpose/non-athlete-sourced values; `RevealedPurposeSignal` has no change path (Impl 007 declared-vs-revealed test) |
| 17 | A non-current projection raising the voice | freshness only clamps the ceiling down; `clampCeilingByFreshness` never raises; `invalid`/`unknown` → `none` (Impl 008 freshness tests) |
| 18 | A stale/invalid projection earning a `Recommendation` | `Recommendation` needs `confident`; non-current freshness caps below it (→ `Withholding` for invalid/unknown); integration test |
| 19 | Refresh mutating an old projection / inventing traceability | `applyFreshness` returns a new frozen assessment; the old stays auditable; source refs derive only from the real trace (Impl 008 tests) |
| 20 | A trigger globally staling unrelated projections | `projectionRefreshPolicy` is selective by source-ref intersection; non-matching → `keep-current` (Impl 008 refresh-policy tests) |
| 21 | `DecisionSupportCase` owning the athlete's decision | the case holds only an `AthleteDecisionRef`; the `AthleteDecision` lives in `athlete`; integration test asserts no decision object on the case (Impl 009) |
| 22 | An `AthleteDecision` becoming `Evidence`/`Understanding` directly | the only re-entry is `decisionAsObservation` → `SubjectiveObservation`; no decision→Evidence/Understanding adapter exists; the ladder is intact (Impl 009 tests) |
| 23 | Obedience/compliance scoring of a decision | `AthleteDecision` carries no compliance/obedience/noncompliance/shame/reward field; `divergedFromSupport` is neutral; following ≠ success, not-following ≠ failure (Impl 009 negative tests) |
| 24 | An outcome retroactively grading the support | `DecisionOutcomeRef` is separate; recording a (divergent) decision leaves `SupportQuality` unchanged — integrity-at-the-time (Impl 009 test) |
| 25 | Reconstituting an invalid persisted object | `reconstitute` validates and **throws** on invalid state (no falsifier, empty occasion, missing athleteRef, out-of-order purpose history, orphan amendment); never a raw field bag (Impl 010 negative tests) |
| 26 | A repository handing out a live internal reference | adapters store deep-copied `toState()` and load via `reconstitute` (deep-copied); two finds are independent; mutating a load never touches the store (Impl 010 mutation-isolation tests) |
| 27 | Persistence silently dropping history/traceability/freshness | round-trip preserves append-only history, supersession, traceability refs, and (via helper) projection freshness (Impl 010 round-trip tests) |
| 28 | A production persistence layer / infrastructure leaking in | no `src/infrastructure`, no `persistence`/`repositories` module, no DB/ORM/event-bus token in production code (Impl 010 persistence-boundary guard) |
| 29 | An event record carrying copied aggregate state / an arbitrary payload bag | `EventPayloadRef` has only `kind`/`id`/`role?`/`ownerModule?`; no `payload`/`data`/`metadata: unknown`; reconstitution rejects extra keys (Impl 011 ref-only tests) |
| 30 | An event record acting as a command / executing or mutating downstream | a `DomainEventRecord` has no behavior beyond being recorded; appending mutates nothing; causation/correlation are lineage/grouping, not triggers (Impl 011 negative tests) |
| 31 | Overwriting/deleting event history; an event record bypassing the closed catalog | `DomainEventRecordLog`/repository are append-only (duplicate ids rejected; no update/delete); `record()`/`reconstitute()` validate type↔module/category + required refs against the closed catalog (Impl 011 append-only + validation tests) |
| 32 | `event-recording` coupling to domain modules / the kernel becoming event-aware / a bus or event sourcing | `event-recording` imports only `shared-kernel`; no domain module imports it; the catalog lives outside `shared-kernel`; no bus/publish/subscribe/handler/event-sourcing/serialization token or dir exists (Impl 011 boundary + negative-capability guards) |
| 33 | A reprojection run mutating an aggregate / calling a write method | `check-only` is the only implemented mode; the harness calls only reads; before/after deep-equality snapshot is unchanged and a throwing `save` is never reached (Impl 012 mutation-safety tests) |
| 34 | Rebuilding aggregate state from the event log / replaying events as commands | an event referencing an absent aggregate yields `event-record-only`/`missing-source`, never synthesized state; candidate detection is a pure events→targets map that executes nothing (Impl 012 empty-repo + candidate tests) |
| 35 | A reprojection run promoting freshness / strengthening voice / overwriting a stored view / emitting an output | recompute may only re-derive the same-or-more-cautious view (stale→ceiling lowered, never raised); drift is reported (`changed`), never overwritten; no `TerminalOutput`/`SupportQuality` rewrite/`Purpose` overwrite/`DomainEventRecord` is produced (Impl 012 drift + ceiling + negative tests) |
| 36 | A production `reprojection` module / scheduler / event sourcing / projection repository leaking in | the harness lives under `__tests__/`; structural guard asserts no `src/modules/{reprojection,projection,scheduler,event-sourcing}` and no scheduler/bus/DB/serialization token; no domain module imports the harness (Impl 012 structural guards) |
| 37 | Manual input becoming meaning / a `Signal` / inferred state at ingestion | the adapter's only output is an `ObservationSet` built via `recordObservationSet`; it never calls `detectSignals`; subjective words are verbatim; no readiness/fatigue/impact/capacity field; negative tests assert no Signal/Evidence/Hypothesis/Understanding/DecisionSupport (Impl 013) |
| 38 | The adapter inventing a value / silently interpreting ambiguity / losing rejected input | missing data is an explicit `missing-data` observation (never invented); ambiguity → a limitation or rejection; rejection saves nothing (a throwing `save` is never reached) (Impl 013 partial/rejection tests) |
| 39 | `observation` coupling to `event-recording` or a downstream module / the adapter mutating athlete records | the adapter imports only `observation` + `shared-kernel`; structural guard asserts `observation` imports no `event-recording`/`reasoning`/`understanding`/`decision-support`/`athlete`; an athlete-decision report is observation-only (no `AthleteDecisionRecord` write); the optional `ObservationSetRecorded` is harness-composed, ref-only (Impl 013 boundary + neutral-integration tests) |
| 40 | A renderer selecting/escalating voice or creating a `TerminalOutput`/`Recommendation` | rendering reads a read-only projection; voice may only match/soften; the validator rejects recommendation language unless the domain voice is `Recommendation` (`voice-escalation`/`recommendation-created-by-renderer`); a style request (`"be decisive"`) is not a `SAFE_STYLE` → `unsupported-style-request` (Impl 014 validator tests) |
| 41 | Generated text hiding uncertainty / inventing a fact or citation / becoming domain authority | the mandatory validator rejects `uncertainty-hidden`/`limitation-hidden`/`invented-fact`/`missing-traceability`; `Inquiry` stays a question, `Withholding` stays a refusal; a `RenderedMessage` carries no aggregate-write path and is not re-ingested as `Evidence`/`Observation`/`Understanding`/`AthleteDecision` (Impl 014 validator + negative tests) |
| 42 | A real LLM provider / `rendering` coupling / domain mutation by rendering | `rendering` imports only `shared-kernel` + read-only `decision-support` *types*; no domain module imports it; structural guard asserts no `src/{llm,api,ui,infrastructure}` / `src/modules/{llm,openai,provider}` and no provider/network token; the fake renderer is deterministic; rendering mutates/emits nothing (Impl 014 structural + neutral tests) |
| 43 | A persisted/approved rendered message becoming domain authority | a `RenderedMessageRecord` carries no domain field/write handle; approval changes no `VoiceMode`/traceability/freshness/`SupportQuality`; rejection invalidates nothing; the record is not usable as `Evidence`/`Observation`/`Understanding`/`DecisionSupport`/`AthleteDecision` (Impl 015 record + negative tests) |
| 44 | A failed render displayed / review history overwritten / old record lost | a failed attempt is never display-eligible and cannot be approved; review history is append-only with derived status; revision/supersession preserve the old (immutable) record; display eligibility is derived, never stored authority, never delivery (Impl 015 record/eligibility tests) |
| 45 | Rendered-message persistence emitting an event / leaking to a DB or delivery | the record repo is in-memory (port + adapter; deep-copy mutation isolation; validated reconstitution); **`rendering` imports no `event-recording` and auto-emits nothing** — even though `event-recording`'s catalog now carries ref-only `RenderedMessageRecorded`/`RenderReviewRecorded` types (Impl 024), `rendering` neither imports the module nor emits a record; structural guard asserts no DB/delivery/provider/UI/API (Impl 015 persistence + negative-capability tests, reconciled for the Impl 024 catalog) |
| 46 | Delivering a non-display-eligible record / calling the sink on a blocked request | `requestDelivery` gates on `displayEligibilityOf(record)`; not-reviewed/rejected/superseded/failed-render/missing-ref records and unsupported/reserved targets yield `blocked-not-eligible`/`not-attempted` and the sink is provably never called (Impl 016 boundary tests assert `sink.delivered.length === 0`) |
| 47 | Delivery re-deriving eligibility / success validating or failure invalidating the domain | delivery reuses rendering's `displayEligibilityOf` and only maps its raw reasons (no parallel rule set); delivery success/failure/cancellation leave the rendered record and domain output byte-for-byte unchanged; a `DeliveryRecord`/`DeliveryOutcome` carries no domain field and is not usable as `Evidence`/`Observation`/`Understanding`/`AthleteDecision`/`SupportQuality` (Impl 016 no-mutation + negative tests) |
| 48 | Delivery emitting an event / a real provider/channel / `delivery` coupling / upstream importing `delivery` | `delivery` imports only `shared-kernel` + read-only `rendering`; the repo-named files import only own module + `shared-kernel`; structural guard asserts no `event-recording` import, no `Delivery*` event-catalog entry, no `src/{api,ui,infrastructure}` / `src/modules/{provider,channel,notification,scheduler,event-bus,llm}`; `rendering` does not import `delivery` and no upstream module does (Impl 016 boundary + negative-capability tests) |
