| 49 | A provider draft becoming a `RenderedMessage` without passing the validator / the provider returning a message directly | `requestProviderRendering` only builds a `RenderedMessage` via `validateDraft`; the `ProviderAdapter` port returns `ProviderDraftOutcome` (draft/failure), never a message; a `ProviderDraft` has only `text`/`providerKind`/`warnings` (no preservation flags it sets itself) (Impl 017 service + adapter-boundary tests) |
| 50 | A provider draft escalating voice / inventing a fact / hiding uncertainty/limitations / answering an inquiry / advising a withholding | each unsafe fake scenario is refused by the **unchanged** `validateDraft` (`voice-escalation`/`invented-fact`/`uncertainty-hidden`/`limitation-hidden`/`inquiry-rendered-as-answer`/`withholding-rendered-as-advice`), surfaced as `provider-output-failed-validation`; an unsafe request is refused before the call; every failure degrades to safe non-rendering (Impl 017 service tests) |
| 51 | A real provider SDK/network / prompt-as-code / `provider` module / provider-seam coupling or side effect | provider files import only own `rendering` surfaces + read-only `decision-support` *types*; structural guard asserts no `openai`/`anthropic`/`axios`/`node:http(s)`/`fetch(`/`http(s)://`/`process.env` token, no `src/{providers,prompts,api,ui,infrastructure}` / `src/modules/{provider,llm,openai,anthropic,model}`; provider request exposes no raw reasoning/chain-of-thought/handle; the seam persists/reviews/delivers/emits/mutates nothing, and no module outside `rendering` imports it (Impl 017 negative-capability tests) |
| 52 | A provider-attempt audit retaining a raw draft / unsafe text / prompt / chain-of-thought | `ProviderDraftSummary` has no `draft`/`text`/`content`/`raw`/`excerpt`/`prompt` field; `rawDraftRetained` is the literal `false`; `reconstitute` rejects `rawDraftRetained: true` and any smuggled raw-content/payload-bag key; content tests assert no raw draft text in the record state (Impl 018 record + negative tests) |
| 53 | A provider-attempt audit calling the provider/validator, becoming authority, or firing a downstream effect | `auditProviderAttempt` is a pure mapping of an observed `ProviderRenderOutcome` — structural guard asserts it does not call `requestProviderRendering`/`ProviderAdapter.draft`/`validateDraft`; the record is not `Evidence`/`Observation`/`Understanding`/`AthleteDecision`/`DecisionSupport`/`RenderedMessage`/`RenderedMessageRecord`, creates no review/display/delivery, appends no event, and a validation failure does not invalidate the domain (Impl 018 audit + negative tests) |
| 54 | The audit auto-emitting an event / a `provider-audit`/`telemetry`/`evaluation` module / audit coupling or upstream import | the audit imports only own `rendering` surfaces + read-only `decision-support` *types*; structural guard asserts **no `event-recording` import** and **no auto-emit**, no `src/modules/{provider-audit,telemetry,evaluation,provider,llm,…}`, and no module outside `rendering` imports the audit (the rendering-internal `auditProviderAttempt` / audit-repository symbols stay forbidden outside `rendering`). The `event-recording` catalog now carries a ref-only `ProviderAttemptRecorded` event type (Impl 024), but the audit neither imports the module nor emits one; reasons reuse the real `ProviderFailure` + `RenderingFailure` catalogs (no invented parallel catalog) (Impl 018 boundary + negative-capability tests, reconciled for the Impl 024 catalog) |
| 55 | A real-provider draft bypassing the validator / the real-ready path changing the sync seam | `requestRealProviderRendering` reuses `providerRenderingRequestFrom` + the unchanged `validateDraft` and returns the existing `ProviderRenderOutcome`; the `RealProviderAdapter` returns only a `ProviderDraftOutcome` (never a message); a structural test asserts the synchronous `ProviderAdapter` port stays sync (no `Promise`) and the Impl 017 seam/tests are unchanged (Impl 019 boundary + sync-seam tests) |
| 56 | A real provider SDK/network/secret/prompt leaking in / a raw secret persisted-logged-errored | real-provider files import only own `rendering` surfaces + read-only `decision-support` *types*; structural guard asserts no `openai`/`anthropic`/`axios`/`node:http(s)`/`fetch(`/`process.env` token, no `src/{providers,prompts,…}` / `src/modules/{provider,llm,telemetry,evaluation,…}`; `ProviderSecretRef` is a status + opaque ref (no field for a raw secret); a returned outcome leaks no `secret`/`apikey`/`credential`/ref (Impl 019 negative-capability tests) |
| 57 | A real provider failure retrying/escalating / mapping that expands `ProviderFailure` / metadata becoming evidence | `ProviderOperationalFailure` maps **down** to the existing closed `ProviderFailure` (`PROVIDER_FAILURES.length === 10`, not expanded); the client is called at most once (no automatic retry); a non-`present` credential fails before any client call; provider metadata is operational (the outcome surfaces no `metadata`/`latency`/`finishReason` as a domain field) (Impl 019 failure-mapping + boundary tests) |
| 58 | A concrete provider being used without an explicit selection / a live call running by default / a vendor token leaking into a guarded provider file | the provider target is recorded **doc-level** in 020A (a selection test asserts the decision is explicit); `ConcreteProviderClient` is **disabled by default** (no transport → safe `provider-unavailable`, no I/O — there is no live-call code); the negative-capability guard asserts no `openai`/`anthropic`/`axios`/`node:http(s)`/`fetch(`/`http(s)://`/`process.env` token in the `concrete-provider-*` files and code stays vendor-neutral (Impl 020 selection + negative-capability tests) |
| 59 | The concrete serializer carrying an arbitrary prompt/chain-of-thought / the parser retaining a raw payload or creating a message / provider metadata becoming evidence | `serializeProviderInstruction` projects **only** safe constraints (the payload has no prompt/system/chainOfThought/secret field — a key-set test asserts it); `parseProviderResponse` returns an **untrusted draft + operational metadata only** (empty/malformed → safe failures; content tests assert no raw payload survives; it never builds a `RenderedMessage`); a draft becomes a message only via the unchanged `validateDraft` (Impl 020 serialization + parsing tests) |
| 60 | The concrete error mapper expanding the failure catalog / a missing/unknown error not failing safe / an SDK dependency leaking in | `mapProviderError` maps provider-shaped errors to the existing `ProviderOperationalFailure`, which `toProviderFailure` maps **down** to the existing `ProviderFailure` (**not expanded**); missing/invalid credential and unknown errors fail safe (→ `provider-unavailable`) leaking no payload/secret; a package guard asserts **no runtime dependency** and devDeps remain `typescript` + `@types/node` (Impl 020 error-mapping + package-guard tests) |
| 61 | A live call running by default / a disabled-or-uncredentialed call reaching the network / the default suite or CI making a live call | `LiveCallPolicy.disabled()` is the default; `LiveProviderClient` **fails closed before any transport call** when the policy is disabled or the credential is missing/invalid — a spy transport proves it is never invoked; the default suite drives only a fake in-process transport and requires no credential (Impl 021 live-call-gate tests) |
| 62 | A native network token / SDK dependency / env read / vendor token leaking past the surgical exception | the network token (`fetch(`/`https?://`/`node:http(s)`) is allowed in **exactly one** approved file (`live-provider-http-transport.ts`) — the Impl 014 + Impl 017 guards assert it is the *only* network file and forbid `process.env`/`openai`/`anthropic`/`axios` **everywhere**, including that file; a package guard asserts **no runtime dependency** (Impl 021 negative-capability + rendering/provider guards) |
| 63 | A live draft bypassing the validator / a transport failure expanding the catalog or invalidating the domain / metadata becoming evidence | `LiveProviderClient` returns only a `ProviderClientResponse` and **never calls `validateDraft`** — a draft becomes a message only via the unchanged `requestRealProviderRendering` → `validateDraft`; transport conditions map onto the existing `ProviderOperationalFailure → ProviderFailure` (**not expanded**; unknown → safe `provider-unavailable`); the outcome surfaces no operational metadata as a domain field and leaks no credential (Impl 021 gate + failure-mapping tests) |
| 64 | A credential resolver reading the real environment / scanning / deriving a key from domain data / leaking a raw secret | `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver` reads **one explicitly configured key** from an **injected** `EnvironmentCredentialSource` — `process.env` appears **nowhere** in `src/` (a grep-style guard + the Impl 017 `/provider-/` and Impl 021 `/provider-credential/` scans forbid the token, no exception); failures carry no token and the raw secret never appears in outcome/audit/state (Impl 022 resolver + negative-capability tests) |
| 65 | Credential availability enabling a live call by itself / a credential failure invalidating the domain / the resolver firing a side effect | even with an `available` credential, a `LiveCallPolicy.disabled()` still blocks the transport and a missing/invalid credential blocks it too (a spy transport is never called); the resolver calls no transport/provider/`validateDraft`, creates no record/review/display/delivery/event, mutates nothing, and adds no package dependency (Impl 022 integration + package-guard tests) |
| 66 | The `process.env` token leaking beyond one approved file / the real environment being read in tests/CI / the adapter scanning the environment | a **new repo-wide guard** scans all production `src/` files and asserts the `process.env` token appears in **exactly** `process-environment-credential-source-adapter.ts` (positive `deepEqual`); the adapter **requires an injected accessor** (no implicit default), so the default suite uses a fake and reads no real environment; it reads only the one configured key (called once), with no scan/fallback/domain-derived name (Impl 023 negative-capability + adapter tests) |
| 67 | The process-env adapter classifying a credential / enabling a live call / firing a side effect | the adapter only **produces an `EnvironmentCredentialSource`** (it never classifies — `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver` does); credential availability does not enable a live call (a disabled policy / missing credential each block the transport — spy never called); the adapter calls no resolver(unless composed)/live-client/transport/provider/`validateDraft`, persists/audits/logs nothing, leaks no raw secret to outcome/audit, expands no catalog, and adds no dependency (Impl 023 integration + redaction + package-guard tests) |
| 68 | A provider/rendering/delivery event factory persisting, calling a collaborator, or firing a side effect | the 8 factories build a record through `DomainEventRecord.record(...)` and **return** it — a source scan asserts the factory file calls no `validateDraft`/provider seam/`LiveProviderClient`/`DeliverySink`/`.save`/`.append`/`fetch`; they create no rendered-message record/review/delivery record/provider attempt and mutate no domain (Impl 024 negative-capability + behavior tests) |
| 69 | A provider/rendering/delivery event carrying copied state / raw draft / secret / env value | every ref carries only the allowed ref-only keys (`kind`/`id`/`role?`/`ownerModule?`); a serialized-state scan over all 8 events asserts no `bearer`/`authorization`/`process.env`/`apikey`/`secret`/`prompt`/`draft` marker; `DisplayEligibility` is id-less so it is a ref *role*, never a kind (Impl 024 ref-only + leak-scan tests) |
| 70 | `event-recording` coupling to rendering/delivery/provider, or those paths auto-emitting events | the factory file imports only `event-recording` domain + `shared-kernel` (an import scan forbids any rendering/delivery/provider path); the catalog references artifacts by **string kind**, never by import; rendering/delivery/provider import no `event-recording` and emit nothing automatically; no `src/modules/{event-bus,queue,scheduler,telemetry,evaluation,provider}` / `api` / `db` exists and devDeps stay `typescript` + `@types/node` (Impl 024 import-boundary + structural + package-guard tests) |
| 71 | The orchestration module owning a domain model / a repository / persistence of its own | `application-orchestration/` has **no `domain/` directory** and defines **no repository class**; every side-effecting collaborator (provider client, repositories, sink, event repo) is **injected** via `ExplicitOrchestrationDependencies`; the result/trace are the only outputs and carry no aggregate (Impl 025 application-only structural tests) |
| 72 | An event record / repository save / display eligibility *triggering* the next step, or a delivery failure retrying | every step is an explicit call in `orchestrateRenderDeliver`'s control flow — the audit-failure / record-failure / review-rejection / display-ineligibility / non-rendered-provider cases each **stop before delivery**; delivery runs **only** when explicitly selected *and* eligible (eligibility is necessary, not sufficient); a delivery failure returns `delivery-failed` with **no retry**; an event-append failure returns **non-invalidating `partial-success`** (the domain steps stand) (Impl 025 behavior tests: audit-failure-before-delivery, record-failure-before-review, review-rejection, display-ineligible, delivery-failure-no-retry, event-failure-partial) |
| 73 | The orchestration trace/result carrying raw content, or the module importing live transport / credential resolver / process-env / concrete provider / an event-bus-scheduler-retry-workflow module | the trace is **ref-only** (every field a string id / closed enum / string[]); a serialized-result+events scan asserts no `bearer`/`authorization`/`apikey`/`secret`/`process.env`/message-body marker; an import scan asserts orchestration imports only the **public indexes** of rendering/delivery/event-recording (+ `shared-kernel`) and references no live-transport/credential-resolver/process-env/concrete-provider internal; a structural guard asserts no `src/modules/{workflow,event-bus,queue,scheduler,retry,telemetry,evaluation,provider}` / `api` / `db` and devDeps stay `typescript` + `@types/node`; rendering/delivery/event-recording import no `application-orchestration` (Impl 025 ref-only + leak-scan + import-boundary + structural + package-guard tests) |
| 74 | The live-provider smoke helper running in the default suite / CI, or reaching a provider call without explicit opt-in + CI-clear + a valid credential + an enabled policy | `liveProviderSmoke` runs **only** the explicit ordered gates first — absent opt-in → `not-enabled`, CI indicator → `ci-disabled`, resolver `missing`/`invalid` → `credential-*`, disabled policy → `live-policy-disabled` — **each before any provider call** (a spy client proves `calls === 0`); the **credential is resolved only after opt-in + CI pass** (a throwing resolver is never reached on those paths); the default suite drives it with **fakes only** (no live network, no real env, no CI credential) (Impl 026 gate-ordering + stop-before-call tests) |
| 75 | The smoke helper making more than one provider call / looping / re-issuing, or accepting an unvalidated draft | the helper makes **exactly one** call through the unchanged `requestRealProviderRendering` (spy proves `calls === 1`) with **no loop/no re-issue**; a draft becomes `passed` **only** via the mandatory `validateDraft` (a failing draft → `validation-failed`, never accepted); other provider failures → `provider-failed` + a closed code; an unexpected throw → `unexpected-failure` (Impl 026 one-call + validation-gate tests) |
| 76 | The smoke result leaking raw content, or the helper importing transport/adapter/delivery/event/orchestration internals, persisting, delivering, recording, or mutating | the result is **closed + redacted** (`rawRetained: false`; a serialized-result scan asserts no rendered body / raw draft / prompt / payload / response / secret / credential token / `process.env` value / metadata bag); an import scan asserts the helper imports **no** live HTTP transport / process-env adapter / concrete-provider internal / `delivery` / `event-recording` / `application-orchestration` / upstream-domain module and carries no network/vendor/secret/retry token; it is imported by no module outside `rendering`; it persists/delivers/records/mutates nothing; the repo-wide `process.env` one-file guard + the live-provider guard stay green and **AC20 is untouched** (Impl 026 redaction + import-boundary + structural + package-guard tests) |
| 77 | The operator entrypoint running in the default suite / `npm run check` / CI, or being wired as an npm script | `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs` is **outside `src`** and **outside the test glob** (`src/**/*.test.ts`) — never auto-run; a structural test asserts **no `package.json` script invokes it**; the reconciled `scripts/` guard asserts `scripts/` contains **only** the approved entrypoint; the default suite is fakes-only and makes **no live call** (Impl 027 structural + reconciled-`scripts/`-guard + package-guard tests) |
| 78 | The operator entrypoint duplicating smoke semantics, bypassing the validator, or leaking raw content | the pure `src` helper holds only parse/synthetic-request/redacted-projection/exit-code logic and **reads no `process.env`** (assembled-token scan); the script **references `liveProviderSmoke`** and the approved credential chain and contains **no retry/loop/scheduler construct** and **no env dump** (`JSON.stringify(process.env)` forbidden); the redacted output carries no rendered body / raw draft / payload / response / secret / env value (Impl 027 helper-purity + script-structural + redaction tests) |
| 79 | The operator entrypoint adding a second in-`src` `process.env` site, a dependency, or a side effect | the script reads operator flags **outside `src`** and resolves the credential **only** through the approved adapter; the repo-wide guard still finds the `process.env` token in **exactly** `process-environment-credential-source-adapter.ts`; the package guard asserts `dependencies` empty + devDeps `typescript`+`@types/node`; the helper imports no `delivery`/`event-recording`/`application-orchestration`/transport/process-env-adapter/concrete-provider; it persists/delivers/records/mutates nothing (Impl 027 process-env-seal + package + import-boundary tests) |

---

## 5. End-to-End Reflection Proof (Implementation 006)

[FACT] The integration test (`src/modules/__tests__/end-to-end-responsible-reflection.test.ts`) runs a synthetic scenario ("I felt unusually heavy": an elevated HR measurement + a subjective report + a missing power datum) through all four modules and asserts the terminal output is `DecisionSupport` with `VoiceMode = Reflection`.

[FACT] **Why the first full output is `Reflection` — by the modules' own logic, not by force:**
1. A single **`supported`** outcome is first contact: `applyOutcome` sets `level = higherOf("Unknown","Working") = Working`; with one distinct condition (`< 2`) it does not reach `Trusted`/`Mature`.
2. `deriveSafeVoiceCeiling(Working, low fragility, fresh)` = **`tentative`**.
3. `maxVoiceForCeiling("tentative")` = **`Reflection`**.
4. **Complete traceability is not enough for Recommendation** — the Recommendation guard also requires a `confident` ceiling.
5. **Clean gates do not override the understanding ceiling** — all five gates pass, yet the ceiling still caps the voice at Reflection.

[FACT] The proof also asserts the chain's honesty: the quality limitation survives as an auditable `SignalRejection`; traceability resolves back to the `ObservationSet`; agency is preserved; and no `AthleteDecision` is owned.

> [ASSUMPTION] **Aurora can complete the reasoning chain and still refuse to overreach.**

---

## 6. What Does Not Exist Yet

[FACT] Aurora does **not** yet have, and this is by design at this stage:

| Absent | Intentional? | Note |
|---|---|---|
| **Full** `athlete` aggregate | **Intentional** | A thin **Purpose-first** `athlete` module now exists (Impl 007); state/capacity/constraints/path-memory/identity-detail/reports are still absent. |
| Real `Purpose` source | **Implemented (Impl 007)** | Now a real, athlete-owned, versioned, append-only source; reaches `decision-support` as `PurposeContext` via a neutral adapter. The decision-support `PurposeContext` *placeholder* is **partly retired** (§7). |
| Real `Constraints` source | **Intentional** | Belongs to a future `athlete` slice (not in the Purpose-first slice). |
| Inferred athlete state / capacity / readiness / fatigue | **Intentional** | Never implemented; `athlete` owns the *given*, never the *inferred*. |
| Real `RiskAssessment` source | **Intentional** | Provided as input placeholder; no diagnostic engine. |
| **Manual input boundary (real "data in")** | **Implemented (Impl 013)** | An `observation`-owned Manual Input Adapter records manual input faithfully as an `ObservationSet` (provenance/source/quality preserved; verbatim words; explicit missing data; rejection/partial outcomes), persisted via the repository port — no interpretation. |
| UI / API / external ingestion entrypoint | **Intentional** | The adapter is an in-process boundary; how input is *collected* (UI) or *submitted* (API), auth, and external/FIT/wearable import remain future. |
| Garmin/FIT importer | **Intentional** | First real input is the **manual adapter** (Impl 013); device/FIT adapters are a later spec, behind the same `ObservationSet` entry point. |
| **Repository ports + in-memory persistence** | **Implemented (Impl 010)** | Validated `toState()`/`reconstitute()` + ports + in-memory adapters for the six boundaries; round-trip preserves invariants/traceability/freshness/history. |
| Production DB / ORM / schema / migrations | **Intentional** | Persistence is **ports + in-memory only**; no technology chosen. The domain's `toState()` drives the (future) store, never the reverse. |
| Cache | **Intentional** | Projections recompute; no cache layer. |
| Projection **freshness** on `UnderstandingAssessment` | **Implemented (Impl 008)** | Explicit `current`/`stale`/`partial`/`invalid`/`unknown` + `derivedAt` + source refs; non-current only lowers the voice (invalid/unknown → ceiling `none`), via the existing ceiling. |
| Generic projection **engine** / top-level `projection` module | **Intentional** | Freshness is local to `understanding` for the one concrete projection; a shared kernel/engine waits for a second projection (`ImpactAssessment`). |
| `ImpactAssessment` (second projection) | **Intentional** | Not introduced; Spec 008 governs *how any projection behaves*, not which exist. |
| **Domain event/outcome records + traceability envelope** | **Implemented (Impl 011)** | The `event-recording` module records *what happened* — append-only, ref-only `DomainEventRecord` (occurrence/outcome) over a closed catalog, with a `TraceabilityEnvelope` + in-memory log/repository. Complements aggregate repositories; does not replace them. |
| Event bus / publish-subscribe / handlers / async delivery | **Intentional** | Records are stored, never delivered or executed. `PurposeChanged`/refresh triggers and event records are values, not bus messages; there is no runtime bus, subscriber, or handler. |
| Event sourcing / production event store / serialization format | **Intentional** | The log records occurrences; aggregates rebuild via `reconstitute`, not by replaying the log. No event-sourcing rebuild path, production store, or serialization tech is chosen. |
| **Reprojection (recompute-and-compare)** | **Implemented (Impl 012)** | A **neutral, check-only** harness (`__tests__/reprojection-harness/`, **not a production module**) recomputes `UnderstandingAssessment`, recalculates freshness, detects candidates from event records, and reports drift/findings — mutating nothing. |
| Production `reprojection` module / scheduler / projection repository / production service | **Intentional** | Reprojection is proven as a check-only harness; a production recompute *service*, a scheduler/background refresh, a projection store, and an orchestration layer are deferred (each behind the same contracts when specified). |
| UI | **Intentional** | No rendering; outputs are domain values, not copy. |
| API | **Intentional** | No external entrypoint boundary specified yet. |
| **Rendering boundary (output-out)** | **Implemented (Impl 014)** | A deterministic `rendering` module turns a domain-approved `TerminalOutput` into human-facing text via a fake renderer + mandatory validator — voice/uncertainty/limitations/freshness/traceability/agency preserved; generated text is presentation, not authority. |
| **Provider adapter seam (output-out)** | **Implemented (Impl 017)** | Inside `rendering`: a deterministic **fake provider** drafts text behind the **unchanged mandatory `validateDraft`**; an untrusted draft becomes a `RenderedMessage` only on validation; failures degrade to safe non-rendering — the validator, not the provider, is the authority. |
| **Real-provider-ready boundary (output-out)** | **Implemented (Impl 019)** | Inside `rendering`: an **additive async** `ProviderClientBoundary` (deterministic `FakeProviderClient`) makes a real provider **pluggable** — operational secret refs, structured instructions, operational-failure mapping — behind the **unchanged `validateDraft`**; the sync seam is untouched. Real-provider-**ready**, not integrated. |
| **Concrete-provider adapter shell (output-out)** | **Implemented (Impl 020)** | Inside `rendering/application`: the **first selected-provider adapter** behind the async `ProviderClientBoundary` — a **disabled-by-default `ConcreteProviderClient`** + pure serializer/parser/error-mapper. Provider target (**OpenAI**) selected **doc-level (020A) only**; code stays vendor-neutral (`concrete-provider-*`). Untrusted draft → unchanged `validateDraft`; operational failures map down without expanding `ProviderFailure`; **no SDK/network/live-call/secret/prompt**. A selected-provider **shell**, not live integration. |
| **Opt-in live-provider boundary** | **Implemented (Impl 021)** | Inside `rendering/application`: a **`LiveProviderClient`** behind the async `ProviderClientBoundary`, an injected **`LiveCallPolicy`** (disabled by default; explicit opt-in), an injected **`ProviderCredentialResolver`** (deterministic `StaticProviderCredentialResolver`; no env), and a single **`LiveProviderHttpTransport`** (native `fetch`, the only network file). Fails closed before transport; reuses serializer/parser/error-mapper; `validateDraft` stays mandatory; audit raw-free. **Live-call-*capable*, not a production rollout.** |
| **Injected environment credential resolver** | **Implemented (Impl 022)** | Inside `rendering/application`: an **`EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver`** (sibling of `StaticProviderCredentialResolver`) reads **one configured key** from an **injected `EnvironmentCredentialSource`** — **no real `process.env`**, no scan, no fallback, no domain-derived name. Classifies missing/invalid/available (opaque transient token); the raw secret stays transient. **Availability ≠ live-call enablement**; calls no transport/provider/`validateDraft`; no guard exception. **An injected *operational* resolver, not a production secret manager.** |
| **Direct `process.env` adapter** | **Implemented (Impl 023)** | A **`ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter`** binds the real process environment into the resolver's injected source shape, reading one neutral key via an injected accessor; **`process.env` is sealed to exactly one approved file** by a new repo-wide guard. Tests use a fake accessor (no real env); it feeds, does not replace, the resolver. **A one-file *operational* source adapter, not a secret manager.** |
| **Live-provider smoke-test boundary (wiring check)** | **Implemented (Impl 026)** | A **pure, fully-injected `liveProviderSmoke(command, deps)`** in `rendering/application` exercises **one** live provider call through the existing `requestRealProviderRendering(...)` seam behind the unchanged validator — gated by explicit fail-closed opt-in → CI → credential → live-policy checks (each stopping before any provider call), returning a **closed, redacted result** (`rawRetained: false`). Reads no `process.env`; imports no transport/adapter/delivery/event/orchestration internal; persists/delivers/records/mutates nothing. **A smoke test proves wiring, not wisdom.** |
| **Operator live-smoke entrypoint (manual)** | **Implemented (Impl 027)** | A manual, executable **`scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs`** (plain ESM, **outside `src`**/`tsconfig.include`/the test glob/both guard scan roots) reads the real opt-in/CI/endpoint flags, resolves the credential **only** via the approved adapter chain, wires the existing live surfaces, and **calls `liveProviderSmoke` once** (preserving `requestRealProviderRendering` + `validateDraft`); prints one **redacted JSON** object; exits 0 for `passed`/`not-enabled`/`ci-disabled`, 1 for failures. Run via `node scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs`. **No npm script, no package/lockfile change, no SDK; not in the default suite/CI; persists/delivers/records/orchestrates/mutates nothing.** A pure typechecked `src` helper holds the env-free logic. |
| npm script / CI-live lane for the operator entrypoint | **Intentional** | The entrypoint is **manual only** — there is **no** npm script wiring it and **no** CI-live lane (a CI environment fails closed). Whether a future CI-live lane is ever allowed is a separate, deliberate spec. |
| **Provider-neutral managed-secret credential-source seam** | **Implemented (Impl 028)** | A pure TypeScript async `ManagedSecretStoreClient` interface + `ManagedSecretCredentialSource` (pre-fetch pattern: `await toEnvironmentCredentialSource()` before constructing the synchronous `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver`) + `FakeManagedSecretStoreClient` (4 scenarios; sentinel value). The downstream synchronous chain is unchanged. No cloud SDK, no `process.env` read, no dependency, no live-call enablement. `secret manager = credential source; ≠ cloud adapter ≠ production rollout.` |
| **Provider-neutral cloud-secret adapter contract behind the managed-secret seam** | **Implemented (Impl 029)** | A **`CloudSecretStoreAdapter implements ManagedSecretStoreClient`** drives an **injected `CloudSecretValueClient`** (cloud-like transport boundary, distinct from `ManagedSecretStoreClient`; MAY throw — the adapter catches), maps a richer cloud-like outcome union (`CloudSecretLookupResult`, classified by the closed redacted `CloudSecretAdapterFailureCode`) into the existing 4-state `ManagedSecretResolution`, **always resolves / fails closed**, and redacts raw secret values **and** raw cloud responses (`FakeCloudSecretValueClient`, sentinel `"opaque:test-cloud-secret"`). **No concrete provider selected (no AWS/GCP/Azure), no SDK/dependency, no real cloud/network call, no `process.env` read, no source precedence, no live-call enablement.** A provider-neutral cloud adapter **contract**, not a provider-specific SDK adapter. |
| Real provider-specific cloud-SDK adapter (AWS / GCP / Azure / Vault) + production secret wiring | **Intentional** | The provider-neutral cloud-secret adapter **contract** now exists (Impl 029 — `CloudSecretStoreAdapter implements ManagedSecretStoreClient`); a **concrete provider-specific SDK adapter** (real AWS/GCP/Azure/Vault client) plus production secret wiring (and source precedence) is a **later slice**. |
| Production secret manager / secret rotation / cache / TTL | **Intentional** | The provider-neutral managed-secret seam (Impl 028) and a provider-neutral cloud adapter contract behind it (Impl 029) now exist; a production cloud adapter (with rotation / cache / TTL) bound to a real secret store and wired into the credential chain is a **later slice**. |
| Production live-call rollout (live call on, real credentials/endpoint) | **Intentional** | The live boundary is *capable* but **disabled by default**; the real `process.env` can feed the resolver (Impl 023), a managed secret store can supply a credential via the seam (Impl 028), and a cloud-secret adapter contract now sits behind that seam (Impl 029); turning it on in production (a real provider-specific cloud-SDK adapter + a real endpoint + a deliberate opt-in) is a **later slice**. |
| Real LLM provider SDK / production secret manager / prompt templates | **Intentional** | The provider boundary is proven with a **deterministic fake provider/client** (Impl 017/019), a **vendor-neutral concrete shell** (Impl 020), an **opt-in live boundary using native `fetch`** (Impl 021), an **injected environment credential resolver** (Impl 022), a **one-file process-environment source adapter** (Impl 023), a **provider-neutral managed-secret seam** (Impl 028), and a **provider-neutral cloud-secret adapter contract behind that seam** (Impl 029 — `CloudSecretStoreAdapter implements ManagedSecretStoreClient`, fail-closed, redacting raw secret values and raw cloud responses); a real *deployed* client supplies a real endpoint/credential through the injected seams (network isolated in the one approved transport + credential supplied via the env adapter or the managed-secret/cloud-secret seam) behind the same validator; **no SDK/installed dependency, no concrete cloud provider selected, no real provider-specific cloud-SDK adapter behind the managed-secret seam, no production secret wiring, no source precedence, no production secret manager, no prompt-templates-as-code, and no `provider`/`llm` module** exist. |
| **Provider-attempt audit (output-out safety)** | **Implemented (Impl 018)** | Inside `rendering`: an append-only **`ProviderAttemptRecord`** (port + in-memory adapter) records *what the seam did* by observing a `ProviderRenderOutcome` — safe summary (status + real-catalog reasons), **no raw draft retention** — auditability not authority; observe-only (calls no provider/validator); creates no record/review/display/delivery/event. |
| **Provider occurrence event surface (ref-only)** | **Implemented (Impl 024)** | `event-recording` now carries ref-only `ProviderAttemptRecorded`/`ProviderDraftValidationFailed`/`ProviderDraftValidationPassed` types + pure factories (produced by `rendering`). A `ProviderAttemptRecord` is **still not** an event record — it can now be **referenced by id** in one; the audit still imports no `event-recording` and **auto-emits nothing**. **Auto-emission / persistence-as-events remain future.** |
| Raw provider draft retention | **Intentional (forbidden)** | Drafts are untrusted; `rawDraftRetained` is the literal `false`; raw draft/text/content/prompt fields are rejected on reconstitution — debugging is reason-based, not text-based (Impl 018). |
| Provider telemetry / model evaluation | **Intentional** | The provider-attempt audit is auditability/safety-debugging only; it grades no model/recommendation quality and infers no athlete state. |
| **Rendered-message record / review persistence** | **Implemented (Impl 015)** | Inside `rendering`: an append-only `RenderedMessageRecord` + `RenderReview` (display-safety) + derived `DisplayEligibility`, behind a repository port + in-memory adapter — auditability, not authority. |
| **Rendered-output / delivery occurrence event surface (ref-only)** | **Implemented (Impl 024)** | `event-recording` now carries ref-only `RenderedMessageRecorded`/`RenderReviewRecorded`/`DisplayEligibilityDerived` (produced by `rendering`) and `DeliveryRequestRecorded`/`DeliveryOutcomeRecorded` (produced by `delivery`) types + pure factories. A `RenderedMessageRecord`/`DeliveryRecord` is **still not** an event record — it can now be **referenced by id** in one; `rendering`/`delivery` still import no `event-recording` and **auto-emit nothing**. **Auto-emission / an event bus / persistence-as-events remain future.** |
| **Delivery / exposure boundary** | **Implemented (Impl 016)** | A downstream `delivery` module exposes a *display-eligible* `RenderedMessageRecord` to a deterministic **test sink** and records an auditable `DeliveryRecord` (port + in-memory adapter). Verifies (never re-derives) eligibility; blocks everything ineligible; success/failure never touch the domain. |
| Real delivery **channel / provider** (email/SMS/push/web) | **Intentional** | The delivery boundary is proven with a **deterministic `InMemoryTestSink`**; a real channel would implement the same `DeliverySink` interface behind the same eligibility gate. |
| Scheduler / retry / background-job layer | **Intentional** | `requestDelivery` is synchronous and deterministic; retries/cancellation lifecycles and any `accepted-for-delivery` two-phase flow are deferred. |
| Rendered-message / delivery **production persistence** | **Intentional** | The record/audit repositories are **in-memory** (port + adapter); no production DB/schema/ORM/migration. |
| UI / API for reviewed/delivered messages | **Intentional** | Display eligibility is **derived, not delivery**; delivery exposes only to a test sink; how an approved message reaches a human surface (UI/API/notification) is future. |
| Notification layer | **Intentional** | A real channel/notification transport is out of scope; only a test/manual/future-channel abstraction exists. |
| **Explicit application orchestration boundary** | **Implemented (Impl 025)** | A new **application-composition module** `application-orchestration` — `orchestrateRenderDeliver(command, deps)` composes the existing rendering/provider-audit/record/review/display/delivery/event services in explicit ordered steps over injected collaborators, returning a closed `OrchestrationOutcome` + a ref-only `OrchestrationTrace`. No domain model/repository/persistence of its own; no event bus/scheduler/retry/workflow; no automatic delivery; no event-triggered step; no domain mutation. AC20 updated additively. |
| **First product-runtime code slice (operator-mediated offline reflection runtime)** | **Implemented (Impl 032R-A)** | A **pure application-level function `offlineReflectionRuntime(command, deps)`** in `application-orchestration` wires the **injected** manual-intake collaborator (`deps.runManualIntake`) + the render-only `orchestrateRenderDeliver` (with `validateDraft` still mandatory) to project a **safe athlete-facing reflection**, **withhold delivery** (`deliveryWithheld: true`), and return a **decision-capture prompt** — creating **no `AthleteDecision`** (operator mediation ≠ athlete decision). Closed status union (`reflection-ready`/`input-rejected`/`not-rendered`/`recording-failed`/`unexpected-failure`); `reflection-ready` is keyed off the **rendered record**, not delivery/display-eligibility. The Impl 025 guard held — manual intake is **injected**, the command is **generic over the submission type**, the production file imports **no `observation` module**, and the **tests** wire the real `ingestManualInput`. **NOT** an executable script/package command/CLI/API/server/UI/worker/deployment target/production rollout/operator smoke; no DB/auth/package/deployment/CI/runtime-shell; no live provider by default; no real secret; no implicit events. |
| Real reasoning pipeline (`ObservationSet → reasoning → understanding → decision-support → RenderableDomainOutput`) feeding the runtime | **Intentional** | Impl 032R-A is the **first product-runtime slice**, but the renderable / `RenderingRequest` is **supplied in the command** — the slice does **not** invent the pipeline (renderable injected ≠ inferred pipeline result; manual intake ≠ full reasoning pipeline). The observation-to-renderable reasoning composition is **future work** (see Spec 034, §9). |
| Production / online runtime surface for the reflection runtime (API/UI/worker, deployment, production rollout) | **Intentional** | The product-runtime slice is **offline / operator-mediated only** (offline runtime ≠ deployment target ≠ production rollout; runtime function ≠ CLI/package command; application service composition ≠ executable runtime shell). A real API/UI/worker, a deployment target, and a production rollout remain **future**. |
| Production orchestration **entrypoint** (UI/API/use-case/scheduler trigger) | **Intentional** | Impl 025 is the explicit composition *function*; Impl 032R-A is the first product-runtime *function* that composes it offline — but how either is *invoked* in production (a UI/API use-case surface, or a scheduler/event-driven trigger) is deferred, and a trigger must never become an event bus/auto-emission/retry layer. |
| **External renderable admission check (Tier 2, wired)** | **Implemented (Impl 035-A + 035-B)** | A pure, synchronous, **structural** `admitExternalRenderable(request: RenderingRequest): ExternalRenderableAdmission` in `application-orchestration/application` (Impl 035-A) — verifies provenance (`sourceCaseRef`), supported kind, claim fields (support needs ≥ 1 `allowedClaim`), `agencyRequired`, `uncertaintyVisibleRequired`, traceability where required, and the support voice ceiling (rejects `Recommendation`/`Silence`/absent); empty `forbiddenClaims` is admissible (documented limitation). **WIRED** into `offlineReflectionRuntime` (Impl 035-B) **after manual intake, before render-only orchestration**, adding the additive closed status `renderable-inadmissible` (optional safe `admissionReason`, `deliveryWithheld: true`, `trace.stoppedAt: "stopped"`, no reflection). A rejected renderable **fails closed before provider rendering** (never calls `validateDraft`/delivery, creates no `AthleteDecision`); an admitted renderable still goes through the mandatory `validateDraft`. The external renderable contract is now **ENFORCED before rendering**, not merely contractual. **admitted ≠ true ≠ evidence-backed fact ≠ recommendation quality ≠ wisdom — Tier 2 cannot prove Tier 1.** AC20 unchanged; no package/dependency/runtime/API/UI/CLI/worker/deployment/CI change. |
| **First operator-mediated reflection session (test-level proof)** | **Implemented as a TEST PROOF (Impl 036-A)** | A **TEST-ONLY whole-core responsible-reflection harness** (one new file under `src/modules/__tests__/`) composes the **real chain end-to-end** — athlete manual input → real `TerminalOutput` → `renderableFromTerminalOutput` → `RenderingRequest` → `offlineReflectionRuntime` → `admitExternalRenderable` (Tier 2) → render-only orchestration → downstream mandatory `validateDraft` → reflection-ready → **delivery withheld** → **no `AthleteDecision`** — across 5 cases (safe → reflection-ready; inadmissible renderable → renderable-inadmissible; admitted-but-invalid draft → not-rendered; invalid manual input → input-rejected; cross-path: never delivers, never creates an `AthleteDecision`). Adds **NO production code, runtime shell, CLI/script/package command, or API/UI/worker/deployment/CI/SDK file**; composing the whole core in `__tests__/` is **AC20-permitted**. The athlete remains the future decision owner; **a test proves the loop, not a deployment.** |
| Production reflection-session service / wrapper / CLI | **Intentional** | The first operator-mediated reflection session exists **only as a TEST-LEVEL proof** (Impl 036-A). A **production session service/wrapper/CLI** (an invocable surface that runs the loop outside `__tests__/`) is a **later slice** — and whole-core composition must stay a TEST HARNESS until a real entrypoint is specified. |
| Production whole-core composer / reflection-composition module | **Intentional** | **Whole-core composition remains a TEST HARNESS (AC20).** No production whole-core composer and no reflection-composition module exist; `offlineReflectionRuntime` keeps its **injected-renderable seam** (renderable supplied in the command — now produced from a real `TerminalOutput` inside the test harness only, Impl 036-A) — still **GUARDED by the Tier 2 admission check** (Impl 035-A/035-B). Spec 034 Option C remains superseded; Tech Spec 034A remains on hold/superseded. |
| `AthleteDecision` feedback loop | **Implemented (Impl 009)** | Athlete-owned, append-only `AthleteDecision` in `athlete`; referenced (not owned) by the case; re-enters as `SubjectiveObservation`. The `AthleteDecisionRef` placeholder is **retired**. |
| Full `DecisionOutcome` object / pattern engine | **Intentional** | Only `DecisionOutcomeRef` exists; outcome modeling and decision-pattern→hypothesis inference are deferred. |
| Compliance / obedience / outcome-based validation | **Intentional (forbidden)** | No score is produced; the outcome never grades `SupportQuality`. |
| Training-plan generator | **Intentional** | Explicitly forbidden at this stage. |
| Real-world ingestion adapter | **Intentional** | Synthetic fixture only. |

[ASSUMPTION] None of the above is a failure. Each was excluded so the core's invariants could be proven *before* the surfaces most likely to erode them are introduced.

---

## 7. Known Placeholders / Adapters

[FACT] Current placeholders and adapters, each with why it exists, what it protects, and its eventual replacement.

| Placeholder / adapter | Why it exists | What it protects | Future replacement |
|---|---|---|---|
| `ReasoningOutcome` adapter (`reasoningOutcomeFrom`, local to `understanding`) | Lets understanding consume reasoning **outcomes** without importing reasoning internals (type-only import) | Keeps claim confidence + raw evidence out of understanding; "understanding earned from tested outcomes" | Stable cross-module outcome contract / event when an event surface lands |
| `PurposeContext` placeholder (input to `decision-support`) | **Partly retired (Impl 007).** A real, versioned purpose now exists in `athlete`; the decision-support input is still a passed-in `PurposeContext` value (no `decision-support`→`athlete` import) | Lets `PurposeGate` run without `decision-support` importing/owning purpose | A production coordinator that snapshots current purpose into `PurposeContext` (the harness adapter is the current seam) |
| `RiskAssessment` placeholder (input to `decision-support`) | No diagnostic/risk engine yet | Lets `RiskGate` run (caution-only) without inventing risk inside the case | Real risk assessment service, still caution-only |
| `AthleteDecisionRef` (field on `DecisionSupportCase`) | **Retired as a placeholder (Impl 009).** It now references a real, athlete-owned `AthleteDecision` in `athlete` | Keeps the decision **referenced, never owned**; `SupportQuality` ≠ outcome | — (the loop is built; production persistence/event surface is the remaining piece) |
| `DecisionOutcomeRef` (reference only, Impl 009) | The outcome is later/separate; a full `DecisionOutcome` object is deferred | Keeps outcome distinct from the decision; outcome never grades support | A specialized `DecisionOutcome`/observation type when outcome modeling is specified |
| Decision harness adapters (`src/modules/__tests__/decision-observation-adapter.ts`) | Converting `AthleteDecision` → `SubjectiveObservation` / adapting the ref needs `observation`/`decision-support`; `athlete` must not import them | Keeps `athlete` a pure upstream leaf; re-entry is observation-only (Impl 006 precedent) | A production application service when a real entrypoint is specified |
| Purpose harness adapters (`src/modules/__tests__/purpose-adapters.ts`) | Converting purpose → `PurposeContext` / applying `PurposeChanged` → `markUnderstandingStale` requires importing downstream; `athlete` must not | Keeps `athlete` a pure upstream leaf; coordination lives outside it (Impl 006 precedent) | A production application service when a real entrypoint is specified |
| `ProjectionRefreshPolicy` applied via harness/caller (Impl 008) | Refresh has no scheduler/event surface yet; the policy is a pure decision | Keeps refresh deterministic and selective without infrastructure; `understanding` owns freshness, the caller applies triggers | An event-driven/maintained refresh when the event surface + persistence land |
| `PurposeReinterpretationStatus` / result (type only) | The reinterpretation *engine* is deferred | Gives a stable shape for future reinterpretation without deciding statuses now | A reinterpretation pipeline once reasoning is purpose-version-aware |
| In-memory repositories (Impl 010, module-local `application/`) | Persistence proven without a DB; the in-memory adapter is the test double for each port | Proves round-trip safety + invariant preservation with no technology committed | A real adapter behind the **same port** when a DB/persistence requirement is specified |
| `<Aggregate>State` types + `reconstitute()` (Impl 010) | Validated rebirth path (constructors/`toProps()` are private); persistence shape is an adapter contract | Keeps rehydration validating, never a raw field bag; keeps state out of the primary public domain API | Possibly a versioned `<Aggregate>State` (`schemaVersion`) at the first real serialization |
| Synthetic end-to-end fixture (`__tests__`) | The e2e composition proof must be deterministic | Proves composition + restraint without committing to an input format | **Partly retired (Impl 013):** a real **manual** ingestion boundary now exists; the synthetic fixture remains the deterministic e2e driver until a real entrypoint is specified |
| Manual Input Adapter (Impl 013, `observation/application/manual-input-*`) | First real "data in" must be proven *before* any UI/API/parser is built on top | Keeps ingestion a faithful scribe — records source material, never meaning; persists via the port; imports no downstream module or `event-recording` | A production entrypoint (UI/API) and external (FIT/wearable) adapters that submit to the same `ObservationSet` boundary |
| Deterministic fake renderer (Impl 014, `rendering/domain/fake-renderer.ts`) | The rendering *boundary contract* must be proven *before* any real provider; tests must be deterministic | Proves voice/uncertainty/traceability/agency preservation with no provider/nondeterminism; the **validator** is the provider-independent guarantee a real renderer must also pass | A real LLM provider adapter **behind the same validator**, with production prompts isolated outside the domain |
| In-memory rendered-message record repository (Impl 015, `rendering/application/`) | Auditability/review must be proven *before* delivery/persistence tech is chosen | Proves append-only records + review + derived eligibility with no DB; mutation isolation + validated reconstitution | A real backend behind the **same port**; ref-only rendered-output events now exist (Impl 024); a delivery/UI/API surface remains future |
| Deterministic `InMemoryTestSink` (Impl 016, `delivery/domain/delivery-sink.ts`) | The delivery *boundary contract* must be proven *before* any real channel/provider; tests must be deterministic | Proves eligibility-gated exposure semantics with no external call/nondeterminism; the **eligibility gate** (`displayEligibilityOf`) is the channel-independent guarantee a real sink must also respect | A real channel/provider adapter **behind the same `DeliverySink` interface** and the same eligibility gate |
| In-memory delivery audit repository (Impl 016, `delivery/application/`) | Delivery auditability must be proven *before* a delivery transport/storage is chosen | Proves auditable `DeliveryRecord`s (request + eligibility + outcome) with no DB; mutation isolation + validated reconstitution; success/failure never touch the domain | A real backend behind the **same port**; ref-only delivery events now exist (Impl 024); a real channel surface remains future |
| Deterministic `FakeProviderAdapter` (Impl 017, `rendering/application/fake-provider-adapter.ts`) | The provider *seam contract* must be proven *before* any real provider; tests must be deterministic | Proves the draft→validate handoff (and every rejection/failure) with no provider/network/nondeterminism; the **unchanged `validateDraft`** is the provider-independent guarantee a real adapter must also pass | A real provider adapter **behind the same `ProviderAdapter` port** and the same validator, with secrets/network/prompts isolated outside the domain |
| In-memory provider-attempt audit repository (Impl 018, `rendering/application/`) | Provider-attempt auditability must be proven *before* a real provider (and its telemetry/eval temptations) arrives; the audit must observe, never act | Proves safe-summary records (status + reasons, **no raw draft**) with no DB; mutation isolation + validated reconstitution; the audit calls no provider/validator and triggers nothing | A real backend behind the **same port**, plus (later) ref-only provider events; a real provider integration consumes the same audit contract — never by retaining raw drafts as source material |
| Deterministic `FakeProviderClient` + `ProviderSecretRef` (Impl 019, `rendering/`) | The real-provider *boundary contract* (async client, secrets, instructions, failure mapping) must be proven *before* any real SDK/network/secret; tests must be deterministic | Proves the async draft→validate handoff, the credential fast-path, and every operational-failure mapping with no real provider/network/secret; the **unchanged `validateDraft`** + the operational `ProviderSecretRef` are the provider-independent guarantees a real client must respect | A real client implements the same async `ProviderClientBoundary` (secrets/network/prompts isolated there) behind the same validator — never by leaking a raw secret or bypassing the gate |
| Disabled-by-default `ConcreteProviderClient` + neutral serializer/parser/error-mapper (Impl 020, `rendering/application/`) | The first **selected-provider** adapter's vendor-specific serialization/parsing/error-mapping must be proven *before* any live call/SDK/credential; the provider target is chosen (020A) but live integration is deferred; tests must be deterministic and credential-free | Proves provider-specific request/response/error mapping behind the async `ProviderClientBoundary` with **no live call, no SDK, no network, no secret** — disabled by default (safe failure); keeps the vendor **doc-level only** so guards stay intact; the **unchanged `validateDraft`** remains the authority | A real **live** client replaces the disabled shell's transport behind the same `ProviderClientBoundary` and the same validator (credentials/network isolated there) — never by weakening a guard, leaking a secret, or bypassing the gate |
| `StaticProviderCredentialResolver` + injected `LiveCallPolicy` (Impl 021, `rendering/application/`) | The live-call *gate* (opt-in policy + credential resolution) must be proven *before* any real env/secret mechanism exists; tests must be deterministic and credential-free | Proves fail-closed opt-in + credential states (available/missing/invalid) drive safe behavior with **no `process.env`, no real secret, no network** (the credential is a non-secret sentinel; missing/invalid/disabled fail closed before transport) | A **production secret/env resolver** implements the same `ProviderCredentialResolver` port (env/secret-manager isolated there) and a deliberate opt-in supplies an `enabled` `LiveCallPolicy` — never by reading `process.env` in application logic or persisting a secret |
| `LiveProviderHttpTransport` over native `fetch`, injected endpoint (Impl 021, `rendering/application/`) | The native-HTTP *containment* must be proven *before* a real endpoint/SDK is chosen; the network token must live in exactly one auditable place | Proves a real call can be made behind the boundary with **no SDK/dependency** and the network token sealed in **one approved file** (vendor/SDK/env forbidden everywhere); the transport validates/persists nothing and leaks no secret | A real endpoint (and, if ever justified, an SDK) supplied to the same transport seam — the network token stays confined to this one file behind the same surgical guard exception |
| `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver` over an injected source map (Impl 022, `rendering/application/`) | Credential *resolution* must be proven *before* the real environment is bound; tests must be deterministic | Proves one-configured-key resolution + classification with an **injected** source (no scan, no fallback) so the boundary works with zero environment access; the raw secret stays transient (opaque token only) and never enters failures/audit/state. **Still the classifier** — Impl 023's adapter feeds it, it is not replaced | A production secret manager implements the same `ProviderCredentialResolver`/source seam — never by reading the environment in the resolver itself or persisting a secret |
| `ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter` + `defaultProcessEnvironmentAccessor` (Impl 023, `rendering/application/`) | The real environment must be bound *before* any production secret store, and the `process.env` read must be auditable in **one place**; tests must stay deterministic | Proves the real environment can feed the resolver's injected source through **one approved file** (the only `process.env` read site, enforced by a repo-wide guard) with an **injected accessor** so the default suite reads no real env; the adapter classifies nothing and triggers nothing | A production cloud adapter implementing `ManagedSecretStoreClient` (Impl 028 seam) + `ManagedSecretCredentialSource` supplies the source instead for secrets-manager-backed credentials — behind the same injected-source seam; the one-file confinement and the resolver's classification role are preserved |
| `ManagedSecretCredentialSource` + `FakeManagedSecretStoreClient` (Impl 028, `rendering/application/`) | The async managed-secret seam must exist *before* any cloud adapter is written; the downstream synchronous chain must be provably unchanged; tests must be deterministic and credential-free | Proves the pre-fetch pattern (async store client → sync `EnvironmentCredentialSource` map → unchanged synchronous `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver`) with a **deterministic fake** covering all 4 resolution scenarios; the sentinel value is not a real credential; no cloud SDK, no `process.env` read, no network token, no dependency; the downstream chain and all guards stay intact | A real **cloud adapter** (AWS Secrets Manager / GCP Secret Manager / Azure Key Vault / HashiCorp Vault) implements the `ManagedSecretStoreClient` interface; `ManagedSecretCredentialSource` wires the pre-fetch into the existing credential chain when a real secret store is provisioned — the interface and the pre-fetch pattern are already the seam |
| `CloudSecretStoreAdapter` + `FakeCloudSecretValueClient` (Impl 029, `rendering/application/`) | The **cloud-secret adapter contract** must be proven *before* any provider-specific SDK adapter is written; the richer cloud-like outcome→4-state mapping and fail-closed/redaction behavior must be provable with no real cloud; tests must be deterministic and credential-free | Proves a `ManagedSecretStoreClient` implementation can drive an injected cloud-like transport (`CloudSecretValueClient`, which **MAY throw**), map a richer cloud-like outcome union (`CloudSecretLookupResult`) into the existing 4-state `ManagedSecretResolution`, **always resolve / fail closed**, and **redact raw secret values and raw cloud responses** — with a **deterministic fake** covering every scenario incl. "throws" (sentinel value); no concrete provider, no SDK, no real cloud/network call, no `process.env` read, no source precedence, no live-call enablement; the seam, the downstream chain, and all guards stay intact | A real **provider-specific cloud-SDK adapter** (AWS / GCP / Azure / Vault) implements the same `CloudSecretValueClient` (or `ManagedSecretStoreClient`) seam behind this contract, with production secret wiring + source precedence + rotation/cache/TTL — the contract and the outcome→4-state mapping are already the seam |
| Pure provider/rendering/delivery occurrence event factories (Impl 024, `event-recording/application/`) | The occurrence-event vocabulary must exist *before* any composition that records output-out events, but no production application/orchestration layer (or event bus) exists yet to call it | Keeps recording **explicit composition only** — pure, ref-only, inert factories that return records and persist/emit/trigger nothing — so the surface cannot become an auto-emitting command/retry/delivery path or grow into authority | A production application layer composes these at the right seams (still explicit, still ref-only); an event-driven/bus delivery and event persistence wait for a deliberate later slice — never by auto-emitting from rendering/delivery/provider or by copying state into the event |
| Reprojection harness (Impl 012, `__tests__/reprojection-harness/`) | Reprojection must be proven *before* any production recompute service/scheduler is specified; it crosses repositories/events/modules and no production application layer exists | Keeps reprojection a check-only safety mechanism — recompute-and-report, no mutation — without implying a scheduler/projection-engine/service | A production orchestration/application layer that promotes the harness concepts behind unchanged contracts when a real entrypoint is specified |
| Explicit application orchestration (Impl 025, `application-orchestration/`) | The first **production composition** layer must be proven *before* any UI/API/scheduler entrypoint or event-driven trigger; composition must stay explicit (no bus/auto-emission) and own nothing | Keeps composition **explicit and ref-only** — `orchestrateRenderDeliver` wires the existing services over **injected** collaborators in ordered steps, owning no domain model/repository/persistence; no event/save triggers a step; delivery is never automatic; failures are safe stops/partial; the trace stays raw-free | A production **entrypoint** (UI/API use-case, or a scheduler/event-driven trigger) that *calls* `orchestrateRenderDeliver` behind the same injected-dependency seam — never by auto-emitting events, becoming an event bus/scheduler/retry layer, or making composition a hidden side effect |
| No production orchestration *entrypoint* (the orchestration function is the seam) | Impl 025 supplies the explicit composition function; no external entrypoint boundary is specified yet | Avoids implying a use-case/transport boundary; keeps invariants inside aggregates and composition explicit | A production application entrypoint (UI/API/scheduler) that injects real collaborators into `orchestrateRenderDeliver` when a real entrypoint is specified |
| Live-provider smoke-test helper (Impl 026, `rendering/application/live-provider-smoke.ts`) | The live path's wiring must be **verifiable manually** *before* any operator entrypoint or production rollout — and it must be proven **without** a live call in the default suite/CI | Keeps the wiring check **pure, injected, and redacted** — `liveProviderSmoke` gates opt-in → CI → credential → live policy (each before any call), makes one bounded call through the unchanged `requestRealProviderRendering → validateDraft`, owns no repository, reads no env, imports no transport/adapter/delivery/event/orchestration internal, and persists/delivers/records/mutates nothing | An **operator entrypoint** (outside `src/`, so it does not become a second `process.env` site) that reads the real opt-in/CI flags and wires the real transport/credential adapter into the same helper when a deliberate smoke runbook is specified (Tech Spec 026A §14) |
| Operator live-smoke entrypoint (Impl 027, `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs` + `rendering/application/operator-live-smoke-entrypoint.ts`) | The live wiring must be **runnable on demand** by an operator *before* any production rollout, **without** running in the default suite/CI or breaching the production `process.env` seal | Keeps the entrypoint **manual + redacted**: outside `src`/`tsconfig.include`/the test glob/both guard scan roots; reads real flags outside `src` and the credential only via the approved adapter; calls `liveProviderSmoke` once (no duplicated semantics); the decidable logic lives in a pure, typechecked, env-free `src` helper; persists/delivers/records/orchestrates/mutates nothing | A future **production rollout** (real endpoint policy) + a **production secret manager** behind the same injected seam; possibly a runbook doc and (only if ever justified) typechecking `scripts/` |
| No CI-live lane / npm script for the operator entrypoint (it stays manual) | A CI-live lane would risk a live call in automation; an npm script would risk default-suite/`check` discoverability | Keeps the entrypoint a deliberate manual action; CI fails closed; `npm run check` runs only typecheck + the suite | A separately-specified CI-live lane (if ever) behind its own explicit policy and guards |

[FACT] **`reasoning` already carries `Hypothesis.purposeContextRef`** (a string slot), so a `PurposeVersionRef` flows in with no reasoning refactor — but **reasoning is not yet purpose-version-aware** (it stores the handle opaquely; it does not reinterpret past hypotheses on a purpose change). That deeper integration is a later spec.

---

## 8. Boundary Rules Going Forward

[DECISION] Future work must preserve these (consolidated from the Boundary Map and the domain index):

1. **`observation` remains upstream** — it imports only `shared-kernel`; it never learns about signals-as-meaning, hypotheses, or voice.
2. **`reasoning` may depend on `observation`, not vice versa** — reasoning consumes signals; observation never imports reasoning.
3. **`understanding` consumes reasoning *outcomes*, not raw `Signal`s** — only via the `ReasoningOutcome` adapter; never reads claim confidence or raw evidence.
4. **`decision-support` consumes `reasoning` and `understanding`, not vice versa** — the upstream modules must never import `decision-support`.
5. **`athlete` is the upstream context of meaning** — it imports only `shared-kernel` and must never import `observation`/`reasoning`/`understanding`/`decision-support` (the *given* must not depend on the *inferred*). Purpose reaches downstream only through neutral adapters/inputs, never by `athlete` reaching out.
6. **`Athlete` must not own inferred state or capacity** — those remain projections (defeasible, traceable), never authoritative attributes; the slice holds only the *given* (declared, versioned purpose; athlete-recorded decisions).
7. **A purpose change never rewrites the past** — `PurposeHistory` is append-only; prior reasoning is never edited/auto-falsified; understanding is staled *selectively* through a coordinator, never reset globally, and never mutated by `athlete` directly.
7b. **The athlete owns the decision; Aurora references and learns, never grades (Impl 009)** — `AthleteDecision` is athlete-owned and append-only; `decision-support` records only an `AthleteDecisionRef`; the decision re-enters **only as `Observation`** (then the full ladder), never as Evidence/Understanding directly; **no compliance/obedience scoring**, and the outcome never grades `SupportQuality`.
8. **UI / LLM must not become domain authority** — generated text is a rendering of domain values, never their source of truth.
9. **Persistence must not turn projections into facts** — a stored `CurrentState`/`UnderstandingLevel` must keep its staleness/confidence; never a plain attribute.
10. **A projection is a derived view, never a source of truth (Impl 008)** — it carries explicit freshness + source references; non-current freshness can only *lower* downstream assertiveness; refresh *recomputes* (never edits the old view); a trigger stales *selectively*, never globally. Consumers honor freshness through the owning module's output (e.g. the clamped `safeVoiceCeiling`), not by owning refresh.
11. **No production service may bypass aggregates or gates** — application services *coordinate, never reason*; a voice/level/verdict is produced only inside its owning module. (Boundary Map's named "most dangerous shortcut.")
12. **Persistence preserves the model; it never becomes the model (Impl 010)** — repositories `save`/`findById` only; rehydration goes through a **validating `reconstitute()`** (never a raw field bag); they store **state copies, not live references**; they **create no domain meaning**; the **domain's `toState()` drives the store, never the reverse**; and a repository **never owns** what its aggregate only references (e.g. a `DecisionSupportCase` repo never persists an `AthleteDecision` object).
13. **Event records remember what happened; they never command it (Impl 011)** — a `DomainEventRecord` is **append-only, ref-only, and inert**: it is **not** a command/aggregate/projection/source-truth, payloads carry **refs not copied state**, appending **executes nothing**, and **causation/correlation are lineage/grouping, never an execution chain**. The log **complements, never replaces**, the aggregate repositories; **`event-recording` imports only `shared-kernel`**, **no domain module imports it**, the **catalog stays out of `shared-kernel`**, and there is **no event bus / publish-subscribe / handler / async delivery / event sourcing / serialization tech**.
14. **Reprojection recomputes and verifies; it never mutates, executes, or asserts truth (Impl 012)** — a run is **check-only**: it recomputes derived views *only through the owning module's functions*, **recalculates** freshness (re-deriving only the same-or-more-cautious view — never promotes), reads **event records as candidates/context only** (never replayed/executed; never rebuilds an aggregate from the log), and **reports drift** instead of overwriting. It **mutates no repository**, creates **no** `TerminalOutput`/recommendation/`SupportQuality` rewrite/`Purpose` overwrite/`DomainEventRecord`, and stays a **neutral test-support seam** — **no production `reprojection` module, scheduler, event sourcing, projection repository, or service layer**, and **no domain module imports it**.
15. **Ingestion records source material; it never interprets (Impl 013)** — the Manual Input Adapter lives in `observation/application`; its **only output is an `ObservationSet`** (via `recordObservationSet`, persisted through `ObservationSetRepository`); it preserves **verbatim words / explicit missing data / provenance (`source: "manual"`) / quality**, **rejects** the unrepresentable (saving nothing), and **partially accepts** only faithful entries. It **detects no `Signal`**, **infers no state**, **invents no value**, **mutates no `AthleteDecisionRecord`**, **scores no compliance**, and **imports no downstream module or `event-recording`** — `observation` stays `event-recording`-free, and any `ObservationSetRecorded` is harness-composed, ref-only, and inert. **Manual input is source material, never meaning.**
16. **Rendering expresses the decision; it never makes one (Impl 014)** — the `rendering` module is **downstream presentation**: it reads a read-only projection of a completed `TerminalOutput` and owns **phrasing only**. A **deterministic fake renderer** produces drafts; **every draft passes a mandatory validator** (the validator is the guarantee) that lets voice **match or soften, never escalate**, keeps `Inquiry` a question and `Withholding` a refusal, keeps uncertainty/limitations/freshness/traceability **visible**, and rejects invented facts/citations + unsafe domain language (**safe non-render** on failure). Generated text is **never domain authority** (`≠ Evidence/Observation/Understanding/AthleteDecision`); rendering **selects no voice, creates no `TerminalOutput`/recommendation, mutates no aggregate, writes no event**; it imports only `shared-kernel` + read-only `decision-support` types, **no domain module imports it**, and **no real LLM provider/prompt/UI/API/external call** exists. **Generated text is a presentation artifact, never authority.**
17. **Persistence audits the presentation; review judges display, not reasoning (Impl 015)** — `rendering` keeps an **append-only `RenderedMessageRecord`** (auditable; source-domain-output ref preserved) and an **append-only `RenderReview`** (display-safety only), with **derived** current status + **derived `DisplayEligibility`**, behind a **repository port + in-memory adapter**. **Persisting is auditability, not authority**: a record is never domain truth; approval changes no `VoiceMode`/traceability/freshness/`SupportQuality` and creates no `Recommendation`; rejection invalidates nothing; failed attempts are never display-eligible/approvable; revision/supersession preserve the old record; **display eligibility is not delivery**. **`rendering` imports no `event-recording`** and **auto-emits nothing** (a `RenderedMessageRecord`/`RenderReview` may now be *referenced by id* in a ref-only `event-recording` event — Impl 024 — but `rendering` neither imports the module nor emits one), the repo is **in-memory** (no production DB), and there is **no delivery/UI/API/provider**. **Persisting or approving rendered text improves auditability and display safety only.**
18. **Delivery exposes the reviewed message; it never makes it true (Impl 016)** — the `delivery` module is **downstream exposure**: it **verifies** display eligibility by calling `rendering`'s **`displayEligibilityOf(record)`** (never re-deriving it), exposes an eligible record **only** to a deterministic **`InMemoryTestSink`** (only `test-sink` supported), records an auditable **`DeliveryRecord`** behind a port + in-memory adapter, and **blocks** every ineligible (not-reviewed/rejected/superseded/failed-render/missing-ref) or unsupported-target request without calling the sink. **Delivery is auditability, not authority**: a `DeliveryRecord` is never source truth (`≠ Evidence/Observation/Understanding/DecisionSupport/AthleteDecision`); **delivery success is not evidence** and **delivery failure is not domain invalidation**; delivery **mutates no rendered record/aggregate**, **emits no event**, and **triggers no reasoning/reprojection/retry**. `delivery` imports **only `shared-kernel` + read-only `rendering`** (no `event-recording`) and **auto-emits nothing** (a `DeliveryRequest`/`DeliveryRecord` may now be *referenced by id* in a ref-only `event-recording` event — Impl 024 — but `delivery` neither imports the module nor emits one), **`rendering` does not import `delivery`**, **no upstream module imports `delivery`**, and there is **no real provider/channel / UI / API / scheduler / retry / event bus / production DB**. **The test sink is not a real provider/channel; a delivered message is still a presentation artifact, never authority.**
19. **A provider drafts; the validator decides (Impl 017)** — the `rendering` provider seam replaces **only** the draft-text step: a (fake, deterministic) `ProviderAdapter` returns an **untrusted `ProviderDraft`**, and a `RenderedMessage` exists **only** by passing the **unchanged mandatory `validateDraft`** (the validator, not the provider, is the authority). The provider request is a **constrained projection** of `RenderingRequest` (no raw reasoning / chain-of-thought / mutable handle / override-voice / hide-uncertainty / prompt-injection field — unrepresentable); an **unsafe request is refused before the provider call**; **every** provider failure or unsafe draft **degrades to safe non-rendering** (a validation failure → `provider-output-failed-validation` + the underlying `RenderingFailure[]`). The provider **selects/changes no `VoiceMode`**, **creates no `TerminalOutput`/`Recommendation`/`RenderedMessage`/`RenderedMessageRecord`**, and **persists/reviews/marks-display-eligible/delivers/emits-an-event/mutates nothing**. The seam imports **only** its own `rendering` surfaces + read-only `decision-support` *types*; **no module outside `rendering` imports it**; and there is **no real provider SDK/API/network/`process.env`/prompt-templates-as-code and no `provider`/`llm` top-level module**. **A provider draft is an untrusted presentation draft, never authority; only the validator turns it into a message.**
20. **The audit remembers the attempt, never the draft (Impl 018)** — the `rendering` provider-attempt audit **observes** a `ProviderRenderOutcome` and records an append-only **`ProviderAttemptRecord`** (port + in-memory adapter): a **safe summary** (status `validation-passed`/`validation-failed`/`provider-failed`/`unsafe-request-blocked` + reasons reusing the real `ProviderFailure` + `RenderingFailure` catalogs) with **no raw draft retention** (`rawDraftRetained` literal `false`; reconstitution rejects raw draft/text/content/prompt fields, `rawDraftRetained: true`, unknown payload-bag keys, and status/flag mismatches). It is **observe-only** — it **does not call** the provider / `requestProviderRendering` / `validateDraft` — and **auditability, not authority**: a record is **not** a `ProviderDraft`/source-truth/`Evidence`/`Observation`/`Understanding`/`AthleteDecision`/`DecisionSupport`/`TerminalOutput`/`RenderedMessage`/`RenderedMessageRecord`; it **creates no review/display-eligibility/delivery**, **appends no event**, **triggers no retry/scheduler/reprojection/reasoning**, and **mutates nothing**; a **validation failure is not domain invalidation**, provider success is not recommendation validation, and provider failure does not weaken `SupportQuality`. The audit imports **only** its own `rendering` surfaces + read-only `decision-support` *types*; **no module outside `rendering` imports it**; **no `event-recording` import and no auto-emit** (a `ProviderAttemptRecord` may now be *referenced by id* in a ref-only `event-recording` event — Impl 024 — but the audit neither imports the module nor emits one); and it is **not model evaluation or telemetry infrastructure**. **No raw draft retention is not no auditability; the safe summary is the audit.**
21. **A real provider changes the draft source, not the authority model (Impl 019)** — the `rendering` real-provider-*ready* path is **additive and async**; the **synchronous Impl 017 seam is untouched** (Option B). `requestRealProviderRendering` **reuses** the unchanged `providerRenderingRequestFrom` guard (unsafe requests refused **before** any client call), a **credential fast-path** (a non-`present` `ProviderSecretRef` fails safely before the call), the deterministic async `ProviderClientBoundary`/`FakeProviderClient`, and the **same mandatory `validateDraft`**; it returns the **existing `ProviderRenderOutcome`**. **Secret refs, never secrets** (status + opaque ref; no raw secret in records/responses/errors; **no `process.env`**; never audited); **structured instruction, not prompts** (derived; no template/arbitrary-prompt/chain-of-thought); **operational failures map down** to the existing `ProviderFailure` (**catalog not expanded**); every failure **degrades to safe non-rendering** with **no automatic retry**. Provider output is **untrusted draft** (only `validateDraft` makes a message); **provider metadata is operational, not evidence**; **provider success validates no recommendation quality** and **failure invalidates no domain output**; the raw-free audit observes the outcome by **explicit composition** (**no automatic persistence**); and there is **no review/display-eligibility/delivery/event/domain mutation**. It imports **only** its own `rendering` surfaces + read-only `decision-support` *types*; **no module outside `rendering` imports it**; and there is **no real provider SDK/API/network/`process.env`/prompt-template and no `provider`/`llm`/`telemetry`/`evaluation` top-level module**. **Real-provider-*ready*, not real-provider-*integrated*; the gate, the audit, and the domain are unchanged.**
