22. **A provider is selected in docs, neutral in code; a shell prepares the vendor without becoming it (Impl 020)** — the first **concrete-provider adapter** lives inside `rendering/application` behind the Impl 019 async `ProviderClientBoundary`. The provider target (**OpenAI**) is recorded at the **doc/decision level (020A) only**; production/test code stays **vendor-neutral** (`concrete-provider-*`, `providerKind: "concrete"`) so **no negative-capability guard is weakened and no vendor token (`openai`/`anthropic`) appears in a guarded provider file**. `ConcreteProviderClient` is **disabled by default** (no transport → safe `provider-unavailable`, no I/O — **there is no live-call code path**); a non-`present` credential fails safe before any transport; the only non-default behavior is a **deterministic in-process fixture transport for tests** (never a network call). The **serializer** projects **only** safe constraints (no arbitrary-prompt/chain-of-thought/voice-override/secret field — unrepresentable; **no prompt template / `src/prompts`**); the **parser** returns an **untrusted draft + operational metadata only** (empty/malformed → safe operational failures; **no raw payload retained**; **no `RenderedMessage`**; metadata is operational, never evidence); the **error mapper** maps provider-shaped errors to the existing `ProviderOperationalFailure`, which `toProviderFailure` maps **down** to the existing `ProviderFailure` (**not expanded**; unknown → `provider-unavailable`, no leak). A draft becomes a message **only** via the unchanged `validateDraft`; the raw-free audit observes the outcome by **explicit composition** (no automatic persistence). It imports **only** its own `rendering` surfaces + read-only `decision-support` *types*; **no module outside `rendering` imports it**; there is **no installed SDK/package dependency** (`package.json`/lockfile unchanged), **no network/`process.env`/raw secret**, and **no retry/scheduler/record/review/display/delivery/event/domain side effect**. **A selected-provider *shell* prepares the vendor deterministically; it is not a live integration, and it weakens nothing.**
23. **A live call is operational I/O behind the gate; opt-in is explicit and fail-closed (Impl 021)** — the `rendering` live-provider boundary makes a provider call *able to be real* without changing the authority model. A **`LiveProviderClient`** implements the existing async `ProviderClientBoundary` (a **sibling** of `ConcreteProviderClient`, reusing the unchanged `serializeProviderInstruction`/`parseProviderResponse`/`mapProviderError`); it **never calls `validateDraft`** — validation stays owned by the unchanged `requestRealProviderRendering`. It is **disabled by default** (`LiveCallPolicy.disabled()`), **opt-in is explicit** via the injected policy (never inferred from the environment; no global state), and it **fails closed before any transport call** when the policy is disabled or the credential (from the injected `ProviderCredentialResolver`) is missing/invalid. **Native `fetch` is sealed in exactly one approved file** (`live-provider-http-transport.ts`, behind an injected endpoint, `AbortSignal.timeout`, no retry/persist/validate/secret-in-errors); **no SDK/package dependency** (`package.json`/lockfile unchanged), **no `process.env`/env resolver/real secret** (the credential is a non-secret sentinel, used transiently, never persisted/audited/logged/in errors), and **no default/CI live call or credential**. Failures map **down** onto the existing `ProviderOperationalFailure → ProviderFailure` (**not expanded**; unknown → safe `provider-unavailable`); provider output is **untrusted draft** (only `validateDraft` makes a message); **provider metadata is operational, not evidence**; the raw-free audit observes by **explicit composition** (no automatic persistence); and there is **no review/display-eligibility/delivery/event/domain mutation** and **no retry/scheduler/event bus**. The **network-guard exception is surgical** — one file, network-token only; **vendor / SDK / env tokens stay forbidden everywhere** (Impl 019/020 guards untouched). The synchronous seam, `FakeProviderAdapter`, `FakeProviderClient`, and `ConcreteProviderClient` are **untouched**. It imports **only** its own `rendering` surfaces + read-only `decision-support` *types*; **no module outside `rendering` imports it**. **A live call changes the draft source, never the authority model; it is live-call-*capable*, not a production rollout.**
24. **A secret resolver is operational; availability is not enablement, and the secret stays transient (Impl 022)** — the `rendering` `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver` implements the **unchanged** injected `ProviderCredentialResolver` port (a **sibling** of `StaticProviderCredentialResolver`). It reads **exactly one explicitly configured key** from an **injected `EnvironmentCredentialSource`** — **never the real `process.env`**, **no scan**, **no fallback list**, **no domain-derived key name** — and returns the existing resolution states (absent → `missing`; blank/control/too-short → `invalid`; else → `available` with the existing opaque transient `ProviderCredentialToken`; a blank/whitespace key name fails closed). The **raw credential stays transient**: it never enters a failure, the provider-client outcome, the raw-free audit, persisted state, provider metadata, or tests; failures are stable non-secret states. **Credential availability is not live-call enablement** — a `LiveCallPolicy.disabled()` still prevents the transport, and a missing/invalid credential prevents it even when the policy is enabled. The resolver **calls no transport / provider / `validateDraft`**, **creates no record/review/display-eligibility/delivery/event**, **mutates no domain**, **expands no failure catalog**, and **adds no package dependency**. **`process.env` appears nowhere in `src/`** — the resolver file is scanned by the Impl 017 `/provider-/` + Impl 021 `/provider-credential/` guards (both forbid the env token) plus a dedicated negative-capability test, so **no guard was weakened and no exception was needed**. It imports **only** its own `rendering` surfaces (+ `shared-kernel` if needed); **no module outside `rendering` imports it**; the static resolver, the live transport, the concrete shell, and the sync seam are **untouched**. **An injected *operational* resolver supplies a transient credential; it is not a production secret manager, and it reads no real environment.**
25. **The real environment is read in exactly one approved file; the adapter feeds, never classifies (Impl 023)** — the `rendering` `ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter` binds the real process environment to the resolver's injected `EnvironmentCredentialSource` shape. It reads **exactly one explicitly configured neutral key** (`AURORA_PROVIDER_CREDENTIAL`) via an **injected `ProcessEnvironmentAccessor`** called **once** — **no scan, no fallback, no domain-derived key name** — and returns a source with only that key when present, else an **empty source**; it **classifies nothing** (a blank value passes through; a blank/whitespace key name fails closed). **Classification stays in `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver`.** The **direct `process.env` token appears in exactly one production file** (`process-environment-credential-source-adapter.ts`, via `defaultProcessEnvironmentAccessor`), enforced by a **new repo-wide guard** — **no existing guard was weakened**, and the network token stays confined to the Impl 021 transport file. Because the accessor is **required** (no implicit default), the default suite injects a fake and **reads no real environment**; the production factory's real read is **never exercised by tests**. **Credential availability is not live-call enablement** (a disabled `LiveCallPolicy` and a missing/invalid credential each block the transport); the **raw secret stays transient** (never in errors/outcome/audit/state/metadata/tests). The adapter **calls no resolver (unless the caller composes it) / live client / transport / provider / `validateDraft`**, persists/audits/logs nothing, mutates no domain, **expands no failure catalog**, and **adds no dependency**. It imports **only** its own `rendering` surfaces (+ `shared-kernel` if needed); **no module outside `rendering` imports it**; the resolver, the static resolver, the live transport, and the sync seam are **untouched**. **The real environment is bound through one auditable file; the adapter is an operational source, not a secret manager, and it never makes the value domain truth.**
26. **Events record what happened; they never make anything happen (Impl 024)** — the `event-recording` provider/rendering/delivery occurrence surface is an **additive catalog expansion + pure factories**, never an event bus. `ProducingModule` gained `rendering`/`delivery` (provider events are produced by `rendering`; **no `provider` producing module**); `EventArtifactKind` gained `ProviderAttemptRecord`/`RenderedMessageRecord`/`RenderReview`/`DeliveryRequest`/`DeliveryRecord` (`DisplayEligibility` is id-less → a ref **role**, not a kind); `DomainEventType` gained eight occurrence/outcome types — every prior entry intact. The **eight factories** build a `DomainEventRecord` through the existing `DomainEventRecord.record(...)` and **return** it: they **persist nothing**, **call no provider/transport/validator/renderer/delivery sink**, **create no rendered-message record/review/delivery record/provider attempt**, **mutate no domain**, and **emit from nothing automatically** — recording is **explicit application composition only**. Payloads stay **ref-only and raw-free** (`kind`/`id`/`role?`/`ownerModule?`; no raw draft/prompt/payload/secret/env value/chain-of-thought/copied body/metadata bag). `event-recording` stays **dependency-neutral** (imports only `shared-kernel`; referencing an artifact by **string kind is not a cross-module import**); **rendering/delivery/provider import no `event-recording` and auto-emit nothing**; the rendering-internal audit symbols stay forbidden outside `rendering`. An event is **never** a command/retry trigger/delivery command, **never** evidence or recommendation quality, **never** an athlete decision, and **never** a domain mutation; **event read/replay creates no side effect**; **no event bus/queue/scheduler/telemetry/DB exists**. The two earlier "catalog not extended" guards (Impl 015/018) were **reconciled, not weakened** — the post-024 boundary is stronger and more precise. **The output-out edge is now occurrence-traceable while the records stay inert.**
27. **Application orchestration composes explicitly; it never becomes a workflow engine or a hidden side effect (Impl 025)** — `application-orchestration` is an **application-composition module, not a domain capability module**: it owns **no domain model, no repository, no persistence of its own**, and introduces **no bounded context**. Its one surface, `orchestrateRenderDeliver(command, deps)`, composes the **existing** public services of `rendering`/`delivery`/`event-recording` in a **fixed, explicit order** over **injected** collaborators, returning a **closed `OrchestrationOutcome`** + a **ref-only `OrchestrationTrace`** (string ids / closed enums / safe codes — **no raw draft/prompt/payload/provider-response/secret/env value/message body**). **Each step is an explicit call**; **no event or repository write triggers the next step** (the function's control flow does); **delivery is never automatic** (display eligibility is necessary, not sufficient); a **delivery failure does not retry**; an **event-append failure is a non-invalidating `partial-success`** (the completed domain steps stand). The **persistence asymmetry is honored** — audit/record/review **return** records persisted explicitly (a review is appended to the rendered-message record; **no separate review repository**), `requestDelivery` **self-persists**, the event repo uses **`append`**. `validateDraft` (inside `requestRealProviderRendering`) stays the **only** path to a `RenderedMessage`; **provider success is not evidence**, **a validation pass is not recommendation quality**, **delivery success is not athlete understanding or an athlete decision**, and **nothing here mutates the domain** (`Athlete`/`Understanding`/`DecisionSupport`/`Observation`/`Hypothesis` are untouched). It imports **only the public indexes** of rendering/delivery/event-recording (+ `shared-kernel`) and the `ProviderClientBoundary` **abstraction** — **never** live HTTP transport / credential-resolver internals / process-env adapter / concrete-provider internals / an upstream domain module; **`rendering`/`delivery`/`event-recording` import no `application-orchestration`**, and no module depends on it for core behavior. There is **no event bus / queue / scheduler / retry / workflow engine / telemetry / DB / UI / API and no dependency change**, and **AC20's `ALLOWED_MODULES` was extended additively** (approved module, not a weakening; the guard still rejects every other unapproved top-level module). **Composition is explicit; an injected collaborator is not a global service locator; an event-recording step is not an event-triggered step; a repository save is not an implicit next step; display eligibility is not automatic delivery.**
28. **A smoke test proves wiring, not wisdom; it is manual, opt-in, fail-closed, redacted, and side-effect-free (Impl 026)** — the `rendering/application` `liveProviderSmoke(command, deps)` is a **pure, fully-injected operational wiring check**, **not an operator script** (none exists; **no npm script, no `scripts/`**) and **not a default/CI test**. It exercises **one** live provider call through the **existing** `requestRealProviderRendering(...)` seam (so the **unchanged mandatory `validateDraft`** stays the **only** path to a `RenderedMessage`), and **only** behind **explicit, ordered, fail-closed gates — opt-in → CI → credential → live policy — each stopping before any provider call**; the **credential is resolved only after the opt-in and CI gates pass**, and the call runs **only** when the credential is available **and** the policy is enabled. It makes **at most one call (no loops, no re-issue)** and returns a **closed, redacted `LiveProviderSmokeResult`** (`rawRetained: false`): rendered → `passed`, `provider-output-failed-validation` → `validation-failed`, any other `ProviderFailure` → `provider-failed` (closed `providerFailureCode`), unexpected throw → `unexpected-failure`. The result carries **no rendered-message body, no raw draft/prompt/payload/response, no secret/credential token, no `process.env` value, no chain-of-thought, no metadata bag, no delivery target/body**. It **reads no `process.env`** (opt-in/CI injected; credential via the injected resolver), composes the live client through the **injected `ProviderClientBoundary`**, and imports **no** live HTTP transport / process-env adapter / concrete-provider internals / `delivery` / `event-recording` / `application-orchestration` / upstream-domain module; it carries **no** network/vendor/secret/retry token; **no module outside `rendering` imports it**. It **persists nothing, delivers nothing, records no event, derives no display eligibility for delivery, creates no rendered-message record / review / evidence / athlete decision, and mutates no domain**. The **default suite and CI make no live call and need no credential**; the repo-wide **`process.env` one-file guard** and the **live-provider guard** (which catches `live-provider-smoke.ts`) stay green; **AC20 is untouched** (no new module); and **package.json/lockfile are unchanged**. **Smoke success is wiring success, not evidence; smoke failure is not domain failure; provider reachable is not provider output trusted; validation pass is not wisdom; the operator entrypoint that reads real env flags remains future.**
29. **The operator entrypoint may connect the wiring; it never changes what the wiring means (Impl 027)** — the manual `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs` (plain ESM, **OUTSIDE `src`/`tsconfig.include`/the default test glob/both guard scan roots**) is a **manual adapter around `liveProviderSmoke`**, **not** new smoke semantics, **not** an npm script, **not** part of `npm run check`, **not** in the default suite, and **not** a CI-live lane. It reads the **real** opt-in/CI/endpoint flags **outside `src`** (legitimate there — no in-`src` token is added, and the production **`process.env` one-file seal stays intact**: the credential is read **only** through the approved `ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter → EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver` chain) and **never dumps the environment**. It wires the existing public surfaces (`LiveCallPolicy.enabled` + `LiveProviderClient` + `liveProviderHttpTransport` + the unchanged serializer/parser/error-mapper) and **calls `liveProviderSmoke` once** — **duplicating no smoke semantics** and **bypassing neither `liveProviderSmoke` nor `requestRealProviderRendering` nor the mandatory `validateDraft`**; the helper still owns the opt-in → CI → credential → live-policy gates, the one bounded call, and the redaction. It prints **one redacted JSON object** (`rawRetained: false`; `wiringOnly`; `sideEffects: "none"`; no rendered body / raw draft / payload / response / secret / env value / metadata bag) and **exits 0** for `passed`/`not-enabled`/`ci-disabled`, **1** for operational failures. The **decidable/redaction logic lives in a pure, typechecked `src` helper** (`operator-live-smoke-entrypoint.ts`) that **reads no `process.env`** (injected record) and imports nothing side-effecting. It **persists nothing, delivers nothing, records no event, calls no `application-orchestration` delivery path, creates no evidence / athlete decision, and mutates no domain**. **No `package.json`/lockfile change, no npm script, no SDK, no dependency.** The Impl 026 `scripts/` guard was **reconciled (strengthened, not weakened)** to permit **only** the approved `operator-live-smoke.mjs`. **An operator can now run the wire; the wire still proves wiring, not wisdom — operator success is not product readiness, the `scripts/` directory is not an arbitrary operational surface, an approved script is not a package script, and an outside-`src` env-flag read does not weaken the production env guard.**

---

## 9. Next Responsible Missions

[ASSUMPTION] Ranked. Each names why it matters, what it must **not** do, and what it depends on.

0. **✅ Spec 007 — Athlete Purpose Change and Reasoning Reinterpretation — DONE (Impl 007).**
   - *Delivered:* a thin, Purpose-first `athlete` module (declared, versioned, append-only purpose; `PurposeChanged`; `PurposeVersionRef`); purpose flows to `decision-support`/`understanding` via neutral adapters; selective staleness; no reasoning rewrite.
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* reasoning becoming **purpose-version-aware** and the **reinterpretation engine** (status type ships, engine does not); the **full** `athlete` aggregate (state/capacity/constraints/path-memory).

0b. **✅ Spec 008 — Projection Refresh and Staleness Strategy — DONE (Impl 008).**
   - *Delivered:* explicit `ProjectionFreshness` (5 states) + `derivedAt` + source refs on `UnderstandingAssessment`; a pure, selective, conservative `ProjectionRefreshPolicy`; non-current freshness only lowers the ceiling (invalid/unknown → `none` → Withholding); `decision-support` unchanged.
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* a generic projection kernel/engine; `ImpactAssessment` as a second projection; event-driven/persisted refresh; `Inquiry`-on-unknown (currently Withholding).

0c. **✅ Spec 009 — AthleteDecision Feedback Loop — DONE (Impl 009).**
   - *Delivered:* athlete-owned, append-only `AthleteDecision` in `athlete` (choice/rationale/context/source; amend-supersede); `DecisionSupportCase` references only an `AthleteDecisionRef`; re-entry as `SubjectiveObservation` via a neutral adapter; no compliance/obedience scoring; outcome never grades `SupportQuality`. The `AthleteDecisionRef` placeholder is retired.
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* a full `DecisionOutcome` object; a decision-pattern→hypothesis engine; a feedback/interaction bounded context if interaction history grows.

0d. **✅ Implementation Architecture — Persistence and Event Surface — DONE (paper).** Defines persistence/event-surface boundaries (ports, append-only ref-only events, projections-as-caches, traceability handles); chooses no technology.

   - *Deferred (carried forward):* the **reprojection harness** (Spec 012); a **projection repository**; an **event bus / production event store / serialization format**; whether **event sourcing** is ever appropriate.

0g. **✅ Spec 012 — Reprojection Harness — DONE (Impl 012).**

Reserved modes throw.
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* a **production recompute service / orchestration layer**, a **scheduler / event-driven refresh**, a **projection repository**, `ImpactAssessment` as a second projection, and any `refresh-derived`/`mark-stale` write path.

0h. **✅ Spec 013 — Manual Input Adapter — DONE (Impl 013).**

Rendering mutates/persists/emits nothing; imports only `shared-kernel` + read-only `decision-support` types.

0k. **✅ Spec 016 — Delivery Boundary — DONE (Impl 016).**

   - *Deferred (carried forward):* a **real provider/channel** behind the `DeliverySink` interface; a **delivery event surface** (ref-only `DeliveryAttempted`/`DeliveryOutcomeRecorded`); a **delivery UI/API**; retry/cancellation lifecycles + the `accepted-for-delivery` two-phase flow; a production persistence backend.

0l. **✅ Spec 017 — Provider Adapter Boundary — DONE (Impl 017).**

   - *Deferred (carried forward):* a **real provider integration** behind the same `ProviderAdapter` port (secrets/network/prompts isolated); **provider-attempt persistence / provider events**; production prompts + safety evaluation beyond deterministic validation.

0m. **✅ Spec 018 — Provider Attempt Audit Boundary — DONE (Impl 018).**

   - *Deferred (carried forward):* a **real provider integration** behind the same `ProviderAdapter` port (secrets/network/prompts isolated); **provider/delivery event records**; provider telemetry / model evaluation; a future raw-retention/redaction policy (only if separately specified).

0n. **✅ Spec 019 — Real Provider Integration Boundary — DONE (Impl 019, real-provider-*ready*).**

The sync Impl 017 seam is untouched; secrets/metadata stay operational; the audit stays raw-free (explicit composition); every failure degrades to safe non-rendering with no automatic retry; no real SDK/network/secret/prompt, no new module, no downstream side effect.
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* the **real provider adapter implementation** (a real client behind the async `ProviderClientBoundary` — secrets/network/prompts isolated there); **provider/delivery event records**; provider telemetry / model evaluation; a future raw-retention/redaction policy.

0o. **✅ Spec 020 — Real Provider Adapter Implementation Boundary — DONE (Impl 020, selected-provider *shell*).**

The provider target (**OpenAI**) is selected at the **doc/decision level (020A) only**; code stays vendor-neutral (`concrete-provider-*`), so **no guard was weakened and no vendor token leaks into a guarded file**. Draft → unchanged `validateDraft`; operational failures map **down** to the existing `ProviderFailure` (not expanded); raw-free audit by explicit composition. **No SDK/package change, no network, no live call, no `process.env`, no raw secret, no prompt template, no retry/scheduler, no record/review/display/delivery/event/domain side effect.**
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* **live provider call enablement** (the actual network/credential opt-in, still behind the validator and raw-free audit); **provider/delivery event records**; provider telemetry / model evaluation; a future raw-retention/redaction policy.

0p. **✅ Spec 021 — Live Provider Call Enablement Boundary — DONE (Impl 021, opt-in, fail-closed).**
   - *Delivered:* an opt-in live-provider boundary inside `rendering/application` — a `LiveProviderClient` (implements the async `ProviderClientBoundary`; sibling of `ConcreteProviderClient`, reusing the unchanged serializer/parser/error-mapper), an injected `LiveCallPolicy` (disabled by default; explicit opt-in; no env inference), an injected `ProviderCredentialResolver` + deterministic `StaticProviderCredentialResolver` (no env, non-secret sentinel), and a single `LiveProviderHttpTransport` (native `fetch` behind an injected endpoint — the only network-token file). Fails closed before transport when disabled/missing/invalid; never calls `validateDraft` (validation stays with `requestRealProviderRendering`); failures map down onto the existing `ProviderOperationalFailure → ProviderFailure` (not expanded); audit raw-free by explicit composition. **No SDK/dependency/lockfile change, no `process.env`, no default/CI live call or credential, no record/review/display/delivery/event/domain side effect, no retry/scheduler.** The network-guard exception is surgical (one approved file); the sync seam, fakes, and concrete shell are untouched.
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* a **production secret/environment resolver** (a real `ProviderCredentialResolver` reading env/secret-manager, isolated) + a deliberate production opt-in; a **real endpoint/SDK** rollout; **provider/delivery event records**; provider telemetry / model evaluation; a future raw-retention/redaction policy.

0q. **✅ Spec 022 — Environment Secret Resolver Boundary — DONE (Impl 022, injected, no real env).**
   - *Delivered:* an `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver` inside `rendering/application` (sibling of `StaticProviderCredentialResolver`) on the unchanged injected `ProviderCredentialResolver` port. Reads one explicitly configured key from an injected `EnvironmentCredentialSource` (`Readonly<Record<string,string|undefined>>`) — no `process.env`, no scan, no fallback, no domain-derived name; classifies missing/invalid/available with the existing opaque transient `ProviderCredentialToken`. Raw secret stays transient (never in failures/outcome/audit/state/metadata/tests); availability is not live-call enablement (a disabled policy and a missing/invalid credential each block the transport); calls no transport/provider/`validateDraft`; no persistence/review/display/delivery/event/domain side effect; no catalog expansion. **`process.env` nowhere in `src/`; no guard exception; no dependency change.**

0r. **✅ Spec 023 — Direct Process-Environment Adapter Boundary — DONE (Impl 023, one approved file).**
   - *Delivered:* a `ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter` inside `rendering/application` that binds the real process environment to the resolver's injected `EnvironmentCredentialSource` shape — reads one neutral configured key (`AURORA_PROVIDER_CREDENTIAL`) via an injected `ProcessEnvironmentAccessor` (called once), returns a source with only that key when present (else empty), classifies nothing (the resolver still does), and fails closed on a blank key name. The direct `process.env` token is sealed to exactly one approved file (`defaultProcessEnvironmentAccessor`) by a **new repo-wide guard**; the accessor is required (no implicit default) so the default suite uses a fake and reads no real env. Availability is not live-call enablement (disabled policy / missing credential each block transport); raw secret stays transient; calls no resolver(unless composed)/live-client/transport/provider/`validateDraft`; no persistence/review/display/delivery/event/domain side effect; no catalog expansion. **No existing guard weakened; no dependency change.**
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* a **production secret manager** (with rotation) behind the same injected-source seam; a production live-call rollout; **provider/delivery event records**; provider telemetry / model evaluation; **live-call smoke tests** (opt-in, out of the default suite).

0s. **✅ Spec 024 — Provider / Rendering / Delivery Event Surface — DONE (Impl 024, ref-only occurrence surface).**
   - *Delivered:* an additive provider/rendering/delivery occurrence event surface in `event-recording` — catalogs extended with `rendering`/`delivery` producing modules, five artifact kinds (`ProviderAttemptRecord`/`RenderedMessageRecord`/`RenderReview`/`DeliveryRequest`/`DeliveryRecord`; `DisplayEligibility` stays a ref *role*, not a kind), and eight occurrence/outcome `DomainEventType`s — plus eight pure factories that build records through the existing `DomainEventRecord.record(...)`. Factories are ref-only, raw-free, and inert: they persist nothing, call no provider/transport/validator/renderer/delivery sink, create no downstream artifact, mutate no domain, and auto-emit from nothing. `event-recording` stays dependency-neutral (imports only `shared-kernel`; rendering/delivery/provider import no `event-recording`). The two earlier "catalog not extended" guards (Impl 015/018) were reconciled, not weakened. **No event bus/queue/scheduler/telemetry/DB; no dependency change; no auto-emission/persistence-as-events.**
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* a **production application/orchestration layer** that composes these factories at the right seams (still explicit, still ref-only); an **event-driven/bus delivery** and **event persistence**; a **credential-resolution event** (still deferred); a **live-provider smoke-test boundary** (opt-in, outside the default suite); a **production secret manager**; a **real channel** behind `DeliverySink`; provider telemetry / model evaluation.

0t. **✅ Spec 025 — Explicit Application Orchestration Boundary — DONE (Impl 025).**
   - *Delivered:* a new **application-composition module** `application-orchestration` — `orchestrateRenderDeliver(command, deps)` composes the existing rendering/provider-audit/record/review/display/delivery/event-recording services in a fixed, explicit order over **injected** collaborators, returning a **closed `OrchestrationOutcome`** (8 kinds) + a **ref-only `OrchestrationTrace`** (10-stage catalog). It owns **no domain model/repository/persistence of its own**; **each step is an explicit call** (no event/save triggers the next); the persistence asymmetry is honored (audit/record/review return → explicit save; review appended to the record; `requestDelivery` self-persists; events `append`); **delivery is never automatic**; failures are safe stops or a non-invalidating `partial-success` (no retry); the trace/result are **raw-free**; it imports only public module surfaces + the `ProviderClientBoundary` abstraction (no live transport/credential-resolver/process-env/concrete-provider internals); rendering/delivery/event-recording import it back. **AC20 updated additively, not weakened.** No event bus/scheduler/retry/workflow engine/telemetry/DB/UI/API, no automatic delivery, no hidden side effect, no domain mutation, no dependency change.
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* a **production orchestration *entrypoint*** (a UI/API use-case surface, or a scheduler/event-driven trigger, that *invokes* `orchestrateRenderDeliver`); a **live-provider smoke-test boundary** (opt-in, outside the default suite); an **event-driven/bus delivery** and **event persistence**; a **production secret manager**; a **real channel** behind `DeliverySink`; provider telemetry / model evaluation.

0u. **✅ Spec 026 — Live Provider Smoke-Test Boundary — DONE (Impl 026, pure injected helper).**
   - *Delivered:* a **pure, fully-injected smoke-test boundary helper** inside `rendering/application` — `liveProviderSmoke(command, deps)` + a closed `LiveProviderSmokeStatus` (9) / `LIVE_PROVIDER_SMOKE_STATUSES` + closed command/dependencies/result types. It exercises **one** live provider call through the existing `requestRealProviderRendering(...)` seam (so the unchanged mandatory `validateDraft` stays the only path to a `RenderedMessage`), behind **explicit ordered fail-closed gates — opt-in → CI → credential → live policy — each stopping before any provider call** (the credential is resolved only after opt-in + CI pass; the call runs only when the credential is available + the policy is enabled); **at most one call, no loops, no re-issue**; a **closed, redacted result** (`rawRetained: false`; no rendered body / raw draft / payload / response / secret / env value). It **reads no `process.env`** (opt-in/CI injected; credential via the injected resolver), composes the live client through the **injected `ProviderClientBoundary`**, imports **no** live transport / process-env adapter / concrete-provider internals / `delivery` / `event-recording` / `application-orchestration`, and **persists/delivers/records/mutates nothing**. **Per Tech Spec 026A Option C**, it is **not an operator script** and adds **no npm script / no `scripts/`**; the default suite + CI make no live call and need no credential; the repo-wide `process.env` one-file guard + the live-provider guard stay green; **AC20 untouched** (no new module). **A smoke test proves wiring, not wisdom.**
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* an **operator entrypoint** (outside `src/`) that reads the real opt-in/CI env flags and wires the real transport/credential adapter (Tech Spec 026A §14), and any deliberately guarded **second env-read site**; an **npm script / CI-live lane**; finer **provider-failure granularity** (timeout/malformed surfaced distinctly); an **`application-orchestration` end-to-end live smoke**; a **production secret manager / live-call rollout / real endpoint**; a **real channel** behind `DeliverySink`; provider telemetry / model evaluation.

0v. **✅ Spec 027 — Operator Live-Smoke Entry Point Boundary — DONE (Impl 027, manual executable entrypoint).**
   - *Delivered:* a **manual, executable `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs`** (plain ESM, **outside `src`/`tsconfig.include`/the default test glob/both guard scan roots**) + a **pure, typechecked `src` support helper** (`operator-live-smoke-entrypoint.ts`: `parseOperatorSmokeEnv` / `syntheticSmokeRenderingRequest` / `operatorSmokeOutput` / `operatorSmokeExitCode` + flag constants; reads no `process.env`). The script reads the real opt-in/CI/endpoint flags **outside `src`**, resolves the credential **only** via the approved `ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter → EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver` chain, wires the existing public live surfaces, and **calls `liveProviderSmoke` once** — preserving `requestRealProviderRendering` + the mandatory `validateDraft`, **duplicating no smoke semantics**; it prints **one redacted JSON object** (`rawRetained: false`, `wiringOnly`, `sideEffects: "none"`) and **exits 0** for `passed`/`not-enabled`/`ci-disabled`, **1** for failures (verified end-to-end). **Run manually** (`node scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs`) — **not an npm script, not in `npm run check`/the default suite, no CI-live lane**; **persists/delivers/records/orchestrates/mutates nothing**. `[FACT]` **Node 22 native type-stripping** lets the `.mjs` import the real `.ts` `src` with **no build/dependency** (027A-verified). The production `process.env` seal stays sealed to the one approved adapter; the Impl 026 `scripts/` guard was **reconciled (strengthened, not weakened)** to allow only the approved entrypoint. **No package/lockfile change, no SDK, no dependency.**
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* a **production secret manager** (with rotation) behind the same injected resolver/source seam; a **production live-call rollout / real endpoint**; a **CI-live lane** (separate spec); an **operator runbook doc** + (only if ever justified) **typechecking `scripts/`**; finer **provider-failure granularity**; an **`application-orchestration` end-to-end live smoke**; a **real channel** behind `DeliverySink`; provider telemetry / model evaluation.

0w. **✅ Spec 028 — Production Secret Manager Boundary — DONE (Impl 028, provider-neutral seam).**
   - *Delivered:* a **provider-neutral managed-secret credential-source seam** inside `rendering/application` — **`ManagedSecretStoreClient`** (pure TypeScript async interface; `retrieve(secretName): Promise<ManagedSecretResolution>`; always resolves; injected in all usage), **`ManagedSecretCredentialSource`** (`async toEnvironmentCredentialSource(): Promise<EnvironmentCredentialSource>`; pre-fetch pattern; `available` → `{ [secretName]: value }` map; non-`available` → `{}` → resolver classifies as `missing` → no provider call), 4-state **`ManagedSecretResolution`**, and **`FakeManagedSecretStoreClient`** (4 scenarios; sentinel `"opaque:test-managed-secret"`; no real secret). The downstream synchronous `EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver` is entirely unchanged. No cloud SDK, no `process.env` read, no dependency change, no new module, no live-call enablement. +39 tests; 672/672 pass; process-env seal intact; operator script unchanged; package.json/lockfile unchanged; AC20 untouched. `secret manager = credential source; ≠ live-call enablement ≠ cloud adapter ≠ production rollout.`
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* a **real cloud adapter** (AWS / GCP / Azure / Vault) implementing `ManagedSecretStoreClient`; **secret rotation** strategy; a **production live-call rollout** (a real cloud adapter + a real endpoint + a deliberate opt-in); **provider/delivery event records**; provider telemetry / model evaluation.

0x. **✅ Spec 029 — Cloud Adapter Behind the Managed-Secret Seam — DONE (Impl 029, provider-neutral cloud-secret adapter *contract*).**
   - *Delivered:* a **cloud-secret adapter contract** inside `rendering/application`, **behind the Impl 028 managed-secret seam** — a **`CloudSecretStoreAdapter`** that **`implements ManagedSecretStoreClient`** (its `retrieve(secretName): Promise<ManagedSecretResolution>` **always resolves, never rejects** — it catches every exception internally) driving an **injected `CloudSecretValueClient`** (a cloud-like transport boundary **distinct from `ManagedSecretStoreClient`** that **MAY throw**), a richer cloud-like outcome union **`CloudSecretLookupResult`** classified by the closed redacted **`CloudSecretAdapterFailureCode`**, and a **deterministic `FakeCloudSecretValueClient`** covering every scenario incl. "throws" (sentinel `"opaque:test-cloud-secret"`; no real secret/SDK/network). The mapping into the existing 4-state `ManagedSecretResolution` is exactly `found`(valid)→`available` / `blank`-or-control→`invalid` / `malformed`→`invalid` / `not_found`-or-empty-ref→`missing` / `denied`/`unauthenticated`/`unavailable`/`timeout`/`throttled`/thrown→`unavailable`; it **fails closed** and **redacts raw secret values AND raw cloud responses** (markers `sk-test-cloud-secret-do-not-leak`, `raw-cloud-response-do-not-leak`, `cloud-access-token-do-not-leak`). **No concrete provider selected (no AWS/GCP/Azure), no SDK/package/lockfile change, no real cloud/network call, no `process.env` read, no production `process.env` token, no source precedence, no live-call enablement; `ProcessEnvironmentCredentialSourceAdapter`/`EnvironmentProviderCredentialResolver`/`ManagedSecretCredentialSource` semantics unchanged; operator smoke unchanged (cloud adapter not wired in by default); no delivery/events/orchestration/evidence/athlete-decision/domain mutation; no telemetry/model-evaluation/DB/schema/retry/scheduler/queue/event-bus.** +38 tests; 710/710 pass; process-env seal intact; operator script unchanged; AC20 untouched. `cloud-like adapter contract ≠ selected provider ≠ SDK integration ≠ production rollout ≠ live-call enablement; safe cloud failure code ≠ raw cloud response; secret ref ≠ secret value.`
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* a **real provider-specific cloud-SDK adapter** (AWS Secrets Manager / GCP Secret Manager / Azure Key Vault / HashiCorp Vault) implementing the seam; **production secret wiring**; **source precedence**; **rotation / cache / TTL**; a **CI-live lane** (separate spec); a **production live-call rollout / real endpoint**; **provider/delivery event records**; provider telemetry / model evaluation.

0y. **✅ Spec 032R / 032RA — Operator-Mediated Offline Reflection Runtime — DONE (Impl 032R-A, Aurora's first product-runtime code slice).**
   - *Delivered:* a **pure application-level function `offlineReflectionRuntime(command, deps)`** inside `application-orchestration/application/` — **Aurora's first PRODUCT-RUNTIME code slice**. It wires the **injected** manual-intake collaborator (`deps.runManualIntake`) + the render-only `orchestrateRenderDeliver` (with the mandatory `validateDraft` still on the existing path) to project a **safe athlete-facing reflection**, **withhold delivery** (`deliveryWithheld: true`), and return a **decision-capture prompt/ref** — creating **no `AthleteDecision`** (operator mediation is mediation, not an athlete decision; the athlete stays the sole decision owner). Inference is marked as inference (not fact); provider output is not returned raw; no hidden reasoning is returned; no live provider by default; no real secret required; no events recorded implicitly. **Closed status union:** `reflection-ready`/`input-rejected`/`not-rendered`/`recording-failed`/`unexpected-failure`; `reflection-ready` is keyed off the **rendered record** itself (a successful render with no review may stop at orchestration `display-ineligible` because display eligibility gates DELIVERY, which is withheld). **The TRUE BLOCKER + RESOLUTION:** the Impl 025 negative-capability guard forbids `application-orchestration` production files from importing upstream domain modules (incl. `observation`), so importing `ingestManualInput` directly would have broken the guard — resolved by **injecting** the manual-intake step (`deps.runManualIntake`), making the **command generic over the submission type**, keeping the production file importing **no `observation` module**, and wiring the **real `ingestManualInput` in the tests**; **no guard weakened**. It is **NOT** an executable script/package command/CLI/API/server/UI/worker/deployment target/production rollout/operator smoke; **no DB/auth/package/deployment/CI/runtime-shell, no dependency change.** +27 tests; **737/737 pass**; process-env seal intact; operator script unchanged; AC20 honored. `operator-mediated runtime ≠ operator smoke; runtime function ≠ CLI/package command; application service composition ≠ executable runtime shell; reflection-ready ≠ delivered; delivery withheld ≠ delivery failure; decision-capture prompt ≠ AthleteDecision; renderable injected ≠ inferred pipeline result; reflection ≠ prescription; Aurora advises, the athlete decides; Aurora never presents inference as fact.`
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* the **`ObservationSet → reasoning → understanding → decision-support → RenderableDomainOutput` reasoning composition** that would let the runtime derive the reflection from manual input **end-to-end** (the renderable is currently supplied in the command — the slice does not invent the pipeline) — **see Spec 034 (recommended next)**; a **production / online runtime surface** (API/UI/worker), a **deployment target**, and a **production rollout** for the runtime; a production orchestration *entrypoint* that invokes it.

0z. **✅ Spec 035 / Tech Spec 035A — External Renderable Admission Check (Tier 2) — DONE (Impl 035-A pure check + Impl 035-B wired).**
   - *Delivered:* a **pure, synchronous, structural Tier 2 admission check** — `admitExternalRenderable(request: RenderingRequest): ExternalRenderableAdmission` in `application-orchestration/application` (**Impl 035-A**) — that verifies **structural safety only**: provenance (`sourceCaseRef`), supported kind, claim fields (a support renderable needs **≥ 1 `allowedClaim`**), `agencyRequired`, `uncertaintyVisibleRequired`, traceability where required, and the **support voice ceiling** (rejects `Recommendation`/`Silence`/absent); **empty `forbiddenClaims` is admissible** (documented limitation — Tier 2 cannot prove a claim set exhaustive). **Impl 035-B WIRED** it into `offlineReflectionRuntime` — running **after manual intake, before render-only orchestration** — adding the **additive closed status `renderable-inadmissible`** (optional safe `admissionReason?: ExternalRenderableRejectionReason`, `deliveryWithheld: true`, `trace.stoppedAt: "stopped"`, no reflection). A rejected renderable **fails closed before provider rendering** — orchestration never starts, so it **does not call `validateDraft`/delivery and creates no `AthleteDecision`**, and `deliveryWithheld` stays `true`; an **admitted renderable still goes through the mandatory `validateDraft`**. The **three-tier contract is now enforced**: Tier 1 caller contractual guarantees · Tier 2 `admitExternalRenderable` (wired, structural) · Tier 3 downstream mandatory `validateDraft`. The external renderable contract is now **ENFORCED before rendering**, not merely contractual. **AC20 unchanged** (no new top-level module); **Spec 034 Option C remains superseded; Tech Spec 034A remains on hold/superseded; no production whole-core composer and no reflection-composition module exist; whole-core composition remains a TEST HARNESS; the injected-renderable seam stays, now GUARDED by admission.** +32 tests (Impl 035-A) + 10 tests (Impl 035-B); **779/779 pass**; process-env seal intact; operator script unchanged. **No package/dependency/runtime/API/UI/CLI/worker/deployment/CI change.** `external renderable ≠ truth; caller guarantee ≠ machine proof; admitted ≠ true ≠ evidence-backed fact ≠ recommendation quality ≠ wisdom (Tier 2 cannot prove Tier 1); admission check ≠ validateDraft; validateDraft ≠ recommendation quality; RenderingRequest ≠ provider call; renderable-inadmissible ≠ delivery failure; delivery withheld ≠ delivery failure; validated reflection ≠ AthleteDecision; operator mediation ≠ athlete decision; AC20 seam ≠ whole-core composer.`
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* the **`ObservationSet → reasoning → understanding → decision-support → RenderableDomainOutput` reasoning composition** that would let the runtime **derive** the renderable end-to-end (still supplied in the command, now admission-guarded) — **see Spec 034**; a **production whole-core composer / reflection-composition module** (whole-core composition stays a TEST HARNESS); a **production / online runtime surface** (API/UI/worker), a **deployment target**, and a **production rollout**; a production orchestration *entrypoint* that invokes the admission-gated runtime.

0gg. **✅ Spec 042 — Real Caller / Operator Use Protocol Boundary — DONE (docs-only governance gate).**
   - *Delivered:* a **docs-only governance / decision-gate boundary** (`docs/specs/042-real-caller-operator-use-protocol-boundary.md`) that **converts the recurring "no real caller yet" deferral into an explicit, per-lane evidence gate.** Aurora will **not** build a **CLI/script/package command**, **API/UI/operator tool**, **persistence/event integration**, **provider/deployment lane** (reopen 030/031), **live-provider**, **delivery channel**, **DB/auth/session**, or an **AC20 amendment** until that lane's own **concrete, recurring, demonstrated evidence threshold** (§7) is met; **each lane is unlocked only by its own evidence — one lane's evidence never unlocks another**, and the **existence of the runbook/helper/envelope is insufficient by itself.** Until a threshold is met, operator use stays **manual/offline** behind `invokeOperatorSession` (caller-assembled command/deps, deterministic fakes, delivery withheld, **only** `OperatorSessionEnvelope`, **no** automatic `AthleteDecision`; later decision capture stays separate + athlete-declared/reported). It added **NO production code, tests, runtime/API/UI/CLI/worker/deployment/CI/SDK files, persistence/event integration, provider/live/delivery integration, or DB/auth/session work**; it modified **no** code (`invokeOperatorSession`, `OperatorSessionEnvelope`, `offlineReflectionRuntime`, `toOperatorSessionEnvelope`, package files, operator script all unchanged). Validation remains **852/852**; AC20 preserved. `real caller ≠ hypothetical UI ≠ developer convenience ≠ deployment target ≠ provider choice ≠ persistence need ≠ athlete decision; caller evidence for one lane ≠ evidence for another; invokeOperatorSession seam ≠ product surface; OperatorSessionEnvelope ≠ raw runtime outcome; Aurora advises, the athlete decides.`
   - *Deferred (carried forward):* every surface/integration lane (CLI/script/package · API/UI/operator tool · persistence/event · provider/deployment 030/031 · live-provider · delivery · DB/auth/session · AC20 amendment) — each **gated** on its §7 evidence threshold; **a real caller**; a docs-only **surface-readiness matrix** or **runbook note referencing `invokeOperatorSession`** (only if ever warranted).

1. **Spec 034 — Observation-to-Renderable Reasoning Composition Boundary** *(recommended next)*
   - *Why:* with the first product-runtime slice now in place (Impl 032R-A — `offlineReflectionRuntime` composes the injected manual-intake collaborator + render-only `orchestrateRenderDeliver` behind the mandatory validator, withholding delivery and returning a decision-capture prompt without creating an `AthleteDecision`), the deferred bridge is the **`ObservationSet → reasoning → understanding → decision-support → RenderableDomainOutput` composition** — the boundary that would let the runtime **derive** the reflection from manual input **end-to-end** rather than receiving the renderable in the command. It composes existing modules across the ladder, in order, without collapsing any boundary.
   - *Must not:* let observation become meaning, inference become attribute, or claim-strength become voice along the new composition; invent a renderable that bypasses `decision-support`'s gates or the mandatory `validateDraft`; turn the runtime into an executable shell / CLI / API / worker / deployment target; create an `AthleteDecision` or treat operator mediation as an athlete decision; deliver automatically off display eligibility; weaken the Impl 025 negative-capability guard (the composition must stay injected / generic over upstream types, with the production file importing no upstream domain module it is forbidden to import); or present inference as fact.
   - *Depends on:* the offline reflection runtime (Impl 032R-A, done) + `orchestrateRenderDeliver` (Impl 025, done) + the full reasoning ladder (`observation`/`reasoning`/`understanding`/`decision-support`, done) + the manual input adapter (Impl 013, done) + the rendering/validator boundary (Impl 014, done).

1b. **Spec 030 — Secret Provider Selection Boundary**
   - *Why:* with the provider-neutral cloud-secret adapter **contract** now in place (Impl 029 — `CloudSecretStoreAdapter implements ManagedSecretStoreClient` driving an injected `CloudSecretValueClient`, with the cloud-like outcome→4-state mapping, fail-closed behavior, and redaction all proven against a deterministic fake), the next genuine edge is **provider selection**: distinguishing — and wiring, one at a time — a **real provider selection**, a **real cloud SDK adapter** (a concrete AWS/GCP/Azure/Vault client behind the `CloudSecretValueClient`/`ManagedSecretStoreClient` seam), **production secret wiring**, **source precedence**, **rotation / cache / TTL**, and a **CI-live lane** (only if ever approved). The contract is already the seam; selection chooses and binds a real provider behind it without collapsing any boundary.
   - *Must not:* read `process.env` outside an approved, guarded file; leak a secret value or a raw cloud response into the domain/audit/records/errors/logs/trace; persist a raw secret; turn live calls on by default; let a live client skip the validator; weaken a guard; add a new `process.env` site; conflate `credential available` with `LiveCallPolicy` approval / operator opt-in / CI live lane / provider trust; let source precedence become a hidden fallback that masks `missing`/`invalid`; or let the cloud adapter become domain logic.
   - *Depends on:* the `CloudSecretValueClient` / `CloudSecretStoreAdapter` contract (Impl 029, done) + the `ManagedSecretStoreClient` interface + `ManagedSecretCredentialSource` (Impl 028, done) + the injected `ProviderCredentialResolver`/source seam (Impl 022/023, done) + the live boundary (Impl 021, done) + the smoke helper + operator entrypoint (Impl 026/027, done).

2. **Reasoning Purpose-Version Awareness & Reinterpretation Engine** *(the deferred half of Spec 007)*
   - *Why:* Impl 007 ships `PurposeVersionRef` and the reinterpretation *status type* but not the engine; this makes reasoning version-aware and produces real reinterpretation verdicts on a purpose change. It can reuse the Impl 008 freshness/refresh machinery (a purpose change is a `RefreshTrigger`).
   - *Must not:* rewrite or auto-falsify prior hypotheses — reinterpretation is a new, traceable artifact.
   - *Depends on:* `athlete` (Purpose, done) + `reasoning` (done) + projection freshness (done).

3. **Production Reprojection / Refresh layer** *(the deferred half of Spec 012)*
   - *Why:* Impl 012 proved reprojection as a check-only harness; a production recompute *service* (and, later, a scheduler / event-driven refresh and a projection repository) would promote those concepts behind unchanged contracts once a real entrypoint exists.
   - *Must not:* become event sourcing; introduce a write path that bypasses the understanding transition policy; promote freshness or strengthen voice.
   - *Depends on:* Specs 010–012; a real production orchestration boundary.

[DECISION] **Recommended next mission: Spec 034 — Observation-to-Renderable Reasoning Composition Boundary.** With *data in* (Impl 013), *output out* (Impl 014), an **auditable record/review** (Impl 015), an **eligibility-gated delivery boundary** to a deterministic test sink (Impl 016), a **provider adapter seam** (Impl 017), a **provider-attempt audit** (Impl 018), a **real-provider-*ready* async client boundary** (Impl 019), a **selected-provider adapter shell** (Impl 020), an **opt-in live-provider boundary** (Impl 021), an **injected environment credential resolver** (Impl 022), a **one-file process-environment source adapter** (Impl 023), a **ref-only provider/rendering/delivery occurrence event surface** (Impl 024), an **explicit application orchestration boundary** (Impl 025), an **opt-in live-provider smoke-test boundary** (Impl 026), a **manual operator live-smoke entrypoint** (Impl 027), a **provider-neutral managed-secret credential-source seam** (Impl 028 — `ManagedSecretStoreClient`/`ManagedSecretCredentialSource`, pre-fetch pattern, 4-state resolution, deterministic fake), a **provider-neutral cloud-secret adapter *contract*** behind that seam (Impl 029 — `CloudSecretStoreAdapter implements ManagedSecretStoreClient` driving an injected `CloudSecretValueClient`, the cloud-like outcome→4-state mapping, fail-closed, redacting raw secret values and raw cloud responses, deterministic fake; no concrete provider, no SDK, no process-env read, no dependency, no live-call enablement), and now **Aurora's first product-runtime code slice** (Impl 032R-A — a pure application-level `offlineReflectionRuntime(command, deps)` in `application-orchestration` that wires the injected manual-intake collaborator + render-only `orchestrateRenderDeliver` behind the mandatory validator, projects a safe athlete-facing reflection, withholds delivery, and returns a decision-capture prompt without creating an `AthleteDecision`), and now a **wired Tier 2 external-renderable admission check** (Impl 035-A/035-B — a pure structural `admitExternalRenderable(request)` in `application-orchestration` now enforced in `offlineReflectionRuntime` after manual intake and before render-only orchestration, so the admission-gated reflection path is a coherent milestone: a structurally inadmissible renderable fails closed before provider rendering — adding the closed `renderable-inadmissible` status — while an admitted renderable still passes the mandatory `validateDraft`; admitted ≠ true, Tier 2 cannot prove Tier 1; AC20 unchanged; 779/779 pass) all in place, the **deferred bridge** is the **`ObservationSet → reasoning → understanding → decision-support → RenderableDomainOutput` composition** — the boundary that would let the runtime **derive** the reflection from manual input **end-to-end** rather than receiving the renderable in the command (renderable injected ≠ inferred pipeline result; manual intake ≠ full reasoning pipeline; the slice does not invent the pipeline). It must compose the existing ladder in order without collapsing observation into meaning, inference into attribute, or claim-strength into voice, without bypassing `decision-support`'s gates or the mandatory `validateDraft`, without weakening the Impl 025 negative-capability guard (the composition must stay injected / generic over upstream types), and without turning the runtime into an executable shell / CLI / API / worker / deployment target or creating an `AthleteDecision`. Further out: a **production / online runtime surface** (API/UI/worker), a **deployment target**, and a **production rollout** for the reflection runtime; **provider selection** (Spec 030 — a real provider selection / real cloud SDK adapter behind the `CloudSecretValueClient`/`ManagedSecretStoreClient` seam, production secret wiring, source precedence, rotation/cache/TTL, a CI-live lane only if ever approved); a **production live-call rollout / real endpoint**, a **production orchestration *entrypoint*** (UI/API/scheduler that invokes the composition), and a **real channel** behind the `DeliverySink`. Each is a deliberate boundary to open one at a time — the `process.env` read must stay in an approved, guarded file; no secret may enter the domain/audit/records/errors/logs/trace or be persisted; a live client must never skip the validator; live calls must never be on by default; an operator entrypoint must never run in the default suite or require CI credentials; a guard must never be weakened; an event must never become a command/retry trigger; recording and composition must stay **explicit** (never auto-emitted); delivery must never bypass display eligibility; an injected collaborator must never become a global service locator; and no drafted/delivered artifact may become source truth. **A smoke test proves wiring, not wisdom.** The discipline that produced restraint by construction must hold precisely when a real mouth, a real secret, a real channel, and a real event stream become tempting.

---

## 10. Final Assessment

[ASSUMPTION] **What has Aurora proven?**
That the reasoning core can run **end-to-end with restraint**: raw observations become signals without becoming meaning, signals become evidence only inside falsifiable hypotheses, tested outcomes earn dimension-specific understanding without repetition or confidence leaking in, and a gated decision-support case turns all of it into a *modest, traceable, agency-preserving* `Reflection` — refusing to recommend even when the chain is complete and the gates are clean. The dangerous collapses (data→meaning, inference→attribute, claim-strength→voice) are unrepresentable, defended by negative-capability and boundary tests.

[ASSUMPTION] **What has Aurora not proven yet?**
Anything involving **a real provider/channel/surface, transport, durable storage, and production recomputation**: a **real LLM provider/SDK** + production prompts + a real secret/network mechanism + a **live provider call** (a deterministic rendering boundary, an auditable record/review, a provider adapter seam against a deterministic fake, a provider-attempt audit, a real-provider-*ready* async client boundary, a vendor-neutral selected-provider adapter shell — disabled by default — an opt-in live-provider boundary — fail-closed, native `fetch` in one approved file — an injected environment credential resolver — one configured key from an injected source map — **and** a one-file process-environment source adapter — the real `process.env` bound through one approved file, sealed by a repo-wide guard — exist, but no **production** live call / real SDK / production secret manager / production prompts — it is *ready, shelled, live-call-capable, and credential-resolving (now from the real environment through one approved file)*, not *deployed*), a **real delivery channel/provider** and a **UI / API** (an eligibility-gated delivery boundary to a deterministic *test sink* exists, but no real channel), **external (FIT/wearable) ingestion**, **auto-emission / an event bus / event persistence** (the ref-only provider/rendering/delivery occurrence event *surface* itself now exists — Impl 024 — but nothing auto-emits or persists it), **provider telemetry / model evaluation**, a **scheduler/retry layer**, a **production** persistence backend / event store, a production orchestration **entrypoint** (the explicit composition *function* exists — Impl 025 — but no UI/API/use-case/scheduler surface *invokes* it), the **full** `athlete` model (state/capacity/constraints/path-memory), risk from real data, reasoning that is **purpose-version-aware** with a reinterpretation engine, a **generic projection engine** (`ImpactAssessment`, event-driven/persisted refresh), a **full `DecisionOutcome` / decision-pattern engine**, and a **production reprojection service / scheduler / projection repository**. Purpose **is** a real, versioned upstream source (Impl 007), **projection freshness is explicit** (Impl 008), the **decision feedback loop is built** (Impl 009), **aggregates now round-trip through validated ports + in-memory repositories** (Impl 010), **occurrences are now recorded as an append-only, ref-only event/outcome log** (Impl 011), **derived state can now be recomputed and verified by a neutral check-only harness** (Impl 012), **real manual data now enters as faithful `ObservationSet`s through an observation-owned adapter** (Impl 013), **domain-approved terminal outputs now render to human-facing text through a deterministic, validated boundary** (Impl 014), **rendered messages are now conserved and reviewed as auditable presentation artifacts** (Impl 015), **display-eligible messages are now exposed to a deterministic test sink + audit records through a downstream delivery boundary** (Impl 016), **a provider may now draft rendered text through a fake/test-only seam behind the unchanged mandatory validator** (Impl 017), **provider attempts are now audited as safe-summary records with no raw draft retention** (Impl 018), **a real provider is now pluggable behind an additive async client boundary (fake in-process client, operational secret refs, structured instructions, failure mapping) that still ends at the unchanged validator** (Impl 019), and **the first selected-provider adapter shell now prepares a chosen vendor (OpenAI, doc-level) in vendor-neutral code — a disabled-by-default client + deterministic serializer/parser/error-mapper — behind the same validator with no live call/SDK/secret/prompt** (Impl 020), and **the first opt-in live-provider boundary now lets a real call be made *only when explicitly enabled* (fail-closed `LiveCallPolicy`, injected credential resolver, native `fetch` sealed in one approved file) behind the same validator — with no SDK/dependency, no env read, and no default/CI live call** (Impl 021), and **the first environment credential resolver now resolves a credential from an *injected* source map (one configured key, the existing opaque transient token) — without reading the real `process.env`, requiring a real credential, enabling a live call by itself, or adding a dependency/guard exception** (Impl 022), and **the first process-environment source adapter now binds the real `process.env` through *exactly one approved file* (sealed by a new repo-wide guard) into the resolver's injected source — feeding, not replacing, the resolver — with an injected accessor so tests read no real environment, no live-call enablement, no secret leakage, and no dependency or existing-guard change** (Impl 023), and **the first ref-only provider/rendering/delivery occurrence event surface now records that an output-out artifact happened — additive catalogs + pure factories building `DomainEventRecord`s that reference artifacts by id only, persist nothing, call nothing, mutate nothing, and auto-emit from nothing** (Impl 024), and **the first explicit application orchestration boundary now composes those existing services in order over injected collaborators — `orchestrateRenderDeliver` returning a closed outcome + a ref-only trace, owning no domain model/repository/persistence, with no event/save triggering a step, no automatic delivery, no retry, and no domain mutation** (Impl 025), and **the live-provider path is now verifiable by a pure, injected smoke-test wiring check — `liveProviderSmoke` makes one bounded call through the existing seam behind the unchanged validator, only behind explicit fail-closed opt-in → CI → credential → live-policy gates, returning a closed redacted result, reading no environment, importing no transport/adapter/delivery/event/orchestration internal, and persisting/delivering/recording/mutating nothing — with no operator script, no npm script, and no default/CI live call** (Impl 026), and **the live wiring is now runnable on demand by an operator — `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs` (OUTSIDE `src`, plain ESM, verified to run via Node 22 type-stripping with no build/dependency) reads the real opt-in/CI/endpoint flags outside the `src` seal, resolves the credential only via the approved adapter chain, calls `liveProviderSmoke` once (preserving `requestRealProviderRendering` + `validateDraft`), prints redacted JSON, exits per a safe policy, and stays out of the default suite/CI/npm scripts while persisting/delivering/recording/orchestrating/mutating nothing** (Impl 027) — all with **no technology installed and no existing guard weakened** (the two earlier "catalog not extended" guards were reconciled, not weakened; AC20 was extended additively for the new approved module; the `process.env` one-file guard and the live-provider guard stay green; the Impl 026 `scripts/` guard was reconciled/strengthened, not weakened). The linear path is proven, **three domain loops are exercised** (purpose-change staleness, projection freshness/refresh, decision feedback — all no-rewrite), **persistence is proven safe in-memory**, **the event surface is realized as inert, ref-only records (now spanning provider/rendering/delivery occurrences — Impl 024)**, **reprojection is proven to recompute-and-verify without mutating/executing/asserting truth**, **the first real ingress records source material without interpreting it**, **the first real egress expresses the decision without becoming authority**, **the output-out cycle is now auditable without the record becoming authority**, **the exposure edge delivers only display-eligible messages without delivery becoming evidence, authority, or a real channel**, **the provider seam lets a draft source feed the unchanged validator without the provider becoming authority, bypassing validation, or touching domain/delivery state**, **the provider-attempt audit remembers what the seam did without retaining a raw draft or letting an attempt become source truth, evidence, or reasoning**, **the real-provider-ready boundary makes a real provider pluggable without secrets, network, prompts, responses, retries, or metadata becoming authority, evidence, persistence, or a downstream side effect**, **the selected-provider adapter shell prepares a chosen vendor deterministically without a live call, an SDK, a secret, a prompt template, a vendor token in guarded code, or any downstream side effect**, **the opt-in live-provider boundary makes a real call possible only when explicitly enabled — fail-closed, native `fetch` sealed in one approved file, credentials injected (never env-read, never persisted) — without an SDK, a default/CI live call, or any downstream/domain side effect**, **the environment credential resolver resolves a credential from an injected source without leaking a secret, enabling a live call by itself, or adding a dependency**, and **the process-environment source adapter binds the real `process.env` through one approved, guard-sealed file without reading the environment in tests, leaking a secret, enabling a live call by itself, classifying the credential, or adding a dependency/existing-guard change**; the remaining work (a **production secret manager** behind the same injected resolver/source seam, a production live-call rollout / real endpoint, a **production orchestration *entrypoint*** that *invokes* the now-built explicit composition — Impl 025 — a CI-live lane, plus an eventual event-bus/persistence, a real channel surface, a production transport/storage backend, deep purpose reinterpretation, and learning *over time*) is specified or scoped but not yet built — the **operator live-smoke entrypoint that wires the real flags into the wiring check now exists (Impl 027)**.

[ASSUMPTION] **What is the most dangerous next shortcut?**
**Auto-emitting or bus-delivering the new *occurrence event surface*, growing the new *application orchestration* into a workflow engine / event bus / scheduler / retry layer, wiring the *operator live-smoke entrypoint* into an npm script / `npm run check` / a CI-live lane, opening a *production secret manager*, a *production orchestration entrypoint*, or a *real endpoint* in a way that lets an event become a command/retry/delivery trigger or grow into authority, auto-emits an event from a rendering/delivery/provider operation, lets an event or a repository save *trigger* the next composition step, lets composition become a hidden side effect, lets an injected collaborator become a global service locator, delivers automatically off display eligibility, runs a smoke test in the default suite or requires CI credentials, reads `process.env` outside the one approved adapter file, leaks a secret into the domain/audit/records/errors, turns live calls on by default, weakens a guard to admit a vendor token/SDK, bypasses the validator, or lets the audit start retaining raw drafts — or a real delivery channel / UI-API surface that bypasses the display-eligibility gate (or treats a drafted/rendered/delivered message as truth).** The rendering *boundary* is proven safe with a deterministic fake renderer + a mandatory validator (Impl 014), the delivery *boundary* with a deterministic test sink behind `displayEligibilityOf` (Impl 016), the provider *seam* with a deterministic fake provider behind the **unchanged** `validateDraft` (Impl 017), the provider-attempt *audit* with safe summaries and **no raw draft retention** (Impl 018), the real-provider *boundary* is now **ready** with an async client + operational secret refs behind the same validator (Impl 019), the first selected-provider adapter *shell* is in place but **disabled by default** with the vendor kept doc-level (Impl 020), the opt-in live boundary is now **capable but fail-closed** — native `fetch` sealed in one approved file, credentials injected, no env read, no default/CI live call (Impl 021), the credential resolver reads from an **injected source map** (Impl 022), the real `process.env` is now bound through **exactly one approved, guard-sealed adapter file** (Impl 023), the output-out edge is now **occurrence-traceable** via a ref-only, inert event surface — additive catalogs + pure factories, no auto-emit (Impl 024), and the existing pieces are now **explicitly composed** via `orchestrateRenderDeliver` — injected collaborators, ordered explicit steps, no event/save trigger, no automatic delivery, no domain mutation (Impl 025), and the live path is now **verifiable by a pure, injected wiring check** — `liveProviderSmoke`, one bounded call behind fail-closed opt-in/CI/credential/policy gates, redacted, no env read, no default/CI live call (Impl 026), and the wire is now **runnable on demand** through a manual operator entrypoint — `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs` outside `src`, reading real flags outside the seal, credential via the approved adapter, one call to `liveProviderSmoke`, redacted JSON, out of the suite/CI/npm scripts (Impl 027); the danger shifts to the moment **auto-emission / an event bus / event persistence**, a **scheduler/retry/workflow layer over the composition**, a **real secret manager**, a **production orchestration entrypoint**, a **CI-live lane**, a **real endpoint**, a **real** channel, or a demo-able surface is *actually* attached — letting an event become a command/retry trigger, letting a smoke test run in CI, letting the env read escape its one approved file or leak a secret into a record/error/audit, letting a live client skip the validator or be trusted as source truth; letting the audit retain raw drafts "to debug" (re-creating a path for untrusted content to become source material); letting delivery skip eligibility; deriving voice from convenience instead of the gates; or re-ingesting a drafted/rendered/delivered artifact as source truth would reintroduce the exact collapses the core was built to prevent, and it would not look wrong from the inside. The discipline must hold precisely when a real mouth and a real channel become tempting: **a real client goes behind the same async `ProviderClientBoundary` and the same validator (the boundary is already that seam); secrets stay operational refs outside the domain and out of the audit; prompts stay structured/derived; the audit stays raw-free (safe summaries only); a real channel goes behind the same eligibility gate; a drafted/rendered/delivered message is never source truth; delivery success is never evidence; the provider/surface never selects voice.**
