## Success Criterion

> **"What is closed, what is still deliberately absent, and what must future work not collapse?"**

[ASSUMPTION] Answerable from this page: **closed** — the five-stage reasoning core (§2–3) with seventy-nine structural guarantees (§4), an end-to-end Reflection proof (§5), a **Purpose `athlete`** module (Impl 007), **explicit projection freshness** on `UnderstandingAssessment` (Impl 008), the **AthleteDecision feedback loop** (Impl 009), **validated persistence ports + in-memory repositories** (Impl 010) so every aggregate round-trips without corruption, a **dependency-neutral append-only, ref-only event/outcome record log** (Impl 011) that records *what happened*, a **neutral check-only reprojection harness** (Impl 012) that recomputes-and-verifies derived views without mutating, executing, or asserting truth, a **real `observation`-owned Manual Input Adapter** (Impl 013) that records manual data faithfully as `ObservationSet`s, a **deterministic, validated `rendering` boundary** (Impl 014) that expresses a domain-approved terminal output as human-facing text without becoming authority, an **auditable rendered-message record + display-safety review** (Impl 015) that conserves and reviews presentation artifacts without making them domain truth, a **downstream `delivery` boundary** (Impl 016) that exposes only display-eligible messages to a deterministic test sink and records auditable attempts without delivery becoming evidence or authority, a **provider adapter seam** (Impl 017) that lets a deterministic fake provider draft rendered text behind the unchanged mandatory validator without the provider becoming authority or bypassing validation, a **provider-attempt audit** (Impl 018) that records what the seam did as safe-summary records with no raw draft retention, a **real-provider-*ready* async client boundary** (Impl 019) that makes a real provider pluggable (operational secret refs, structured instructions, failure mapping) behind the unchanged validator without touching a real provider, a **selected-provider adapter shell** (Impl 020) — OpenAI chosen doc-level, code vendor-neutral, a disabled-by-default client + deterministic serializer/parser/error-mapper — that prepares the vendor without a live call, SDK, secret, prompt, guard weakening, or any downstream side effect, and an **opt-in live-provider boundary** (Impl 021) — fail-closed `LiveCallPolicy`, injected credential resolver, native `fetch` sealed in one approved transport file — that can make a *real* call only when explicitly enabled, behind the unchanged validator, with no SDK/dependency, no env read, no default/CI live call, and no downstream side effect, an **injected environment credential resolver** (Impl 022) — one configured key from an injected source map, the existing opaque transient token — that resolves a credential without requiring a real credential, enabling a live call by itself, leaking a secret, or adding a dependency, and a **one-file process-environment source adapter** (Impl 023) — the real `process.env` bound through one approved file, sealed by a repo-wide guard, feeding (not replacing) the resolver — that reads no real environment in tests, enables no live call by itself, leaks no secret, and adds no dependency or existing-guard change, and a **ref-only provider/rendering/delivery occurrence event surface** (Impl 024) — additive catalogs (`rendering`/`delivery` producing modules, five artifact kinds, eight occurrence/outcome types; `DisplayEligibility` a ref *role*, not a kind) + eight pure factories that record output-out occurrences by id only, persisting nothing, calling nothing, mutating nothing, and auto-emitting from nothing (the two earlier "catalog not extended" guards reconciled, not weakened), and an **explicit application orchestration boundary** (Impl 025) — a new application-composition module whose `orchestrateRenderDeliver(command, deps)` composes the existing rendering/audit/record/review/display/delivery/event services in explicit ordered steps over injected collaborators, returning a closed `OrchestrationOutcome` + a ref-only `OrchestrationTrace`, owning no domain model/repository/persistence, with no event/save triggering a step, no automatic delivery, no retry, no domain mutation, and AC20 extended additively (not weakened), and an **opt-in live-provider smoke-test boundary** (Impl 026) — a pure, fully-injected `liveProviderSmoke(command, deps)` in `rendering/application` that makes **one** bounded call through the existing seam behind the unchanged validator, **only** behind explicit fail-closed opt-in → CI → credential → live-policy gates (each stopping before any call), returning a **closed, redacted result** (`rawRetained: false`; 9 closed statuses), reading no environment, importing no transport/adapter/delivery/event/orchestration internal, and persisting/delivering/recording/mutating nothing — **not an operator script, no npm script, no default/CI live call** (the operator entrypoint remains future), and a **manual operator live-smoke entrypoint** (Impl 027) — `scripts/operator-live-smoke.mjs` (plain ESM, **outside `src`**/`tsconfig.include`/the default test glob/both guard scan roots; verified runnable via Node 22 type-stripping, no build/dependency) reads the real opt-in/CI/endpoint flags outside the `src` seal, resolves the credential only via the approved adapter chain, **calls `liveProviderSmoke` once** (preserving `requestRealProviderRendering` + the mandatory `validateDraft`, duplicating no smoke semantics), prints one **redacted JSON** object, and exits 0 for `passed`/`not-enabled`/`ci-disabled` / 1 for failures — **manual only** (no npm script, not in `npm run check`/the default suite, no CI-live lane), persisting/delivering/recording/orchestrating/mutating nothing, with the decidable logic in a pure typechecked env-free `src` helper and the production `process.env` seal intact (the `scripts/` guard reconciled to allow only the approved entrypoint); **deliberately absent** — a **real LLM provider/SDK** + production prompts + a real secret/network mechanism, a **real delivery channel/provider**, a **UI / API**, external (FIT/wearable) ingestion, **auto-emission / an event bus / event persistence for the (now-existing, ref-only) provider/rendering/delivery occurrence event surface**, **provider telemetry / model evaluation**, a **scheduler/retry layer**, a **production** persistence/event-store backend (DB/ORM/schema/migrations/serialization), a production service / reprojection service / projection repository, the **full** `athlete` model (state/capacity/constraints/path-memory), a reinterpretation engine, a **generic projection engine**/`ImpactAssessment`, a **full `DecisionOutcome`/pattern engine**, and **event sourcing**, each a placeholder or intentional gap (§6–7); **must not collapse** — observation into meaning, inference into attribute, claim-strength into voice, the upstream→downstream dependency direction, **purpose's past into its present** (declared ≠ inferred; append-only; no rewrite), **a projection into a source of truth** (freshness explicit; non-current only constrains; refresh recomputes), **the athlete's decision into Aurora's verdict** (referenced not owned; Observation-only re-entry; no obedience/outcome grading), **the persistence shape into the domain** (validated reconstitution; state copies not live refs; the store preserves the model, never becomes it), **an event record into a command, copy, projection, or source truth** (append-only; ref-only; inert; complements repositories, never replaces them), **reprojection into event sourcing, a write path, or a way to make a projection true** (check-only; recompute-and-report; mutates nothing; rebuilds nothing from the log), **manual input into meaning** (faithful `ObservationSet`; verbatim words; explicit missing data; rejects the unrepresentable; detects no signal; infers nothing), **generated text into domain authority** (rendering is downstream presentation; voice never escalates; uncertainty/limitations stay visible; mutates/emits nothing; never re-ingested as truth), **a persisted/approved rendering into domain truth** (records audit, review judges display-safety; approval strengthens nothing; rejection invalidates nothing; display eligibility is not delivery), **delivery into authority, evidence, or reasoning** (downstream exposure; verifies not re-derives eligibility; blocks the ineligible; success ≠ evidence; failure ≠ domain invalidation; test sink ≠ real channel), **a provider draft into authority** (untrusted draft; only `validateDraft` makes a message; provider selects no voice, creates no terminal-output/record, persists/delivers/emits/mutates nothing; failures degrade to safe non-rendering; fake ≠ real integration), **a provider attempt into source truth, evidence, or reasoning** (audit observes not calls; safe summary, no raw draft retained; not `Evidence`/`Observation`/`RenderedMessage`/record; creates no review/display/delivery/event; validation failure ≠ domain invalidation; audit ≠ model evaluation/telemetry), **a real provider into the authority model** (real-provider-*ready* changes the draft source only; sync seam untouched; secret refs ≠ secrets; structured instruction ≠ prompt; operational failure maps down without expanding `ProviderFailure`; metadata ≠ evidence; no automatic retry/persistence/side effect; only `validateDraft` makes a message), **a selected provider into vendor code or a live call** (provider chosen doc-level only; code vendor-neutral so guards stay intact; the concrete client is disabled by default with no live-call path; serializer ≠ prompt; parser output ≠ message and retains no raw payload; error mapper maps down without expanding the catalog; no SDK dependency; a draft becomes a message only via `validateDraft`), **a live call into the authority model or an always-on/secret-leaking call** (live calls disabled by default; opt-in explicit and fail-closed before transport; native `fetch` sealed in one approved file; no SDK/dependency, no `process.env`/env resolver reading the real environment, no real secret in domain/audit/errors; credentials injected and never persisted; failures map down without expanding the catalog; metadata ≠ evidence; the live client never calls `validateDraft` — validation stays with `requestRealProviderRendering`; no default/CI live call; no downstream/domain side effect), **a secret resolver into domain data or live-call enablement** (the env resolver reads one configured key from an injected source, no scan, no fallback; the raw secret stays transient and never enters failures/outcome/audit/state/metadata/tests; availability never enables a live call — a disabled policy and a missing/invalid credential each block the transport; it calls no transport/provider/`validateDraft`, persists/audits/mutates nothing, expands no catalog), and **the real environment into an open door** (the `process.env` read is sealed to exactly one approved adapter file by a repo-wide guard; the adapter feeds the resolver and classifies nothing; tests inject a fake accessor and read no real env; availability is not live-call enablement; the raw secret stays transient; no existing guard weakened and no dependency added), and **an occurrence event into a command** (the provider/rendering/delivery event surface is ref-only and inert — factories build records through the existing `DomainEventRecord.record(...)`, persist nothing, call no provider/transport/validator/renderer/delivery sink, mutate no domain, and auto-emit from nothing; an event is never a command/retry/delivery trigger, evidence, recommendation quality, an athlete decision, or a domain mutation; payloads stay ref-only/raw-free; `event-recording` stays dependency-neutral and the rendering-internal audit symbols stay forbidden outside `rendering`), and **explicit composition into a hidden side effect, an event bus, a scheduler, a retry engine, or a workflow engine** (`application-orchestration` owns no domain model/repository/persistence; it composes the existing services in explicit ordered steps over injected collaborators; no event or repository save triggers the next step; delivery is never automatic — display eligibility is necessary, not sufficient; a delivery failure does not retry; an event-append failure is a non-invalidating `partial-success`; the trace/result stay ref-only/raw-free; it imports only public module surfaces + the `ProviderClientBoundary` abstraction and is imported back by no module; provider success is not evidence, a validation pass is not recommendation quality, delivery success is not an athlete decision; AC20 was extended additively, not weakened), and **a smoke test into wisdom, a default/CI live call, a side effect, or product readiness** (`liveProviderSmoke` proves *wiring*, not wisdom; it is a pure, injected wiring check — not an operator script, no npm script — that gates opt-in → CI → credential → live policy, each stopping before any call; the credential is resolved only after opt-in + CI pass; it makes one bounded call through the unchanged `requestRealProviderRendering → validateDraft`, no loop/no re-issue; it reads no `process.env`, imports no transport/adapter/concrete-provider/delivery/event/orchestration internal, and persists/delivers/records/mutates nothing; the result is closed + redacted; the default suite + CI make no live call and need no credential; smoke success ≠ evidence/recommendation quality/product readiness, smoke failure ≠ domain failure, provider reachable ≠ provider output trusted, and the operator entrypoint remains future) (§4, §8). The core is complete and restrained — purpose real, freshness explicit, the decision loop closed, persistence proven safe in-memory, occurrences recorded as an inert ref-only log, reprojection proven to recompute-and-verify without mutation, real data entering as source material without interpretation, real output expressed without becoming authority, the output-out cycle made auditable without the record becoming authority, the exposure edge delivering only display-eligible messages without becoming evidence or a real channel, the provider seam drafting behind the unchanged validator without becoming authority, the provider-attempt audit remembering the attempt without retaining the draft, a real provider made pluggable without changing the authority model, the output-out edge made occurrence-traceable through an inert, ref-only event surface that records what happened without making anything happen, the existing services now **explicitly composed** through an application orchestration boundary that wires them in order over injected collaborators without becoming an event bus/scheduler/retry/workflow engine, delivering automatically, or mutating the domain, and the live-provider path now **verifiable by a pure, injected wiring check** that makes one bounded call behind fail-closed gates without a live call in the default suite/CI, an env read, or any side effect; what remains is a real provider adapter implementation, a real channel surface, an **operator live-smoke *entrypoint*** that wires the real env flags/transport into the injected wiring check, a **production orchestration *entrypoint*** that invokes the explicit composition (with an eventual event-bus/persistence), a production transport/storage backend, the deeper loops, and learning over time — to be added without eroding any of the above.

---

*This is the first Review / Consolidation paper after the reasoning core was completed in code. It summarizes Implementations 001–006 and is **updated for Implementation 007 (Purpose-first `athlete`), 008 (projection freshness), 009 (AthleteDecision feedback), 010 (persistence ports + in-memory repositories), 011 (domain event/outcome records + traceability envelope), 012 (check-only reprojection harness), 013 (manual input adapter), 014 (deterministic rendering boundary), 015 (rendered-message record/review persistence), 016 (delivery boundary), 017 (provider adapter seam), 018 (provider-attempt audit), 019 (real-provider-ready boundary), 020 (concrete-provider adapter shell), 021 (opt-in live-provider boundary), 022 (injected environment credential resolver), 023 (one-file process-environment source adapter), 024 (ref-only provider/rendering/delivery occurrence event surface), 025 (explicit application orchestration boundary), 026 (opt-in live-provider smoke-test boundary), 027 (manual operator live-smoke entrypoint), 028 (provider-neutral managed-secret credential-source boundary), 029 (cloud-secret adapter contract behind the managed-secret seam), and 032R-A (operator-mediated offline reflection runtime — Aurora's first product-runtime code slice, a pure application-level `offlineReflectionRuntime(command, deps)` in `application-orchestration`)**; it makes no new domain or architectural decisions and modifies no module.*
